He partners with the Black Widow's residual network — specifically with James Buchanan Barnes, who is alive — to track those responsible for a string of Widow-related killings. The pairing is psychologically rich: two men who have killed under coercion or contract, both of whom have been formally absolved and neither of whom has internally absolved themselves, working in close quarters across Eastern Europe.

**Observed dynamics:** the subject defers tactically to Barnes (legitimate — Barnes has more direct experience in the relevant operational geography) but verbally jabs at him constantly, *which is the subject's documented signal of relational comfort.* The wisecrack-density measure correlates positively, across his entire history, with felt safety in the immediate companion. He does not wisecrack at people he distrusts; he wisecracks at people he has decided cannot leave him in a way that would matter.

He returns to New York in spring 2018 fluent in approximately sixty additional words of Russian (operational vocabulary; he is not conversational and never will be), with a recurring shoulder-rotation tic on the left side (rotator-cuff aggravation from a fall through a Prague rooftop), and with a low-grade ongoing correspondence with Barnes consisting almost entirely of text messages of three words or fewer.

## 4.4 The Bed-Stuy Reconsolidation (2018–2019)

The subject returns to the apartment building. The building, against actuarial expectation, has survived his absences. The tenants — the surviving ones — have organized in his absence into a residents' association that he is invited to address. He addresses them in a Hawaiian shirt and cargo shorts on a Tuesday evening in June 2018, drinks a single beer in two hours (this is metered), and agrees to continue covering certain shortfalls in the building's operating budget out of Avengers stipend.

The apartment itself, surveilled across this period, shows the following longitudinal changes from the Fraction-era baseline:

- The couch has been replaced once (2018). The replacement is structurally identical to the original. He bought the same model.
- The coffeemaker is new (2019). It is a higher-end model and he uses it correctly, which is mildly out of character and probably indicates Kate Bishop's intervention.
- A second pair of hearing aids — backup set — is kept in the bathroom medicine cabinet. The acceptance of the *backup* is the meaningful datum. He is no longer treating the aids as embarrassing.
- The dog bowl is washed regularly. The human dishes are not.
- A small framed photograph, placed on the kitchen windowsill in late 2018, of himself and Barney as children at the carnival. This is new. He did not previously keep photographs of his brother on display. The placement is such that he sees it when he makes coffee and not when he eats. The selectivity is consistent with controlled-exposure tolerance work that he is almost certainly not consciously executing.

## 4.5 *Hawkeye: Freefall* (2020): The Ronin Reversion

Early 2020. A series of high-end art thefts in Manhattan are being committed by someone in the Ronin costume. The Avengers — including a notably impatient Tony Stark — confront the subject. The subject lies. The subject is, in fact, the Ronin. He is using the identity to infiltrate the Hood's organization from below.

The diagnostic content of this episode is not the operation itself (competent) but the **choice of cover identity**. The subject, given any number of pseudonymous options, reaches for *Ronin* — the masterless-samurai identity he originally adopted in 2007 after Captain America's death. The identity is now coded in him as: *what I become when Steve is not available to me.* Steve is not, in 2020, dead — but Steve is, in the period of *Freefall*, unavailable in the relationally relevant sense (post-*Secret Empire* recovery, distance, the institutional Avengers fractured). The subject reverts to Ronin in functional response to the perceived withdrawal of his internalized superego figure. He does not know he is doing this. He thinks he chose a tactically convenient cover.

The operation succeeds in part and costs him: a fractured orbital, a temporary estrangement from Kate Bishop (resolved within six issues but real), and the renewed attention of the Hood — who will be a recurring problem through 2022. He returns the Ronin costume to its storage locker in May 2020 and does not retrieve it again through the present reporting period.

## 4.6 The Hawkeyes-Plural Period (2021–2022)

The Disney+ adaptation in late 2021 is, for purposes of this dossier, exogenous — but the in-universe consequence is that the subject and Kate Bishop are, for the first time, publicly understood as a *pair* by the civilian population. The subject's response to being asked for autographs as half of a duo is documented as: discomfort, deflection, and then — over a period of months — a kind of resigned proprietary pride. He begins, in interviews he cannot avoid, to introduce her unprompted. He has never done this for any prior partner. The mentorship has become, in his own internal taxonomy, *kinship*. He would not use the word. He uses, instead, the phrase "my partner," in a register that any clinician would recognize as load-bearing.

During this period Kate establishes her own L.A. operation; the subject visits twice (Thanksgiving 2021, and a two-week stint in spring 2022 during a case involving a re-emerged Madame Masque). He sleeps on her couch. He cooks once. The food is bad. He does not say so when she does not finish it.

## 4.7 The Brother Question, 2022–2023

Barney Barton resurfaces — the canonical count is now in double digits — in late 2022, this time non-antagonistically and in legitimate medical distress (cardiac, age-cohort-appropriate). The subject pays for the surgery without telling Barney he is paying. He visits the hospital twice, both times during shift changes when the nursing staff is distracted (a pattern: he prefers to be unobserved during emotional exposures). He brings a paperback the second visit and reads it in the chair while Barney sleeps. He does not initiate conversation. Barney, upon discharge, disappears again within six weeks. The subject does not look for him. He has, finally, after roughly fifty years of cyclical pursuit, accepted that **Barney leaves because Barney leaves**, and the pursuit was always the subject's wound, not Barney's obligation. This is the single largest piece of internal psychological work the subject has accomplished in the reporting period and he has accomplished it without naming it.

## 4.8 Hearing, 2023–Present

Progressive bilateral sensorineural loss has continued its slow course. Current audiometric estimate (inferred from depicted accommodations): moderate-to-severe across the speech-relevant frequencies, profound at high frequencies. Operational adaptations now fully integrated:

- Aids worn waking hours, removed for combat above a certain intensity threshold (he prefers to fight deaf when the alternative is feedback artifacts at gunshot range).
- ASL fluency now genuinely operational, not the partial competence of the Fraction era. He signs at conversational speed with Kate, with Maya Lopez when their paths cross, and — notably — with the deaf eight-year-old in apartment 4B of his building, whom he has been teaching to draw a bow.
- Lip-reading competence high but situationally degraded by low light and facial hair.
- He has stopped, sometime around 2022, making jokes about his own deafness. The cessation of the deflection is itself meaningful. It indicates the integration of the disability into self-concept rather than its quarantine in humor.

## 4.9 Current Operational Status

**Residence:** Primary — the Bed-Stuy apartment building, top floor, southeast unit. Secondary — a key to Kate Bishop's L.A. office, used twice annually on average. Tertiary — a duffel and a list of motels along a north-south corridor through the Plains states, maintained for the recurring exile pattern which has not been triggered in the present reporting window but for which readiness is preserved.

**Affiliation:** Avengers, active but peripheral. Available for call-up, not on the residential roster. This arrangement is mutually preferred. He does not attend gala fundraisers. He attends funerals.

**Income:** Avengers stipend (modest by Avengers standards, by his own request — he has historically declined raises), supplemented by occasional contract work for the Maria Stark Foundation and an unannotated revenue stream that is almost certainly residual licensing from the brief mid-2010s period when his likeness was on a cereal box.

**Health, current:** Chronic. Functional. The shoulder, the back, the knees, the hearing. He has, for the first time in his documented life, a primary care physician whose appointments he keeps roughly 60% of the time. The 60% figure is, for him, historic.

**Substance use, current:** Two cups of coffee morning, one afternoon. Beer, two to four per week, never more than two in a sitting. No spirits at home. The Harold Barton vigilance holds.

**Sleep, current:** Improved from Fraction-era baseline. Six hours, broken, with a documented 4 a.m. waking pattern that is consistent across years and is almost certainly trauma-related. He has stopped fighting the 4 a.m. waking and now uses the hour for bow maintenance and correspondence.

**Relationships, current:**
- *Kate Bishop:* primary attachment. Bicoastal but constant. Texts daily; calls weekly; the load-bearing relationship of his adult life.
- *Steve Rogers:* superego-figure, intact. Sees him quarterly. The conversations are brief and consist mostly of nods.
- *Bucky Barnes:* low-frequency, high-trust. The three-word text correspondence continues.
- *Natasha Romanoff:* the relationship is what it is; she has died and returned in his lifetime as he has in hers; the residue is grief and competence in equal measure.
- *Bobbi Morse:* civil. They run into each other on cases. They do not eat meals alone together. He has stopped trying to apologize and she has stopped requiring it. This is, in its own way, the resolution.
- *Barney Barton:* whereabouts unknown, status accepted.
- *The apartment building tenants:* twenty-three persons, names known, birthdays approximately remembered, rents intermittently subsidized.
- *The dog:* foundational.

**Penance ledger, current balance:** unpayable, but the payment schedule is stable. He works. He shows up. He fixes the boiler in the basement himself when he could afford a contractor, because doing it himself is the point and the contractor is not.

## 4.10 Trajectory Read

The subject is, at the present reporting moment, in the most stable equilibrium of his documented life — and the qualifier *of his documented life* is doing serious work in that sentence, because his baseline of stability is what would constitute crisis in another subject. The escalation cycle (§5) has not run a full iteration since *Freefall*. This is the longest inter-cycle interval in his canonical record.

Two readings are possible. The optimistic: the Bed-Stuy reconsolidation, the integration of the hearing loss, the acceptance of the Barney pattern, and the Kate Bishop kinship have produced genuine, if late, individuation. The pessimistic: the cycle is simply loaded and waiting for the trigger, and the trigger will be — as it always has been — the loss of one of the small number of persons currently holding the structure in place.

The honest read is that both are true and the variable is which intervening event arrives first. He is fifty-something, structurally intact, dangerous when needed, kinder than he gives himself credit for, and quietly — for the first time — *teaching a child to shoot in a hallway in Brooklyn,* which is the closest thing to a life he has ever had.

He does not know this is what it is. We do.


## Medical History

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## SECTION II — MEDICAL HISTORY (EXHAUSTIVE)

---

### II.0 PREAMBLE: THE BODY AS LEDGER

Subject's somatic record is best read as an accounts book in which entries have been made by other hands — fathers, mentors, enemies, employers, and the subject himself — and which has never been closed, reconciled, or audited. He has never voluntarily presented for a comprehensive workup. Every imaging study, blood panel, and operative note in the file was obtained downstream of an emergency, a Stark Industries on-team mandate, a SHIELD post-mission protocol, or an Avengers Mansion / Tower medbay intake forced by Pym, Banner-when-stable, Foster, or Cho. Files held by Avengers Medical, Stark Bio-Tech, SHIELD Tier-3 personnel medical, and (post-Bed-Stuy era) a Brooklyn walk-in clinic on Atlantic Avenue do not cross-reference. This is partly operational hygiene and partly subject-driven: he prefers no single physician to hold the full ledger, because the full ledger would compel a conversation he will not have.

The headline finding: the body of a 45-to-late-40s human male with the cumulative wear of a career-long professional fighter, two near-fatal childhood injuries, at least eleven documented hospitalizations as an adult, one clinical death, bilateral progressive sensorineural hearing loss, and what an honest internist would call "borderline everything" — borderline liver enzymes, borderline blood pressure under load, borderline-low B12 from the diet, borderline-elevated resting cortisol. He is not sick. He is *worn*, in the way load-bearing equipment is worn.

---

### II.1 PERINATAL AND EARLY CHILDHOOD (Waverly, IA, age 0–6)

No medical records survive in retrievable form; the Waverly clinic that would have held them either purged on standard ten-year cycle or was absorbed into a regional consolidation in the mid-1980s. What can be reconstructed:

- **Birth:** uncomplicated by report, vaginal delivery, normal weight per Barney's secondhand recall in *Hawkeye: Blind Spot*.
- **Early developmental milestones:** normal. Subject was a precocious physical child, fine motor coordination notably advanced (this matters — the talent that becomes archery was present early).
- **Vaccination status:** assumed complete through school-entry boosters; school enrollment records confirm attendance through grade 4, and Iowa state requirements at the time would have been enforced.
- **Otitis media history:** unconfirmed but inferable. Subject's adult susceptibility to inner-ear infection (documented twice in Avengers medbay records as recurrent serous otitis post-injury) is consistent with a childhood history of untreated or under-treated ear infections, which would have been likely in a household of the Bartons' socioeconomic and parental-attentiveness profile. **This is medically nontrivial: childhood ear-infection scarring of the tympanic membrane and ossicular chain would have meant that subject was already auditorily compromised before any of the major adult insults to his hearing.** He arrived at the sonic-arrowhead incident with reserves already drawn down.
- **Nutrition:** chronic mild malnutrition almost certain. Adult dental records (see II.7) show enamel hypoplasia consistent with childhood nutritional gaps.

### II.2 THE PATERNAL INJURIES (age 6–10, undocumented)

Subject has spoken of his father's violence on perhaps four occasions across canon, always glancingly, always to people who would not press. The reconstructable inventory:

- **Healed left ulnar fracture, mid-shaft, with slight angulation** — visible on adult forearm imaging, never operatively reduced, healed by callus. Mechanism inferable.
- **Two healed rib fractures, left 7th and 8th, posterior** — incidental finding on a chest CT obtained post-Loki incident. Old, well-corticated, childhood-vintage.
- **Healed nasal fracture, untreated, with mild septal deviation** — accounts for the slight rightward set of the bridge and for the chronic right-side nasal congestion he treats with over-the-counter decongestants he buys in bulk.
- **Probable mild traumatic brain injuries, undocumented, multiple.** No imaging correlate definitively assignable to this period (later TBIs overlay), but the behavioral and somatic profile is consistent.

**Psychological impact:** the foundational equation — *injury is what intimacy produces* — was established here, in the body, before language could mediate it. Subject does not flinch from incoming strikes the way an untrained civilian does; he flinches from incoming *affection*. This is the inversion the body learned first.

### II.3 THE MOTOR VEHICLE COLLISION (age ~10)

The accident that killed both parents. Subject was a passenger; survived. Records from the receiving hospital (reconstructed via narrative reference, never seen on-panel) indicate:

- Concussion, probable grade 2.
- Lacerations, facial and scalp, sutured (a faint linear scar at the right superior temporal hairline is visible in close-quarters art across the Fraction, Lemire, and Thompson runs — consistent with this).
- No long-bone fractures from this event specifically.
- Brief inpatient stay, discharged to relatives, then to state, then to the Carson home.

**Psychological impact:** subject is mildly but persistently uncomfortable as a passenger in any vehicle he is not driving. Across canon he is shown driving — cars, motorcycles, quinjets — disproportionately often relative to teammates. This is preference, not coincidence.

### II.4 CARNIVAL YEARS (age ~10–17)

The period when his body was made into the instrument it now is, and also when it was most systematically broken.

- **Trick Shot training regimen:** documented in flashback as physically punishing — running, climbing, weighted draws beyond what is now considered safe for an adolescent musculoskeletal system. **Bilateral chronic rotator cuff tendinopathy, present in adulthood, is iatrogenic from this period.** Subject was drawing bows of adult competition poundage before his epiphyseal plates had closed. His right (drawing) shoulder shows, on later imaging, mild glenoid remodeling consistent with adolescent overuse.
- **Swordsman beating (~age 14–15):** the assault that nearly killed him. Reconstructed injuries: multiple facial fractures (zygomatic, possibly orbital floor — the slight asymmetry of his left infraorbital region is consistent), broken jaw (mandibular body, left), ruptured spleen suspected but never imaged, multiple rib fractures, severe concussion with probable loss of consciousness exceeding 30 minutes. **No hospital presentation.** Subject was nursed back, irregularly, in the carnival environment by people without medical training. This is the single most consequential medical event of his pre-adult life: he learned that catastrophic injury could be survived without professional care, and the lesson took.
- **Right-hand callus pattern:** the deep, characteristic three-finger callus formation on the pads of the index, middle, and ring fingers of the right hand was established in this period and has never resolved. It is visible in nearly every close-up of his hand across the canon. It is the most reliable single biometric tell on his person.
- **Nutrition and growth:** likely caught up partially in this period (carnival food is bad but plentiful). Adult height (~6'3" per house references) suggests genetic potential was largely expressed.
- **Recreational substance exposure:** carnival environment, adolescent. Almost certainly tobacco (subject quit before adult debut; no current use); almost certainly alcohol initiation in early-to-mid teens, given Trick Shot's documented drinking and the cultural environment.

### II.5 ADULT FRAMEWORK INJURIES, CATEGORIZED

A systematic inventory of the adult-era medical record, organized by system rather than chronologically (chronological accounting would require its own volume).

#### II.5.a Musculoskeletal

- **Right shoulder:** chronic supraspinatus tendinopathy, partial-thickness articular-side tear (Avengers Medical MRI, post-Kang campaign era). Subject manages with ice, ibuprofen, and a self-prescribed range-of-motion protocol he learned from a Stark Industries physical therapist whose name he does not remember. He has refused surgical consult three documented times.
- **Left shoulder:** dislocated at least twice (West Coast Avengers period, then again during the *Hawkeye: Freefall* sequence). Reduced in the field on at least one occasion by himself, against a wall. Mild residual laxity.
- **Cervical spine:** mild multilevel degenerative changes, C4-C5 and C5-C6, age-inappropriate. Whiplash mechanism, repeated. He sleeps on his right side with one flat pillow specifically because supine increases occipital headache frequency; he does not know that this is why.
- **Thoracolumbar spine:** lumbar paraspinal hypertrophy (functional), L4-L5 disc desiccation on imaging, no frank herniation. Episodic low-back pain that he treats with a foam roller kept under the couch.
- **Pelvis / hips:** intact, mild bilateral hip flexor tightness from years of crouched draw-and-release work in confined spaces (rooftops, vents).
- **Knees:** bilateral patellofemoral chondromalacia. Subject's knees crack audibly on stairs. He has been offered orthotic consultation; declined.
- **Right hand:** the working hand. Chronic carpometacarpal arthritis early-onset at the thumb (string-hand stabilization), trigger-finger episodes in the middle finger that have self-resolved twice. Callus formation as above.
- **Left hand:** the bow hand. Persistent ulnar deviation under load; mild De Quervain's-pattern tenosynovitis that flares with heavy draws.
- **Fracture history, adult, documented or strongly implied:**
  - Right tibia/fibula, mid-shaft, *Hawkeye* (Fraction) #15 — the legs broken by the Clown. Open reduction with internal fixation, plate and screws still in situ. Post-operative pin-track was the closest he ever came to accepting a course of physical therapy; he completed roughly 60% of it.
  - Multiple rib fractures across career, both sides, healed without intervention.
  - Right zygomatic arch (re-fracture of childhood site), mid-Avengers era.
  - Mandibular hairline, *Blind Spot* era.
  - Left clavicle, distal third, healed with mild prominence.
  - Multiple metacarpal fractures (boxer's fractures, mostly the 5th — he does not always remember to keep the thumb out of the fist).
  - At least three nasal re-fractures stacked atop the childhood baseline.
- **Scar inventory:** comprehensive. Arrowhead-shaped surgical scar over the left thoracic wall (the *Avengers Disassembled* injury, anachronistically present even given the resurrection — narrative bodies remember). Linear scars on the right forearm from glass. A puckered burn scar on the lateral right thigh, mid-sized, from an incendiary arrow malfunction in the early West Coast era. Various small puncture scars on the back of the left hand (his own arrows, in retrieval). The temporal hairline scar from age 10. A surgical scar on the right shin from the ORIF.

#### II.5.b Auditory

The single most studied system in his file, and the one he has most consistently mismanaged.

- **Baseline (pre-1983):** probably already mildly impaired at high frequencies from childhood ear infections and from years of carnival noise exposure (steam calliope, generators, gunfire from the sharpshooter acts).
- **Index event, 1983 (*Hawkeye* vol. 1 #4):** in the field, gagged and bound by Crossfire's operatives, subject improvises by activating a sonic arrowhead held in his teeth to break free. He breaks free. He also blows out approximately 80% of his remaining hearing bilaterally. **This is the foundational somatic decision of his adult life: he traded a permanent sense for a tactical exit.** That this is what he reflexively chose, under pressure, is the diagnostic data point. Subsequently fitted with hearing aids (early-1980s technology, beige behind-the-ear units he hated).
- **Reset period:** various canonical handwaves (Franklin Richards-era reset, regenerative interventions) restored hearing to functional baseline through middle canon. He told no one when it began to deteriorate again. This is consistent with the entire profile.
- **Re-establishment, Fraction era:** beating by the Clown in *Hawkeye* #15 includes a sustained close-range concussive event that returns subject to profound bilateral sensorineural loss. Audiology workup (the only one in the file) documents bilateral severe-to-profound SNHL with poor word-recognition scores even with amplification. Fitted with modern behind-the-ear digital aids, purple casings (a choice made by Kate Bishop, not by him; he has not changed them).
- **Communication adaptation:** ASL acquired in adulthood, partially self-taught, partially from Barney (who is fluent — the brothers learned together as children, an inference strongly supported by the *Hawkeye* #19 issue conducted largely in ASL between them). His ASL is competent but accented in the visual register — his signs are slightly too large, slightly too fast, the way a hearing person's signed speech often is.
- **Tinnitus:** present, bilateral, chronic, severity unreported but inferable from the documented sleep disturbance. He has never used the word "tinnitus" aloud in any depicted context.
- **Vestibular function:** preserved, remarkably. His balance — necessary for the rooftop work, the rappelling, the moving-platform shooting — is intact. Audiology notes from the Fraction-era workup specifically commented that vestibular sparing in the face of cochlear devastation is fortunate and unusual.

**Psychological impact (auditory):** the hearing loss is the closest thing subject has to a metaphor he will inhabit consciously. He uses it self-deprecatingly ("I didn't hear you, that's the joke"), as a strategic prop (turning the aids off during interrogations, both his own and others'), and as the one disability about which he has, very slowly, allowed himself to be helped — by Kate, by Barney in the barn, by Lucky who responds to vibration. **It is the only injury he has integrated rather than denied.** Every other piece of damage on this file is treated as if it happened to someone else.

#### II.5.c Neurological

- **TBI burden:** substantial. Conservative estimate of clinically significant concussions across career: 12–18. Subclinical cumulative impacts: uncountable. He has been knocked unconscious on-panel at least nine times. **No current evidence of cognitive decline** by depicted function — tactical processing remains elite, reaction time intact, memory functional. Whether this remains true at age 60 is a separate question; the file at present is reassuring.
- **Mind-control / agency-loss events:** Crossfire's sonics (1983); various low-grade telepathic intrusions across Avengers cosmic events; arguably the *Avengers vs. X-Men* Phoenix-adjacent events. Each leaves what is best described as **iatrogenic neurological PTSD** — somatic startle response to specific frequency ranges, to the sensation of headphones being placed, to anyone touching the back of his neck unexpectedly.
- **Migraine:** episodic, post-concussive pattern, treated with OTC analgesics and a darkened room. He calls them headaches. They are migraines.
- **Sleep architecture:** disrupted. Likely reduced REM, frequent middle-of-night awakening, early-morning terminal insomnia. Standard depressive sleep signature overlaid on a hyperarousal pattern. He does not nap well; he micro-sleeps on couches.

#### II.5.d Cardiovascular

- **Resting pulse:** athletic-range bradycardia, ~52 bpm.
- **Blood pressure:** normal at rest, exaggerated reactivity under stress. He flushes visibly when angry; this is autonomic and untrained-out.
- **Lipid panel:** the file's last documented panel showed mildly elevated triglycerides and borderline HDL, attributable to diet and alcohol. LDL fine.
- **Cardiac structure / function:** echo (one on file, Avengers post-resurrection workup) normal. No murmurs, normal ejection fraction.

#### II.5.e Gastrointestinal / Hepatic

- **Liver function tests:** mildly elevated transaminases, last drawn. Consistent with episodic moderate-to-heavy alcohol use and chronic NSAID consumption. **The NSAID load is, medically, the more concerning of the two**; subject's daily ibuprofen intake under flare conditions has exceeded recommended maxima with regularity. Gastric mucosa likely shows chronic NSAID-associated changes. He treats reflux with OTC famotidine kept in the bathroom medicine cabinet.
- **Diet:** catastrophic. Coffee, pizza, beer, the occasional protein-bar performance of nutrition. Vegetables enter the body chiefly via Kate Bishop's intervention.
- **Bowel function:** unremarkable on report.

#### II.5.f Genitourinary

- **Renal function:** preserved, last check.
- **Reproductive history:** no documented children in 616 main continuity (the Renew Your Vows / alternate-continuity offspring are not on this file). Documented adult sexual partnerships: Romanoff (intermittent, complicated), Morse (marriage), Wanda (brief and undefined, post-resurrection), several non-named partners across Fraction's run depicted with characteristic chaotic-bachelor texture. STI history: not on file. Inferable that subject has received at least baseline screening through Avengers Medical periodic exams.

#### II.5.g Dermatologic

- **Sun damage:** moderate, consistent with extensive outdoor work, particularly during the West Coast Avengers period (Southern California rooftops, deserts, beaches). Subject does not consistently use sunscreen. A small actinic keratosis on the left forearm was noted and frozen off during a Stark Tower checkup; he forgot about it within the day.
- **Calluses:** as catalogued.
- **Tattoos:** none, canonically. This is itself a small data point — a man with his class background, his service-adjacent life, and his propensity for permanent self-marking via injury has nevertheless never chosen a permanent mark he could control. Inferential reading: he does not need any more permanent marks. The body is already covered in involuntary ones.

#### II.5.h Dental

- Childhood enamel hypoplasia as noted.
- Multiple chipped teeth (anterior — punch impacts), at least two crowns.
- One missing premolar, lower left, never restored. He notices the gap with his tongue when stressed.
- Dental hygiene self-reportedly poor; in practice, adequate-to-mediocre. He flosses when Kate notices.

### II.6 TRANSFORMATIONS, RESURRECTIONS, AND NON-STANDARD INTERVENTIONS

- **Death event, *Avengers Disassembled* (2004):** clinical death by self-detonated quiver, immediate, unsurvivable by ordinary biology. The body was, in narrative terms, destroyed.
- **Restoration via Scarlet Witch (*House of M* and subsequent reality-reset, 2005):** mechanism: probability-warp / reality-reconstruction. The body that came back is functionally his — same scars present, same callus pattern, same hearing loss baseline, same right-shoulder tendinopathy. **The continuity of physical wear across the resurrection is itself a data point: whatever brought him back brought back the damage too.** This is consistent with subject's own internal narrative, in which the damage is not separable from the self. He would not have come back clean. He would not have known how to be himself in a clean body.
- **No subject-history of:** super-soldier serum, Extremis, Pym Particle exposure of significance, cosmic ray exposure of significance, gamma exposure of significance, mutate transformation, symbiote bonding (in main 616), techno-organic infection, Asgardian biological intervention. The body remains baseline human. **This is a chosen condition.** Subject has been offered enhancement on at least three documented occasions (Pym's offer of a strength-augment regimen, mid-WCA; a Stark performance-suit prototype during the Initiative period; a Wakandan biokinetic mesh during a *Secret Avengers* crossover) and has declined each. **The refusal to be augmented is structural to his identity** and has medical consequences: he competes in a weight class his species does not, and pays for it in cartilage.

### II.7 SUBSTANCES (current and historical)

- **Caffeine:** dependent. Estimated daily intake 600–900 mg, predominantly coffee, occasionally supplemented with energy drinks pre-mission. Withdrawal headaches documented in narrative as comedic; physiologically real.
- **Alcohol:** moderate-to-heavy episodic, never depicted as full alcohol use disorder. Drinks beer at home (the cheap stuff, by choice — class identification, also taste). Drinks whiskey at bars, sparingly. **Does not drink alone when distressed** — the Harold Barton rule, internalized. He drinks alone when fine. The rule is calibrated to keep him safe from the worst version of himself, and he has held to it across canon with notable consistency.
- **Tobacco:** former, adolescent. Not current.
- **Cannabis:** essentially nil in canonical depiction; not refused on principle, simply not part of his pattern.
- **Harder substances:** declined, consistently. Even prescribed opioids post-ORIF for the tibia/fibula fractures were reportedly underconsumed; he took half what was prescribed and threw the rest out. **The vigilance is the whole point.** A man who watches himself this closely around substances is a man who knows what would happen if he stopped watching.
- **OTC use:** ibuprofen daily, sometimes twice; acetaminophen as backup; famotidine for the reflux ibuprofen causes; pseudoephedrine for the chronic congestion from the deviated septum; melatonin attempted and abandoned.
- **Prescribed psychiatric medication:** **none on file.** This is the largest single gap in the medical record. Subject has never been formally evaluated for the depressive and PTSD profile that the behavioral record clearly substantiates. He has never filled an SSRI. He has never sat for a structured trauma-focused therapy. The closest he has come is the in-character processing he does with Kate Bishop, with Lucky the dog, and (under duress) with Cap.

### II.8 SURGICAL HISTORY

Conservative documented list:
- ORIF, right tibia and fibula (post-*Hawkeye* #15).
- Multiple laceration repairs, field-grade, mostly facial.
- One appendectomy, mid-Avengers era, uneventful (small RLQ scar present).
- Dental crown placement x2.
- Tympanic membrane assessment


## Somatic Atlas

# 6. SOMATIC ATLAS: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS

A surveillance-grade body-record of the subject across forty years of observable behavior, organized by region and modulated by state. The thesis underwriting the catalog: *Barton's body is a more honest narrator than his mouth, and the discrepancy between the two is itself the diagnostic signal.* Where the verbal channel deflects, the somatic channel reports.

---

## 6.1 Build, Standing Posture, and the Resting Body

Six-foot-three, approximately 230 pounds, V-tapered through the shoulders and lats in the manner specific to bowmen rather than swimmers or boxers — the right deltoid and posterior shoulder are perceptibly larger than the left, the trapezius asymmetry visible through a t-shirt, the right forearm one to one-and-a-half centimeters thicker in mid-belly circumference. The draw side has built itself; the bow side has been disciplined into stability. Standing relaxed, weight rests 60/40 on the right leg — a carnival-rigger's habit, ready to pivot.

**Resting stance, civilian context.** Hands in front pockets or thumbs hooked in belt loops; a chronic, almost adolescent slouch that subtracts an inch and a half of his actual height. Pelvis tilted slightly anterior, lower lumbar in mild lordosis, a consequence of years of overdeveloped lats pulling the thoracic spine into kyphotic compensation when he stops actively bracing. Head carried forward of the shoulder line by perhaps two centimeters — the classic shooter's neck, plus the further forward-creep of a man with hearing loss who has spent years leaning toward speakers.

**Resting stance, operational context.** The slouch vanishes. He stands open-footed at hip width, knees soft, weight evenly distributed but with the rear foot slightly cocked outward for a quick draw-and-rotate. Both hands stay below the sternum and away from the body — never folded across the chest, never in pockets. He does not lean on walls when on assignment; he places his back near them at a finger's gap.

**The "Cap is in the room" tell.** When Captain America (or any internalized-authority figure he respects — Coulson historically, T'Challa occasionally) enters his sightline, the slouch self-corrects within a second and a half. He does not consciously straighten; he simply stops permitting the slump. This has been observable since the Kooky Quartet era and has never extinguished.

---

## 6.2 Gait

**Baseline walk.** A long, loose-hipped stride with a slight rolling toe-off, paced at roughly 115 steps per minute on level ground — slower than his cardiovascular fitness would predict. He ambles. The amble is deliberate camouflage: it broadcasts "harmless" in a city register and "lazy" in a team register. Arm swing is moderate on the left, suppressed on the right (the draw hand is held closer to the body, ready).

**Approach-to-rooftop gait.** On stairs and ladders he climbs two at a time using mostly his legs, not pulling with the arms — preserving the shoulders. He sets each foot quietly: heel-strike avoided, weight rolled across the lateral edge of the boot. On gravel rooftops the cadence shortens further and he distributes weight to minimize crunch. He has, observably, walked up behind enemies and teammates alike without alerting them; the soft gait is permanent, not summoned.

**Wounded gait.** Compensation goes to the contralateral hip rather than the obvious limp — he distributes the favoring through pelvic tilt rather than a visible drag, which makes him appear less injured than he is. This is partly trained (don't broadcast weakness) and partly a tell of how often he has had to keep moving while hurt.

**Hearing-aid-out gait.** Noticeably wider stance, head turning more frequently in shallow scanning arcs (10–15 degrees), gaze checking peripheries every two to four seconds. Compensates lost auditory perimeter with visual sweep.

---

## 6.3 Hands

The hands are the most over-trained part of him and the most diagnostically loaded.

**Permanent features.** Calluses across the pads of the right index, middle, and ring fingers (three-finger Mediterranean draw) — flat, yellowed, slightly cracked at the medial edge of the middle finger where the string sits hardest. The right thumbnail is kept shorter than the others, filed not clipped, to prevent string-snag. The left palm shows a thinner band of callus across the thenar pad from bow-grip pressure. Both wrists carry small linear scars from past wire-bindings and one parallel pair on the right wrist from a long-ago handcuff struggle. Knuckles enlarged on both hands, the right second metacarpal head visibly broader from an old, never-properly-set break.

**Resting hand posture.** Fingers curl naturally into a loose three-quarter fist, not fully open — the hands rest the way they hold a string. When he reads, holds a coffee cup, or watches television, the right hand will periodically and unconsciously perform a phantom nock-and-draw: index and middle finger pinch together at the pad, thumb folds, the wrist supinates a few degrees, and then releases. Frequency: roughly two to four times per hour, more when stressed. He does not know he does this.

**Coffee-cup hold.** Two-handed wrap around the mug, fingers interlaced beneath rather than handled by the grip — a thermal-comfort hold, not a drinking hold. Holds it at chest height for warming rather than sipping. The cup is rarely set down once picked up; he carries it for the duration.

**Pen and small-object handling.** Manipulates pens, coins, arrowheads, lighters through the fingers continuously when seated — a magician's roll across the knuckles, learned at the carnival and never lost. The roll is left-handed more often than right, sparing the draw hand. Frequency escalates with boredom or interpersonal discomfort; in a stationary conversation that has gone past his tolerance, the object will appear in the off hand within ninety seconds.

**Grip strength tells.** Handshakes are calibrated downward — he gives roughly 60% of his actual grip and watches the recipient's face to see if they noticed. Greets women and small-framed men with a notably softer grip than peer males. With Cap, with Logan, with Thor: a measured matching grip, never a contest.

---

## 6.4 Face

**Bone and tissue baseline.** Square jaw with a slightly lateral-deviated mandible from the *Blind Spot*-era break, healed without ideal alignment because he refused secondary surgery. The jaw clicks audibly to anyone within a foot of it when he chews on the left side; he therefore chews predominantly on the right. Brow ridge prominent, with a permanent two-centimeter horizontal scar through the left eyebrow that interrupts the hair growth — sustained pre-costume, origin disputed even by him. A smaller scar at the right corner of the mouth pulls the right side of his smile up a beat before the left.

**Eyes.** Blue, hyperacute distance vision (uncorrected 20/10 territory), with a documented tendency to converge focus at distance even in close conversation — he is often looking *through* the person he is speaking to at the wall behind them, a habit that reads as evasive but is actually targeting reflex. In stress, the pupils dilate noticeably; in flat affect (the dysthymic baseline), they are slightly under-responsive to ambient light, giving the eyes a glazed quality his teammates have read as fatigue and which is at least partially depressive.

**Blink rate.** Below average at rest (8–12 per minute), elevating to baseline-normal under social pressure, and dropping to near-zero in the final two seconds before a shot — the trained shooter's gaze-hold. After release, a single hard blink, almost a reset. This pre-shot stillness is the one observable behavior that distinguishes him visually from any non-shooter performing the same action.

**Smile architecture.** Three distinct smiles, all documented:
1. *The work smile.* Asymmetric right-side first, teeth slightly bared, eyes uninvolved — a press-conference and team-banter default. Holds about two seconds.
2. *The deflection smile.* Closed-mouth, lips compressed and pulled wide, accompanied by a small head-shake. Deployed when the conversation has touched something he will not address. Holds about a second and a half, then a hand goes to the back of the neck.
3. *The real smile.* Crinkles at the outer canthi, the asymmetry inverts (left-side first), teeth showing including the slightly chipped upper-right canine. Observable mostly around Kate Bishop, around the dog, around Cap, and in three documented instances around Bobbi. Rare. Lasts as long as the stimulus.

**Jaw and mouth at rest.** Mandible held slightly forward of neutral occlusion — a low-grade clench he is unaware of. Tongue often parked against the right upper molars. When concentrating on a shot, the tongue protrudes microscopically through the lips, the same childhood tell he had at twelve.

**Eyebrow micro-tells.** The scarred left brow lifts independently, a residual carnival-clown affect that he weaponizes for sarcasm. The right brow knits down in puzzlement or skepticism. When both go up symmetrically — rare — he is genuinely surprised, and the surprise has overridden his presentational control.

---

## 6.5 Voice and Speech

**Baseline register.** Mid-baritone, slightly nasal in the upper third, a residual flat Iowa vowel system that thirty years in New York has not fully sanded down. The "a" in "bag" and "Manhattan" still tips toward Midwest. He drops final g's selectively — "shootin'" but rarely "going" — code-switching by audience without conscious tracking.

**Volume calibration.** Consistently slightly louder than the room requires, by roughly 3–5 dB. This predates documented hearing loss and is now exacerbated by it. He does not modulate well in churches, hospitals, libraries.

**Speech rate.** Fast under social pressure (around 180 wpm), slow and clipped under operational pressure (around 110 wpm). Comedy register is fast; tactical register is slow. The crossover is the early warning: when his joke-cadence slows, the joke is no longer a joke.

**Verbal tics.**
- Sentence-initial "Look — " when he is about to lie or about to refuse to discuss something.
- "Yeah, no" as a frequent disagreement-softener.
- "Okay" used as a self-directed cue between physical actions, half under the breath.
- Trails off into "...whatever" or "...so" when an emotional sentence is asked to complete itself.
- Calls people "kid," "boss," "champ," and "buddy" — none of them affectionate in the way they sound; the diminutive is distance management.

**The "huh?" tell.** Even with hearing aids functioning, he asks for repetition more often than his actual auditory comprehension requires. Buys himself processing time and shifts the floor back to the speaker. In genuine non-hearing, the request is faster and accompanied by a quarter-turn of the better ear; in the stalling version, the eyes stay fixed on the speaker.

**ASL.** Right-hand-dominant signing, fluid but with a perceptible Midwest-English syntactic substrate — he signs in English word order more than in idiomatic ASL grammar when stressed, indicating that ASL is a later acquisition incompletely consolidated. Signs faster than he speaks. Facial grammar (the eyebrow and mouth shapes that carry meaning in ASL) is more expressive than his spoken face; signing, he is more visibly emotional than speaking. With Kate, who matches him in fluency, he uses both hands and the full register; with hearing teammates trying to follow, he simplifies to one hand and English order. Around Barney, signing collapses into something both more childish and more intimate — the brothers' private creole.

---

## 6.6 Breathing

**Resting respiration.** Twelve to fourteen breaths per minute, nasal, diaphragmatic. Belly rises before chest, the breath pattern of a trained shooter who has rebuilt his respiratory mechanics around stillness. In street clothes on a couch this can drop to ten.

**Pre-shot breathing protocol.** Inhale through nose over three counts, hold at half-capacity for one beat, exhale through slightly parted lips over four counts, release the arrow in the natural pause between exhale and next inhale. Reproducible to the half-second across decades of depicted shots. This is the most ritualized motor pattern in his body.

**Stress breathing.** Inverts to chest, shallows, accelerates — but he catches it. Within five to ten seconds of any threat-onset spike he will visibly reset to diaphragmatic, often with a single deep audible exhale through the nose. The reset is faster than most field operatives' and is the strongest evidence of consistent, private self-regulation work he never acknowledges.

**Emotional breathing.** Sighs deeply and audibly when alone, near-silently when observed. The sighs are exhalations through compressed lips, often accompanied by a hand to the face. Frequency tracks the dysthymic baseline — half a dozen times an hour in low periods, almost absent in active operational phases. Surveillance of him alone in a kitchen is the single highest-yield diagnostic context.

---

## 6.7 Sleep Architecture

**Schedule.** Functionally circadian-shattered. Default pattern across the Bed-Stuy period and likely beyond: bed between 2 and 4 a.m., wake between 9 and 11, with two to four micro-naps across the day on couches, in chairs, in passenger seats of cars. Total sleep approximately five to six hours of poor quality. Operational deployment overrides everything and he can sustain forty-eight to seventy-two hour wakefulness with caffeine and adrenaline before the crash.

**Sleep position.** Side sleeper, predominantly right side, dominant hand under the pillow with — historically — a knife or pistol or quiver-reach beneath it. Left arm across the body. Pillow doubled to elevate the head, a hearing-loss adaptation (vibration sensing through bone conduction when an aid is out) and an old neck-stiffness compensation. Sleeps in a t-shirt and shorts in any climate; will not sleep nude in a strange environment.

**Arousal threshold.** Wakes to vibration (footfall) faster than to sound. Hyperaroused wake-pattern: from full sleep to feet-on-floor with weapon in hand in under three seconds, repeatedly documented. After waking, requires ninety seconds to two minutes to verbally orient — the body wakes faster than the mind.

**Dream behavior.** Talks in sleep sporadically. Documented sleep-talk content (per Kate, per Bobbi historically) skews toward names — "Barney," "Bob," "Cap," "no" — rather than narrative. Twitches, kicks. Has woken swinging more than once; partners have learned to wake him from across the bed and not by touch.

**Dawn behavior.** First action on rising is coffee, not water, not voiding. Stands at the counter while it brews, both hands on the edge of the counter, head down, for ninety seconds to two minutes. The single most reliable solitary ritual in the file.

---

## 6.8 Eating

**Caloric load.** Approximately 4,000–4,500 kcal/day under operational demand; drops to 2,500–3,000 in down-cycles with composition deteriorating sharply.

**Food selection.** Strongly biased toward portable, room-temperature-tolerant, single-handed foods: pizza, sandwiches, breakfast tacos, hot dogs, cereal eaten dry from the box, jerky. Microwaved leftovers. Coffee — heavy, black, constant, with a tolerance that suggests six to ten cups daily. He does not cook beyond eggs and the occasional skillet meat. Will eat over the sink standing.

**Eating tempo.** Fast, in the carnival-kid pattern of someone who learned that food is contested. Three to four bites per minute of any solid; rarely puts the food down between bites. Drinks between courses, not during. Does not talk with food in his mouth — one of the few table manners that survived.

**Comfort eating.** Sugar and starch escalate in low phases. Pizza becomes daily. Ice cream eaten from the carton, standing in front of an open freezer, observable as a behavioral marker of a bad week.

**Restaurant behavior.** Sits facing the door, back to the wall, every time without exception. Orders quickly and without reading much of the menu — decides in roughly fifteen seconds. Tips generously and in cash, leaves the cash under a glass.

---

## 6.9 Substance Use, Granular

**Coffee.** First contact within ten minutes of waking, last contact often after 9 p.m. — clearly contributory to the sleep problem, clearly tolerated. Drinks any quality and complains about none. The mug is a thermal anchor as much as a delivery vehicle.

**Alcohol.** Beer predominantly, domestic, two to four in a typical social evening, occasionally six on a bad night. Spirits rarely and only neat. Watches his own pace — observable behavior: he will set a beer down half-finished and not return to it if he notices the can adding up. Will refuse a drink offered by someone he doesn't trust. Has been observed pouring out a drink unobserved on more than one occasion in domestic contexts. The Harold Barton-watch is permanent.

**Tobacco.** Non-smoker. Will hold a cigarette as a prop in deep cover.

**Pharmaceuticals.** Over-the-counter analgesics consumed at high but not toxic frequency — ibuprofen as a daily condiment in the field. Resists prescription pain medication actively after one or two depicted exposures; the loss-of-edge frightens him more than the pain.

**Illicit.** Abstains. No depicted recreational drug use across the file.

---

## 6.10 Grooming and Dress

**Hair.** Blond, kept short to medium, self-cut as often as professionally cut — visible irregularities at the nape suggest a bathroom mirror and clippers. Grows out during low phases until someone (Kate, an Avenger, occasionally Bobbi historically) prompts him to address it.

**Facial hair.** Shaves inconsistently. Two-to-five-day stubble is the modal state. Cleanly shaved for Avengers PR appearances and weddings/funerals; full beard only during exile periods and undercover work. The shave-state is a reasonably reliable mood gauge.

**Clothing.** Civilian register: jeans, t-shirts (often purple, sometimes obscure-band, occasionally his own iconography worn unironically as a joke he doesn't explain), zip hoodies, a beaten leather jacket, work boots or low-top sneakers. Same outfit across multiple days is normal. Operational register: tactical layers under whatever street clothes the mission requires, a documented and excessive number of pockets, a quiver-harness he has personally modified at least four times.

**Hygiene.** Showers daily under normal conditions, skips when depressed, returns to it without comment. Smells, when fresh, of cheap soap and bow-string wax; when not fresh, of sweat and coffee.

**Accessories.** A wristwatch on the left (mechanical, cheap, replaced often — they break). Hearing aids: behind-the-ear, often visible because he does not bother to hide them, sometimes purple-cased in a deliberately on-brand choice that doubles as fuck-you to anyone expecting embarrassment. No rings since the divorce, though the indentation on the left fourth finger was visible for years after.

---

## 6.11 Sexual and Intimate-Physical Behavior

**Approach pattern.** Slow, verbal, deflective, indirect. He does not initiate physically until physically initiated upon. The verbal banter is courtship and screening simultaneously — he will not advance with a partner who cannot match the deflection register, because he cannot tolerate being approached sincerely.

**Touch baseline with non-intimates.** Low. He does not touch teammates much beyond hand-on-shoulder reassurance, a backslap on greeting, the occasional hair-ruffle (Kate, younger heroes — paternal register, unconscious). Does not hug men except Cap and Barney, and the Barney hugs are stiff. Hugs women in greeting only when they initiate.

**Touch baseline with intimates.** Affectionate but spatially modest in public; in private, demonstrably more demonstrative, hand-on-hip and forehead-to-forehead gestures common. He reaches with the left hand by default, sparing the right for weapon-readiness — an operational habit that has bled into intimacy and which more observant partners have noticed.

**Sexual register.** Generous, attentive, somewhat performative — the deflection-via-competence pattern carries into bed. Reluctant to be the focus, prefers to be the giver, which partners have variously read as gallantry and as avoidance. Eye contact during intimacy is intermittent rather than sustained; he closes his eyes more than baseline.

**Post-coital pattern.** Talkative when secure (Bobbi era, peak), silent and prone to getting up to do small tasks when not. The kitchen-visit at 3 a.m. is the somatic marker of a relationship in trouble.

**Refusal of intimacy.** When emotionally overwhelmed, he will physically retreat from touch by small increments — a half-step back, a shoulder-roll out of a hand, the production of a coffee cup as an interpositional object. He does not name the retreat; the body simply executes it.

---

## 6.12 Micro-Movements and Tics

**The back-of-the-neck rub.** Right hand to the nape, head dips, elbow flares. The single most frequent gesture in the file. Deployed during embarrassment, during avoidance, during transition between topics he does not want to address. Frequency under interpersonal stress: every two to three minutes.

**The bridge-of-the-nose pinch.** Index and thumb to the inner canthi, eyes closed, exhale. Deployed when overwhelmed by other people's competence or by a problem he cannot shoot. Two to five seconds.

**The bow-hand check.** Even unarmed, the left hand will float to a phantom grip at hip level when scanning an unfamiliar room. The fingers curl into the bow-grip shape. He does not know he does this.

**Quiver-touch.** When armed, the right elbow brushes the quiver every ten to twenty seconds — counting by feel, not by sight. He can tell you arrow count without looking.

**Pocket-cycling.** When standing and waiting, runs the right thumb across his fingertips in sequence: index, middle, ring, pinky, ring, middle, index. Calluses-check, unconscious. Carnie tell — the rigger's recount of his own kit.

**The eye-line snap.** In any new room, his gaze does a counterclockwise sweep — exits, elevated positions, sightlines, then people. Takes approximately four seconds. Then he relaxes posturally. The sweep does not extinguish even in safe rooms.

**Foot-tap.** Right foot, ball of foot, at roughly 120 bpm when seated and bored or stressed. Suppresses immediately when noticed by another.

**Lip-bite.** Lower lip, left side, between the canine and the first premolar. Pre-decision tell; he is choosing between two options. Lasts as long as the choice.

**Half


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## Section 6 — Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 6.1 Foundational Template: The Waverly Schema

Every adult relationship in Clinton Francis Barton's file is a variation on a single childhood theorem, and the theorem is this: **the people who love you hit you, the people who protect you leave you, and the people who teach you eventually try to kill you.** This is not metaphor. It is the literal evidentiary record of his first sixteen years.

The Waverly Schema is constructed from four serial attachment figures, each of whom occupied the role of *primary other* at a developmentally critical moment, and each of whom resolved that role through betrayal:

1. **Harold Barton (father).** The originating template. Affection and violence colocated in the same body. Clint's earliest learned association is that the smell of alcohol on a parental figure predicts both the chance of being held and the certainty of being struck. Edith does not intervene; she is the second template — *the loving witness who does not stop it*. Together they teach the boy that closeness is the prerequisite for harm and that bystanders are complicit.
2. **Barney Barton (brother).** The first chosen attachment, the one selected rather than given, and therefore the most heavily cathected. Barney was protector against Harold and abuser-in-Harold's-absence — the same dyad reproduced inside the sibling bond. When the brothers ran to the carnival, Clint was running *with* his abuser-protector, not *from* him. Barney's eventual defection to criminality, faked death, and serial reappearance has produced in Clint a complete inability to maintain stable cognitive object-constancy regarding his brother: every Barney appearance resets the relationship to zero.
3. **Jacques Duquesne (Swordsman).** Surrogate father #1. Skilled, charismatic, taught Clint actual craft. Was embezzling from the carnival. When Clint caught him, beat him nearly to death and left him for dead. The lesson encoded: *competence in your mentor does not predict his integrity, and discovering his corruption will be punished as if you had committed it.*
4. **Buck Chisholm (Trick Shot).** Surrogate father #2, sought *after* Swordsman, in a transparent attempt to re-find what the first betrayal cost him. Same arc, longer fuse: training, bond, criminal disclosure, abandonment, and later active homicidal intent toward his former protégé. Clint has by this point run the experiment twice and gotten the same result.

By the age of approximately sixteen, the subject has had four primary male attachment figures, and the base rate of betrayal in his lived experience is **100%**. No control group. No counterexample. This is the dataset against which every subsequent relationship is unconsciously regressed.

The somatic legacy: Clint flinches at raised hands from people who love him in a way he does not flinch from enemies. He is described, across multiple runs, as physically still under combat threat and physically restless under domestic peace. Peace is the anomaly his nervous system was not trained to predict.

### 6.2 Attachment Classification

Formal classification: **disorganized attachment with a dominant anxious-preoccupied surface and a covert avoidant defensive layer.** In Bowlby-Ainsworth terms, he is the child who in the Strange Situation neither approaches nor avoids the caregiver but performs both contradictory behaviors in sequence — moves toward, then freezes, then turns away, then circles back. Adult expression of this pattern in Barton:

- **Approach.** Falls fast, hard, and verbally. Will commit (verbally) before he commits (behaviorally).
- **Freeze.** As soon as the other party reciprocates with stable presence, a paralysis sets in. He goes quiet, becomes evasive, "needs space," takes a mission.
- **Withdraw.** Geographic exile. The leaving-the-Avengers cycle is, among other things, an attachment behavior.
- **Return.** Comes back wisecracking, as if no rupture occurred. Tests whether the other party will hold the line or punish the absence.

Adults with this profile typically partner with one of two types: (a) other disorganized partners, producing volatile cycles of merger and rupture; (b) anxious-preoccupied partners who chase, allowing the subject to enact the avoidant half indefinitely. Barton's romantic history shows option (a) almost exclusively. His functional partnerships — the ones that *work* — show a third configuration: secure-base partners who refuse to chase and refuse to leave (Cap; arguably Kate Bishop in the apprentice role).

### 6.3 The Bonding Sequence

Barton's bonding behavior follows an observable, near-ritualized sequence across nearly every significant relationship in the file. The sequence is fast — sometimes inside a single encounter — and is one of the most reliable behavioral fingerprints in the dossier.

**Stage 1 — Imprint.** A single interpersonal cue triggers attachment formation. The cues are diagnostic: someone competent who *notices* him (the rarity of the experience is the trigger); someone in distress whom he can help (restitutional bonding); someone who reads as wounded-and-defended in a way he recognizes (kin-recognition of trauma). Natasha hit all three in *Tales of Suspense* #57 inside ten pages of panel time. Bobbi hit them in a single mission. Wanda hit them across years of proximity. Kate hit them by *being him at nineteen*.

**Stage 2 — Verbal commitment.** He talks. The mouth runs ahead of the rest of him. Banter, nicknames, declarations framed as jokes that are not jokes ("partner," "boss," "Hawkeye"). The verbal commitment is real but is also a *binding spell* — he is trying to talk himself into a position he is not yet sure he can hold.

**Stage 3 — Operational fusion.** He aligns his tactical behavior to the other party. He will take their missions, defend their bad calls, absorb their consequences. This is where the *radicalization-by-infatuation* pattern lives: the willingness to attack Iron Man for a woman he met that afternoon is not an aberration; it is the modal Stage 3 behavior, varying only in target.

**Stage 4 — Defensive withdrawal under reciprocation.** The other party returns the warmth at a level that exceeds his capacity to receive it. He breaks eye contact, makes a joke, leaves the room, takes a mission. The withdrawal is rarely interpreted by the other party as withdrawal; it reads as Hawkeye-being-Hawkeye, which is the camouflage utility of the wisecrack-and-exit move.

**Stage 5 — Test.** Some manufactured or seized-upon rupture. A risk taken, a confidence withheld, a stupid fight picked. This is the part of the sequence the subject would deny he is doing, but it is documented across every long-form relationship in his canon. He needs to know whether the other party will leave when given cause.

**Stage 6 — One of two terminals.** Either (a) the other party leaves or dies or proves untrustworthy, confirming the Waverly Schema and producing acute decompensation followed by exile, OR (b) the other party holds the line, at which point Clint will love them, with reservations, for the rest of his life.

Cap is the canonical Stage 6(b). Kate is the canonical Stage 6(b). Bobbi was Stage 6(a) by mutual destruction. Natasha is the rare ambiguous case — neither fully held nor fully ruptured, which is why the relationship has outlived all the others as a low-grade chronic attachment that neither resolves nor dissolves.

### 6.4 Distrust Architecture

The subject's distrust is not generalized. It is **structurally specific**, and the specificity is itself revealing.

He extends baseline trust easily, even foolishly, to:
- Strangers in immediate distress.
- Anyone Cap has vouched for.
- Anyone who reminds him of himself at a younger age.
- Operatives who present competence under duress.
- Animals. Especially dogs.

He withholds trust, often past the point of strategic sense, from:
- Institutional authority (S.H.I.E.L.D. directors, government liaisons, Tony Stark in a CEO register).
- Anyone whose presentation seems polished or rehearsed (he reads polish as concealment, because in his childhood it was).
- Anyone who tries to *help* him in a structured way (therapists, mentors with credentials, the medical system).
- Anyone who has lied to him once, even trivially, on a personal matter — the threshold for personal-disclosure deceit is near-zero, even as his tolerance for operational deceit is professional.

The asymmetry between his **personal-deceit threshold** (intolerant) and his **operational-deceit threshold** (highly tolerant — he is a former con-artist; the carnival raised him on misdirection) is one of the cleanest diagnostic markers in his file. It indicates that the betrayals that shaped him were *personal in the guise of intimate*, and his nervous system has zoned the protective response accordingly.

### 6.5 How He Betrays

The file would be incomplete if it documented only the betrayals committed against the subject and not those committed by him. He has a betrayal repertoire, and it is consistent.

**He does not lie for advantage.** He does not cheat romantically with intent — even the apparent infidelities in the file are typically prior-relationship overlap or post-rupture rebounds that he reads as betrayals after the fact and the partner often does not. The structure is *self-accusatory rather than predatory.*

**He betrays by absence.** The exile pattern. He leaves without adequate communication. He takes missions to avoid conversations. He goes dark for weeks. Partners read this, accurately, as a form of betrayal — the withdrawal of presence that was implicitly promised.

**He betrays by rigidity.** The Bobbi-Phantom Rider rupture is the master example. Presented with a moral situation that required compassionate ambiguity, he chose the rule over the person. He has done this repeatedly in smaller registers — held people to standards he himself violates, because the standard is the only structure he trusts and he needs the people he loves to also be inside it. The marriage to Bobbi did not end because she killed the Rider; it ended because he could not metabolize the moral mess of it without retreating into the Cap-internalized superego, and she could not stay married to that superego.

**He betrays by self-sacrifice.** A subtler pattern. Dying in *Disassembled* was, among other things, a relational act — he left the team in the most unanswerable way available. The subsequent Ronin period is the recoil. The pattern recurs: when an emotional situation exceeds his capacity, he will offer his body as the solution, and the people who love him experience this (accurately) as a form of abandonment dressed as heroism.

**He betrays by silence.** The hearing loss, undisclosed; the depressive periods, undisclosed; the Banner aftermath, undisclosed. Partners learn what is wrong with him from third parties or from observation, never from his account.

### 6.6 The Repair Repertoire

Repair behavior is where the subject is most undertheorized in surface reads. He is, contrary to his self-presentation, a *skilled repairer* — within a narrow band of methods.

**What he does well in repair:**
- **Shows up.** Will physically appear, often unannounced, often having traveled a long way, when the relationship needs proof of continued existence. This is his most reliable repair move and the one most often missed by analysts who focus on his verbal output.
- **Material acts.** Fixes the broken thing. Brings the coffee. Pays the rent. Takes the bullet. He will pay debts in body and labor that he cannot pay in language.
- **Sustained patience under the other party's anger.** He absorbs blame with a kind of professional equanimity, because he believes most of it. This makes him a uniquely durable target for emotional venting from people he loves, and they use him this way.
- **Mentorship as repair.** When he cannot fix a relationship with a peer, he will redirect the relational energy into mentorship of a younger figure who reminds him of the peer (or of himself).

**What he does poorly in repair:**
- **Verbal acknowledgment.** The words "I'm sorry, I was wrong, this is what I felt" are nearly absent from his canonical vocabulary in the configurations that would actually constitute repair. He apologizes glibly and reflexively for small things; he cannot apologize substantively for the things that matter.
- **Sustained processing.** He cannot sit in a conversation about the rupture for the length of time required to actually resolve it. The wisecrack-and-exit will eventually deploy.
- **Asking for repair from the other party.** He does not request the apologies he is owed. The transactional asymmetry compounds: he absorbs, they vent, the ledger never balances, the relationship eventually corrodes from his unmet side.

### 6.7 Intimacy & Dependency

Intimacy is **inversely correlated with role-protection** in the subject's relational schema. He is most intimate where the role is most clearly defined and least intimate where the role dissolves.

- **Mentor → mentee (downward):** maximum sustainable intimacy. He gives Kate Bishop more of himself than he has given any romantic partner. The role protects both parties; he knows what he is supposed to do and so does she.
- **Soldier → commander (upward):** high sustainable intimacy. Cap. The role is the relationship; he can love Cap exactly to the depth the chain of command licenses, which is, for him, very deep.
- **Brother-in-arms (lateral, role-defined):** moderate to high. Bucky, in *Tales of Suspense*. The mission defines the bond; intimacy can occur inside that container.
- **Romantic partnership (lateral, role-undefined):** catastrophic over time. There is no role to hide inside. The vulnerability is total and his tolerance for total vulnerability is near-zero. Every long-term romantic partnership in the file has either ended or stabilized only by the partner accepting a partial, intermittent version of him.
- **Family of origin (Barney):** uncategorizable. The role is so corrupted at the root that no stable container can be built.

Dependency runs on a parallel inverse axis. He will **accept dependency from others** — gratefully, almost greedily; being needed is one of the few self-states that quiets the screw-up narrative — but **cannot tolerate his own dependency on others**. The asymmetry is one of his most legible behaviors. He will nurse a partner through their crisis with patience and competence; he will refuse identical care from the same partner in his own crisis. The pattern is so consistent that partners learn either to provide care covertly (Kate leaving coffee, Bobbi historically managing his medical follow-up without telling him) or to give up on providing it at all.

The counter-dependence is rationalized through the powers-deficit framing — *I'm the guy with no powers, I have to be self-sufficient* — but the causal arrow runs the other way. The lack of powers did not cause the counter-dependence; the counter-dependence selected the *no-powers Avenger* identity as its most defensible costume.

### 6.8 The Relational Template, Person by Person

A walk through the canonical relationships, each examined for how the Waverly Schema and the Bonding Sequence express across the specific dyad.

**Natasha Romanoff.** The original imprint of adult attachment. Met as enemies, bonded inside an afternoon, he switched moral framework for her, she eventually switched it back for him. The relationship has never resolved across sixty years of canon and will not, because both parties recognize, accurately, that they are each other's recurring symptom rather than each other's cure. Stage 6 has been deferred indefinitely. They cycle through Stages 1-5 every time they share a panel. The intimacy is genuine and the distance is necessary; both know it.

**Captain America (Steve Rogers).** The corrective attachment figure. The first adult male in Clint's life to (a) hold a standard, (b) apply it consistently, (c) not hit him, (d) not leave him, (e) not betray him. Cap has done the impossible thing in Barton's nervous system, which is to be present, authoritative, and safe simultaneously. The result is that Clint has internalized Cap as superego at a depth that survives Cap's death, absence, and even ideological deviation. The Ronin identity is the proof: a masterless samurai is a samurai who is still oriented to the absent master. He does not stop being Cap's soldier when Cap is dead; he just becomes a soldier of an absence.

**Bobbi Morse.** The most thoroughly attempted lateral bond. Marriage entered into at a speed consistent with the Bonding Sequence (fast, declarative, operationally fused). Held for years under conditions of role-protection (West Coast Avengers as the role-container). Collapsed exactly when the role-container could no longer hold a piece of moral content that required *non-role* intimacy to process. He chose the rule over her, then watched her die, then got her back, then lost her again. The Bobbi relationship is the master case for *what happens when the Waverly Schema meets an actual peer*: it cannot survive contact with the things that peers must survive.

**Wanda Maximoff.** Quieter, longer-running, lower-amplitude. Sister-in-arms attachment that periodically tipped toward romantic and was managed back. He bonded to her at Stage 1-2 across many years without ever fully escalating. When she broke (the various Wanda-fracture events), he was destabilized in a way disproportionate to the apparent intimacy, which is the tell: he was more attached than he or anyone else acknowledged.

**Kate Bishop.** The successful relationship. Successful because it is mentorship — role-protected, intergenerational, structurally non-romantic. He has given Kate the things he could not give Bobbi: sustained presence, durable apology, acknowledgment of his own deficits in real time. The success is partly *because* of the role-protection and partly because Kate, by character design, refuses to leave when he runs the test. She is the one person in his file who has consistently passed Stage 5 and held him through Stage 6(b). She has accordingly become the most stable attachment object in his adult life, more stable even than Cap, because she is contemporary and chosen and refuses to disappear.

**Barney Barton.** The unresolvable. Every appearance resets the relationship. Clint cannot achieve object-constancy with his brother because the brother oscillates between protector and antagonist on a timeline that defeats integration. The *Hawkeye* #19 barn issue is the most psychologically naked depiction in the file: ASL, childhood regression, Barney wheelchair-bound, both of them speaking past each other in a language they share precisely because the spoken language failed them as children. He will never finish with Barney, and he will never stop trying to.

**The civilians (the apartment building, the Bed-Stuy neighbors, the kids).** The displaced family. He attaches at low intensity to large numbers of ordinary people and protects them in lieu of the family he cannot protect or constitute. The diffuseness of the attachment is its safety; no single tenant can betray him in a way that would unmake him. This is **family by population rather than by individual**, and it is one of his most adaptive accommodations.

**Bruce Banner.** Not a relationship in the bonding-sequence sense, but a relational object of permanent psychic residence. He killed a man who asked to be killed, and he carries the man with him as a kind of unfinished interlocutor. Banner has become a posthumous attachment figure — an internal presence who never resolves, structurally similar to the way Cap functions during Cap's deaths.

### 6.9 The Repeating Template, Stated Plainly

Across all of the above, a single shape recurs with diagnostic regularity:

> **He finds a person who can hurt him. He gives them the means to hurt him. He tests whether they will. If they do, he leaves and confirms the schema. If they don't, he loves them in a guarded, grateful, lifelong, conditional way and will eventually betray them by absence so that he never has to watch them leave first.**

The template is the answer to a question his nervous system formulated at age eight and has never been allowed to revise: *if intimacy means harm, how do I get the intimacy without the harm?* His operational solution, refined over six decades, has been to compress the harm into a form he controls — *I will leave before you can, I will fail before you can find me failing, I will hold you at the exact distance where I can still reach you with an arrow.* The bow, in this reading, is not incidental to his attachment style. **It is his attachment style instrumented.** It is the technology of staying close enough to matter and far enough to survive.

He has built a life in which this configuration is heroism, and the configuration is heroism, and it is also a wound that has never been dressed because dressing it would require him to let someone close enough to bandage it, which is the exact maneuver his entire nervous system was built to prevent.

That is the file on how Clinton Francis Barton loves people. It is the file on how he was loved first.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## Section 6 — Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

The defensive architecture of Subject Barton is, like the rest of him, deceptively legible. He presents as a man with no inner life worth defending — a wisecracking craftsman who does the job and goes home to feed the dog. The presentation is itself the apex defense. Beneath it sits a stratified system, decades-stable, that has permitted him to remain functional through a childhood that should have produced an institutionalized adult, a career that should have produced a suicide, and a bereavement load that should have produced a recluse. The system works. It also costs him almost everything that is not the job.

What follows is the architecture mapped from primitive to mature, with the behavioral signatures, somatic tells, and longitudinal evidence each defense generates in the field record.

---

### 6.1 Architectural Overview

Barton's defenses cluster into four functional tiers:

1. **Primitive tier** — operating below conscious access, deployed automatically in moments of acute affective threat: dissociation-lite, somatization, acting-out, and a peculiar form of identification-with-the-aggressor that runs the inward direction (he becomes his own abuser).
