2. **Neurotic-immature tier** — the workhorse of daily functioning: humor, denial-by-minimization, displacement (almost always into combat or property destruction), and a heavily ritualized form of counter-dependence.
3. **Higher-neurotic tier** — reaction formation against the Harold Barton template, intellectualization-via-craft, isolation of affect.
4. **Mature tier** — sublimation (the bow, the mentorship, the building), altruism (the apartment building, the kid-heroes, the civilians), and a thin, late-developing layer of humor-as-genuine-grace (distinct from humor-as-deflection, and rarer).

The system is dense at the bottom and top and surprisingly thin in the middle. This is diagnostic: he has not built robust neurotic defenses because he never had the developmental window in which they are built. He went directly from infantile coping (the primitive layer, set in the Barton house) to forced adult mastery (the mature layer, set in carnival labor and combat). The intervening shelf of ordinary adolescent neurosis — the small, sustaining hypocrisies, the social face, the easy white lies, the comfortable rationalizations — is conspicuously absent. He is brutally honest with himself in private and almost ceremonially evasive in public, and this mismatch is the gap where the neurotic middle layer should be.

---

### 6.2 Primitive Tier

**Acting-Out.** The first and oldest defense. When affect rises beyond the system's metabolic capacity, Barton converts it into kinetic action. The conversion ratio is roughly 1:1 — one unprocessed feeling, one bad decision, one injury. Behavioral signatures: the unscheduled patrol, the picked fight, the deliberately overmatched engagement (taking on Crossfire's operation solo, taking on the Tracksuits solo after every emotional reverse, the entirety of *Hawkeye: Freefall*'s opening). Diagnostically reliable predictor: the larger the relational rupture in the preceding 72 hours, the worse the tactical hygiene of the next op. Cap-death sequelae, post-Bobbi sequelae, post-Banner sequelae all show the same pattern — competence under planning conditions, recklessness under acute grief.

**Somatization.** Distress that cannot be metabolized cognitively presents in the body. The hearing loss is the catastrophic example — the original injury was sustained in a crisis-improvisation moment, but its *non-treatment* across two decades is somatic-channel defense: keeping the wound in the body keeps it out of speech. He limps for weeks rather than seeing a doctor; the lower-back complaint surfaces in the panels exactly when emotional content surfaces in the dialogue. He gets food poisoning the week of his anniversary. He throws his shoulder out the day after Barney calls. The body keeps the schedule the conscious mind refuses to.

**Dissociation-lite.** Not full dissociative episodes — he is too task-grounded for that — but micro-detachments under acute affect, depicted across runs as the thousand-yard stare, the missed cue in conversation, the *"what?"* that is not (only) the hearing loss. Aja's panel grammar in Fraction's run renders this with unusual fidelity: the wordless sequences where Clint stops registering the room are not stylistic flourishes, they are accurate depictions of a man going briefly absent from his own life to reduce input load. Frequency: low but reliable, clustered around anniversaries (the Bobbi date, the Cap date), holidays, and the periodic visits from Barney.

**Identification with the Aggressor (Inward-Directed).** The most insidious primitive defense in the stack. Barton internalized Harold Barton not by becoming an abuser of others — he aggressively did not — but by becoming the abuser of himself. The internal voice that calls him a screw-up, a moron, a waste of the bunk, the *"Barton, you idiot"* monologue audible across every run from 1965 onward, is not Clint's voice. It is Harold's, repurposed by the child who could not afford to disagree with his father and so installed him as the narrator. This is why the *"sincere"* version of being called dumb (per the Pressure Points analysis) produces disproportionate injury: it is the father speaking through the new mouth, and Clint cannot afford to confirm the verdict.

**Splitting (Partial, Object-Limited).** Not the global splitting of borderline structure. Object-specific, and reserved almost exclusively for Barney and for Clint himself. Barney is brother-savior or brother-betrayer with no intermediate position; Clint is the screw-up or the man who got the shot off, with little tolerance for the ordinary mixed verdict. With most other objects (Cap, Natasha, Bobbi, Kate, even Trick Shot in retrospect) he holds mixed feeling competently. The splitting is geographically restricted to the original family unit, which is consistent with the etiology.

---

### 6.3 Neurotic-Immature Tier

**Humor as Affect-Management.** The defense Barton is most famous for and least credited for the sophistication of. It operates at three distinguishable settings:

- *Setting one — ambient banter.* The wisecracks during combat, the patter with teammates, the running commentary. Function: keep the social temperature warm enough that no one asks the real question. Cost: low. Sustainability: high.
- *Setting two — pointed self-deprecation.* The *"I'm just the guy with the bow,"* the *"that went about as well as expected,"* the pre-emptive admission of incompetence. Function: control the narrative of his own inadequacy by being the first to state it; deny others the satisfaction or threat of stating it for him. Cost: moderate — every utterance reinforces the internal verdict. Sustainability: high, with corrosive long-term effects on self-concept.
- *Setting three — black humor under acute crisis.* The jokes told over a fresh corpse, after Banner, mid-bleed-out. Function: maintain operational consciousness by refusing the affect that would incapacitate. Cost: high — it isolates him from anyone who responds normally to crisis. Sustainability: degrading; the jokes get less funny across the decades, and he knows it.

The diagnostic move is to track which setting is active. Setting one is baseline; setting two indicates moderate stress; setting three indicates the system is at the redline and acting-out is imminent.

**Denial-by-Minimization.** Not denial of fact — Clint is too honest for outright denial — but compulsive downgrading of significance. *"It's fine."* *"It's not a big deal."* *"I've had worse."* The hearing loss is *"a thing."* The marriage collapse is *"how it goes."* The brother is *"complicated."* The death and resurrection is, astonishingly, *"weird, right?"* The defense permits him to acknowledge the data while refusing the weight, which preserves both his honesty and his function at the cost of any actual processing.

**Displacement.** Affective content that cannot be addressed at the source is reliably routed into (a) combat, (b) property destruction, (c) coffee consumption, or (d) the dog. Combat: covered above. Property destruction: the consistent depiction of a man whose living space is in low-grade ruin; the broken furniture, the patched walls, the appliance he punched in 1987 and never replaced. Coffee: the cup count rises with stress; the third pot is a tell. The dog: appropriate, regulated, healthy displacement — affection that cannot be safely directed at humans gets directed at the animal, which is one of the few unambiguously functional channels in the system.

**Counter-Dependence.** Ranked here rather than higher because, despite its sophistication of expression, the underlying logic is infantile: *if I never need anyone, no one can leave me.* Behavioral signatures: declining medical help, declining tactical support, taking the solo route when the team route is available, the *"I got this"* refrain, the geographic exile pattern. He will accept help from precisely two categories of person: those he has identified as needing help themselves (Kate, the apartment tenants — accepting help becomes giving help by inversion) and Captain America, whose authority bypasses the defense entirely. From peers in lateral position the defense holds.

**Isolation of Affect.** The capacity to discuss the worst events of his life in a flat, factual register, stripped of feeling-content. The Banner debrief, the Bobbi anecdotes told to Kate, the childhood material when he can be brought to discuss it at all — all delivered in a tone appropriate to a weather report. The affect is not absent; it is sequestered. It returns later, in the body or in the acting-out, but it does not appear in the speech.

---

### 6.4 Higher-Neurotic Tier

**Reaction Formation Against Harold Barton.** Possibly the single most behaviorally productive defense in his system. Every paternal behavior Clint witnessed has produced its inverse in his adult conduct: Harold drank to oblivion, Clint monitors every drink; Harold hit, Clint will not strike a non-combatant and is conspicuously gentle with children; Harold was cruel for sport, Clint refuses tactical cruelty even at operational cost; Harold abandoned the family by dying drunk at the wheel, Clint cannot leave a building of strangers to a slumlord. The defense is so total that it has become character — he no longer has to think about it. It is also why he cannot tolerate any evidence of similarity to his father; the *"you're just like him"* accusation, in any form, will detonate him.

**Intellectualization-via-Craft.** Affective content gets converted into technical content. Grief becomes a question of draw weight; rage becomes a question of windage; despair becomes a question of fletching. The bench-work, the arrow-building, the obsessive equipment ritual — these are not hobbies, they are the venue where unspeakable material is metabolized into solvable problems. The defense is mature in form and immature in function: it is genuinely productive, but it permits indefinite postponement of the underlying content.

**Isolation (Social).** The geographic exile pattern (Stage 4 of the stress cascade) is the social-isolation defense scaled to a life. He leaves the city, the team, the relationship; he goes off-grid in *Occupy Avengers*, the New Mexico stretch, the Bed-Stuy retreat between Avengers tours. The function is twofold: remove himself from the audience whose disapproval he expects, and remove himself from relationships whose stability he cannot sustain. The defense is competent — he is good at being alone, has the skills for it, comes back functional — but the cost is the accumulated absence from any relational continuity that might actually heal him.

**Rationalization (Penitential).** Every difficult decision is framed retrospectively as *the right thing to do, done by the wrong man, who is therefore obligated to bear the cost.* Banner: *he asked me, I did it, I carry it.* Bobbi: *I held the line, the line was wrong, I should have folded.* Barney: *he's my brother, I owe him another chance.* The defense lets him act decisively in the moment by promising himself he will pay later, and he always pays later. The penitential frame converts moral injury into ongoing labor, which is workable but never finishes.

---

### 6.5 Mature Tier

**Sublimation — The Bow.** The archetypal mature defense, and Barton's most powerful one. Childhood violence, paternal abandonment, mentor betrayal, brother-rivalry, body-shame, class-rage, the constant low hum of inadequacy — all of it gets routed through the draw, the release, the impact. The bow does not merely express the material; it transforms it into a skill the world rewards, a craft a community honors, and a service that demonstrably saves lives. The transformation is real. He is a better man for having found it. He is also a man whose entire integrated self depends on a single channel of expression, and the day the rotator cuff finally goes is the day the defense system loses its keystone.

**Sublimation — The Building.** The Bed-Stuy apartment building is sublimation at a different scale: the displaced restoration of the childhood home he could not save. He is the landlord Harold was not, the protector Barney could not be, the adult presence Edith failed to provide. Every rent dispute settled, every leak fixed, every Tracksuit removed from the lobby is, at the unconscious level, a small repair to the Waverly house. The defense is mature because it produces real social good and because Clint has at least partial conscious access to it (he knows, dimly, why he bought the building); it is also why losing the building, or failing its tenants, wounds him out of proportion to the surface stakes.

**Altruism.** Distinguished from reaction formation by its generative quality. Reaction formation says *I will not be cruel because my father was cruel*; altruism says *I will be useful because usefulness is the form love takes when one cannot say it directly.* The mentorship of Kate Bishop is the cleanest example: not a substitute for therapy, not a re-parenting of the inner child by proxy (though it includes both), but a sustained, expensive, voluntary investment in another person's growth from which he derives meaning and through which he becomes incrementally healthier himself. The defense is mature, productive, and one of the genuinely load-bearing structures of his late-period functioning.

**Anticipation (Partial).** Limited capacity, present mostly in tactical and operational contexts. He plans ranges, contingencies, escape routes, gear failure modes with mature anticipatory discipline. He does not plan emotional contingencies at all. The defense is domain-restricted to combat and craft; it has not generalized to relational life, which is why he is repeatedly ambushed by entirely predictable emotional events (the anniversary, the brother's call, the breakup).

**Humor-as-Grace.** Distinct from humor-as-deflection (covered above). The rarer, later-developing capacity to make a joke that does not protect him but offers something to the other person — a small gift, a moment of relief in a hard room, a permission for someone else to laugh first. Most visible in the Kate scenes, in some late Cap exchanges, in occasional moments with civilians. It is the one defense that, when deployed, makes him and everyone around him healthier. He cannot do it on demand and he cannot do it for himself.

---

### 6.6 What Is Conspicuously Absent

A diagnostic catalogue of defenses Barton does *not* use is as informative as the inventory of those he does:

- **No projection of significance.** He does not assign his own faults to others. The internal verdict stays internal.
- **No grandiosity.** A true narcissistic structure would build a compensatory grandiose self; his compensation runs in the opposite direction, toward deflationary self-presentation.
- **No paranoid ideation.** Despite a life that would justify it, he does not generalize betrayal; each betrayer remains specifically themselves.
- **No moral licensing.** He does not use his good deeds to permit himself bad ones; the ledger does not net.
- **No splitting at the social-political level.** He does not bifurcate institutions or populations into all-good or all-bad; his anti-authoritarianism is granular and case-specific.
- **No fantasy-retreat.** He does not appear to maintain a rich inner fantasy life as compensation; the inner space is depicted as sparse, functional, and somewhat under-furnished, which is consistent with a system that has routed nearly all libidinal energy outward into craft and labor.

---

### 6.7 Failure Modes of the Defense System

The architecture has known failure points, repeatedly demonstrated in canon:

1. **Acute bereavement of a chosen-family figure** (Bobbi, Cap, near-Kate, near-dog). Collapses the humor and isolation defenses simultaneously; system reverts to acting-out and exile.
2. **Barney appearances.** Bypass the entire mature tier and reactivate the primitive splitting. He becomes, briefly, a child again, with a child's defenses.
3. **Loss of agency events** (mind control, coercion, sonic manipulation). Bypass every defense by removing the agent who deploys them. Recovery is slow and incomplete; each event raises baseline vigilance.
4. **Sincere assessment by a respected authority** — Cap saying *"you can do better,"* a doctor naming a diagnosis, Kate saying the thing he has avoided. Cuts under the humor and isolation tiers and lands directly on the internalized-Harold verdict. The defense against this is silence followed by exile.
5. **Cumulative load without action-outlet.** The defenses depend on a kinetic discharge channel. Bed rest, recovery periods, confinement, the rare quiet week — these are when the system runs hot without an exhaust valve and the depressive baseline surfaces undisguised. The Fraction run, structurally, is twenty-two issues of this condition.

---

### 6.8 Integrative Note

The defense system as a whole accomplishes the following: it permits a man who should not be functional to function at an elite operational level for forty years, while protecting his core decency from the cumulative trauma load that would, in most subjects, calcify into cruelty or collapse into incapacity. It does this at the cost of any sustained intimacy, any stable equilibrium, and any chance of actually metabolizing the underlying material. It is a high-performance, low-efficiency system: enormous fuel input, modest existential output, but the output is reliably ethical, which in his case is what was being optimized for.

He has not built defenses to feel better. He has built defenses to remain *good* under conditions that would not require him to be. By that metric — the only metric he has ever applied to himself — the architecture has succeeded, and he does not know it.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## Section 7 — Longitudinal Psychological Profile

A subject whose published record spans 1964 to the present, with internal continuity treating his career as roughly twenty in-universe years, permits the rarest of diagnostic luxuries: a long arc against which to test whether the personality has *moved* or merely *cycled*. The finding, summarized at the head and substantiated below, is that **Barton's psychological architecture has been remarkably stable in its deep structure and remarkably mobile in its surface presentation.** What changes decade to decade is the *register* of the defenses, the *targets* of the projections, and the *vocabulary* of the self-concept. What does not change is the substrate: the carnival-kid waiting for the next adult to leave, managing that expectation through humor and craft.

Frameworks applied throughout: Bowlby/Main attachment theory; Linehan's biosocial model of emotion dysregulation (applied carefully — he is *not* BPD but the affect-regulation vocabulary is useful); Beck's cognitive schemas; Janoff-Bulman on shattered assumptions; Litz et al. on moral injury; Herman on complex PTSD; the trauma-developmental literature of van der Kolk; and Erikson's stage model, used as a scaffolding device for what Barton skipped and what he is still trying to complete.

---

### Decade I — The Insubordinate Apprentice (early-career Avengers stratum, c. *Tales of Suspense* #57 through the late *Avengers* run of the original ongoing)

**Affect regulation.** Crude, reactive, externalizing. The dominant mode is *discharge* — anger and shame are not tolerated internally for more than seconds; they are converted into verbal provocation (toward Cap, toward Pietro, toward authority generally) or into kinetic action (the trick-shot showboating that recurs in this period as a tic). Erikson's framework places a healthy young adult at intimacy-vs-isolation; Barton is still litigating industry-vs-inferiority and identity-vs-role-confusion simultaneously, a developmental log-jam diagnostic of childhood adversity. His baseline arousal is elevated; his startle response, when depicted, is fast; his sleep, where shown in the Mansion, is brittle.

**Cognitive style.** Concrete-operational under stress, formal-operational at rest — meaning he solves problems brilliantly with hands and bow and ad-hoc tactics, but his abstractions about *himself* and his place are simplistic and binary: in/out, hero/crook, kept/abandoned. Beckian schemas already legible: **defectiveness/shame** ("they only let me in because Cap insisted"), **mistrust/abuse** (the Romanoff entanglement is the obvious instance; he reads betrayal into ambiguous behavior from teammates), and **unrelenting standards** projected outward as resentment of Cap's discipline while internally beginning to install that discipline as scaffolding.

**Self-concept.** Negative-stable with a thin compensatory veneer of bravado. The persistent boast-and-deflate rhythm — making a shot then making a joke about it — is the visible signature of someone who cannot let praise land because praise contradicts the schema. The "I'm the best marksman in the world" line, even when accurate, is *always* paired with a self-undercut. This is the first appearance of what becomes a lifelong pattern: praise must be neutralized within the same breath in which it arrives.

**What moves across this decade.** Cap's holding-the-line — *Avengers* #16 onward, but particularly across the early issues where the kooky quartet calcifies into a unit — does the developmental work that no prior adult performed. Slowly, fractionally, the testing-behavior recedes. By the late issues of this stratum he is *defending* Cap's authority to others rather than picking at it. This is the first observed internalization of a benign authority figure and the foundational event of his adult psychology. He acquires a superego on loan.

---

### Decade II — The Reluctant Lieutenant and Early-Marriage Years (the bridge between the Avengers ongoing and the West Coast founding, 1970s in publication, late-Decade-I to mid-Decade-II in-universe)

**Affect regulation.** Improving. The acquired superego is doing work. Discharge-via-provocation drops markedly; he is observably better at sitting with a teammate's anger without escalating. The humor matures: it shifts from defensive deflection toward affiliative humor — jokes that *include* rather than *fend off*. This is significant. Affiliative humor is correlated in the literature with better outcomes; defensive/self-deprecating humor is the marker of the underlying condition. Barton has both registers active in this period, and the affiliative one is genuinely new.

**Cognitive style.** Tactical thinking visibly broadens. He begins to plan in *minutes-to-hours* rather than seconds, and to think about teammates as instruments-with-personalities rather than as instruments. The Goliath stint — taking the size-changing serum — is psychologically diagnostic in another direction: when the bow is insufficient to keep his seat at the table, he *changes his body* rather than questioning the premise. The schema "I must be useful enough to deserve to be here" is so deep that he will accept somatic alteration before he will accept that his place is unconditional.

**Self-concept.** Begins splitting into a *public* Hawkeye (cocky, capable, indispensable) and a *private* Clint (still the carnival kid). The split, once formed, never closes. From here forward he will narrate his life in the third person to himself with disconcerting fluency, and the third-person Hawkeye will receive credit the first-person Clint refuses.

**Pair-bonding.** The Mockingbird courtship and marriage. The selection is diagnostic: she is *operationally* his peer, a trained agent, capable of meeting him as an equal, *and* she is a person constituted by secrets (S.H.I.E.L.D. background, compartmentalized history). Attachment theory predicts that a disorganized-anxious adult will select partners who reproduce the original ambivalence; Bobbi is warm and withholding simultaneously, and this is precisely the emotional climate of childhood. He marries the weather he grew up in and calls it weather.

---

### Decade III — The West Coast Years (1984–1989 publication; mid-career in-universe)

**Affect regulation.** This is the high-water mark. Across the West Coast Avengers run he is the most regulated he will ever be on record. He sleeps. He runs a team. He convenes meetings. He mediates Wonder Man's neuroses and Tigra's identity collapse and USAgent's hostility without escalating any of them. The capacity is real; the question is what it costs and why it does not last.

**Cognitive style.** Demonstrably executive. Strategic planning over weeks; resource allocation; personnel judgment; the willingness to delegate (the surest sign of an adult ego). The "dumb archer" framing is not merely wrong in this period — it is *contradicted weekly* by his own behavior. Yet he never updates the self-concept to match the evidence. This is the central cognitive pathology of his life: **a chronic refusal to incorporate disconfirming evidence about the self.** Beck would call it a stuck schema; the trauma literature would call it the persistence of the internal working model formed before language.

**Self-concept.** A brief, partial, unstable elevation. He is *Chairman Barton*. He occasionally lets himself believe it. The signs of strain, however, accumulate: he overworks; he micromanages where micromanagement is unnecessary; he is unable to accept compliments from Bobbi without converting them to jokes. The schema is being pressured but not revised.

**Pair-bond collapse — the Phantom Rider sequence.** The diagnostic moment of his entire adult life. Bobbi, sexually assaulted and psychologically tortured by the Rider, kills him (or allows him to die) and conceals it. Clint discovers it and chooses the *rule* over the *wife*. This is **moral rigidity as defense** — and the defense is against precisely the kind of moral ambiguity his childhood trained him to find unbearable. If he allows that the people he loves can do unforgivable things and remain loved, the entire architecture by which he forgives Barney, forgives Natasha-the-spy, forgives himself, collapses. He must be a hard-line moralist *with her* in order to remain a soft-line moralist *with himself*. The schema is protected at the cost of the marriage, and the cost is enormous and he knows it. The reservoir of guilt opened here never empties.

**End of decade.** West Coast disbands. Bobbi dies in his arms (in-universe c. *AWC* #100). He is for the first time confronted with a loss whose moral weight he cannot offload onto fate. The regression that follows is sharp.

---

### Decade IV — Itinerancy, Death, and Resurrection (1990s into the *Disassembled*/*House of M* axis)

**Affect regulation.** Decompensates. The acquired regulation of the West Coast years was *role-scaffolded* — the chairmanship held him as much as he held it. Without the role, the dysthymic baseline reasserts. The 1990s solo and team appearances show a Barton who is more openly bitter, whose humor has tipped back toward the defensive register, and whose pattern of geographic exile begins in earnest: Thunderbolts leadership (notable for the *type* of charge he takes on — reformed villains, a population that maps onto his own carnival-criminal origin), then drift.

**Cognitive style.** Narrows. Strategic thinking remains intact in combat but his *life-planning* horizon contracts to weeks. The foreshortened-future criterion of PTSD becomes overtly verbalized in this stratum: variants of "I'm not gonna make it to 40" begin to appear and never stop appearing.

**Self-concept.** Re-darkens. The Bobbi loss is processed badly because he refuses to process it at all; the avoidance criterion of PTSD is met behaviorally — he avoids the West Coast as a geography, avoids reunions, avoids the topic in conversation, redirects via humor with measurable latency drops (the joke arrives faster, which in his behavioral grammar means the pain is closer).

**Death (*Avengers* #500/Disassembled).** The detonation of his own quiver is the most psychologically over-determined act of his career and must be read precisely. It is heroic; it is also the cleanest possible enactment of the **earn-the-right-to-be-here** master motive. Given a choice between living-with-loss and dying-usefully, he chose dying-usefully in under a second. This is not suicidality in the clinical sense — it is the *operationalized* form of a lifelong cognitive distortion: that his value is his utility and that his utility is best demonstrated by its terminal expenditure.

**Resurrection (*House of M*).** And here is the data point canon does not metabolize and which therefore Barton must metabolize alone: **he returned, and the world had reassigned his place.** The Eriksonian crisis this triggers is sui generis — there is no stage for *re-entering a life after one has been concluded*. Janoff-Bulman's shattered-assumptions framework is the closest fit: the assumption that *one's existence is continuous* is among the most foundational, and its disruption produces a destabilization the literature has not had occasion to name. He responds with the Ronin identity — the masterless samurai, the *chosen* effacement — which is a creative and revealing solution: rather than try to reclaim Hawkeye, he becomes a *placeholder* identity, performing competence without claiming personhood. He is, for this period, deliberately a function rather than a man.

---

### Decade V — The Bed-Stuy Episode (Fraction/Aja stratum and its surround)

**Affect regulation.** Visibly impaired across a 22-issue depressive episode that the man himself would never name. The somatic presentation is textbook: anhedonia (archery itself becomes joyless or compulsive depending on the day), psychomotor variability (long couch-immobility punctuated by impulsive prosocial sprints), appetite dysregulation (the pizza-as-baseline), sleep destruction, social withdrawal interrupted by *over-extension* toward strangers — the apartment building tenants, the dog, Grills, the women who pass through. The over-extension is itself a defense: helping others is a permitted form of self-care because it does not require the schema-violating step of believing oneself worth helping.

**Cognitive style.** Splits more sharply than ever. *Operational* cognition remains elite — the tracksuit operations are tactically clean, the rooftop sequences show preserved spatial reasoning under fatigue, his improvisation with arrows is at career best. *Self-referential* cognition deteriorates markedly. His internal monologue, when accessible, is a near-uninterrupted stream of self-diminishment, future-foreshortening, and pre-emptive apology. This is the **dorsal-vs-default-mode dissociation** that the trauma literature has begun to characterize: the action-system stays online while the self-narrative-system corrodes, and the subject functions by living in the former and renting out the latter.

**Self-concept.** The Bed-Stuy period clarifies the lifelong pattern: the schema "I am the screw-up" is now so practiced that it functions as a *prediction engine*. He pre-formulates failure and acts in ways that make failure likely, which then confirms the schema, which then earns him the small relief of having been right. Karen Horney would call this the "tyranny of the should" inverted — the tyranny of the will-have-failed.

**The hearing-loss arc.** The progressive sensorineural loss returns and is, this time, *attended to* — hearing aids, ASL acquisition, occasional disclosure. This is a small, real piece of psychological forward motion. He is forty-plus years late to seeking help and the help in question is audiological, but the precedent — *Clint Barton accepts that something is wrong with him and accepts a tool for it* — matters. The *Hawkeye* #19 issue (the barn, the ASL sequences, Barney returned and wheelchair-bound) is the only published instance of his sitting with childhood material in something like real time rather than via reenactment. He does not resolve it. But he is in the room with it, which is more than he has previously managed.

**Kate Bishop.** The single most therapeutically significant relationship of his adult life, and the only one in which his schema is *successfully challenged* without his fleeing. Why it works: she is structurally his apprentice, which permits him to invest without claiming peer status (no lateral vulnerability); she is young enough to be unambiguously not-a-romantic-object, which removes the entire Mockingbird/Romanoff template from play; and she insists on *seeing* him without requiring him to be seen-and-loved in the romantic mode that he cannot tolerate. Mentorship is the one relational frame in which his counter-dependence and his hunger for connection are not in conflict. He gives to her what he was not given. The act of giving, repeated, repairs a small portion of the substrate. Not enough; not nothing.

---

### Decade VI — Penitential Maturity (post-Fraction through *Civil War II*, *Occupy Avengers*, *Tales of Suspense*, *Freefall*, and the present)

**Affect regulation.** Mixed and meaningful. The Banner killing during *Civil War II* introduces a category of distress that exceeds his existing defensive repertoire: **moral injury** in the Litz sense — a transgression (committed, even if consented to in advance) against deeply held moral convictions, in a context that did not absolve and could not absolve. PTSD frameworks alone underfit the presentation; the moral-injury construct fits the data — the guilt-shame complex, the spiritual/meaning disruption ("what kind of man does this even when asked"), the alienation from peer community, the difficulty accepting the legal acquittal. He is more openly dysphoric in this period than in any prior, *and also* more openly seeking — the *Occupy Avengers* itinerancy reads less as exile-as-avoidance (its prior function) and more as exile-as-pilgrimage. There is a fractional shift toward *meaning-seeking* rather than pure escape.

**Cognitive style.** The first signs of integrative work. The *Tales of Suspense* arc with Bucky places him in functional partnership with another man whose biography is built from coercion, mind-control, and moral injury — and the partnership *works*, in part because each can speak the other's grammar without translation. Barton's capacity to sit with another damaged man as a peer rather than as either student or teacher is new in his record and constitutes the first credible move toward Eriksonian intimacy in lateral form. The *Freefall* arc shows the older negative patterns intact — the going-dark, the framing-it-as-the-plan, the stupid risk — but with a difference: he is now visibly aware that the pattern is a pattern. Insight is partial, not transformative, but is present.

**Self-concept.** Still negative-stable, still organized around the carnival-kid template, but with a new register: **the elder.** He has begun, in this decade, to occupy the role he previously envied — the steady older figure for younger heroes. He does it badly in patches and well in others, and what is significant is that he is willing to do it at all. To be the steady older figure requires implicitly granting oneself the status of *having survived* — which contradicts the foreshortened-future cognition. The contradiction is not resolved; both run in parallel; but the elder-role is doing slow corrective work on the schema simply by accumulating evidence against it.

**Hearing loss, chronicity, the body.** He is by this point a man whose body is a record of his choices. The hearing aids are normalized. ASL is fluent. The accumulated musculoskeletal damage is managed by stubbornness more than by medicine. He has begun, in late-stratum appearances, to comment on his own aging with something other than the foreshortened-future joke — a small but real shift toward *temporal continuity* in self-narrative.

---

### Cross-Decade Synthesis

**What has not changed.** The core schemas — defectiveness/shame, mistrust/abuse, unrelenting standards, abandonment — installed before age twelve and never substantively revised. The master motive: earn-the-right-to-be-here. The defensive stack: humor, action-as-avoidance, counter-dependence, in that order. The escalation cycle, run six-plus times: humor sharpens → withdrawal into task → stupid risk → exile → return as if resolved.

**What has changed.** The *register* of the humor has matured (more affiliative, less purely defensive, though both remain). The *targets* of projection have softened (less authority-baiting, more situational). The *accessibility* of his own pain has increased — he can now sometimes name it, where for two decades he could only enact it. The *relational repertoire* has broadened from the early near-exclusive Cap-and-romantic-partner template to include mentorship (Kate), lateral peer-with-damage (Bucky), and quasi-paternal relations with civilians. The *willingness to accept tools* — hearing aids, ASL, the occasional therapist-coded conversation — exists where it once did not.

**What is moving but not finished.** Mourning. Bobbi, Cap-deaths-and-returns, his own death-and-return, Banner, Barney's serial losses, the apartment-building neighbors he could not all save — none of these has been completed in the Worden/Kübler sense. They are held in suspension by the action-defense and discharged in fragments through the exile cycles. The total psychic load is enormous and the metabolic rate is slow. He will, on present trajectory, die having processed perhaps forty percent of it.

**Prognostic note.** The trajectory is, against expectation, *modestly* hopeful. Six decades of published behavior show a man whose deep structure has not changed and whose surface presentation has, slowly, *softened* — fewer enactments per unit grief, more language per unit pain, more sustained mentorship, more tolerance for being seen. He will not become someone else. He will become, by small increments, a slightly more bearable version of who he has always been. Given the substrate, this is not a small achievement, and the file should record it as such.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS

## Preamble & Methodological Note

What follows is a formal psychiatric formulation derived from six decades of observed behavior, depicted internal monologue (where canon provides it), corroborating accounts by close associates (Romanoff, Morse, Rogers, Bishop, Pym, Wanda Maximoff, and Barney Barton), and the medical record reconstructed in Section 2. The subject has never voluntarily sought psychiatric care. He has been *informally assessed* by Dr. Leonard Samson at least once, evaluated peripherally during Avengers medical clearances, and pressured toward therapy by Bobbi Morse during their marriage and by Kate Bishop more recently — every attempt has been deflected with the characteristic humor stack. The diagnostic picture is therefore inferred from behavior, not self-report, and the inference is high-confidence precisely *because* the behaviors are so consistent across decades, writers, and contexts.

Diagnostic codes are DSM-5-TR/ICD-11 analogs. Where the construct is contested or the presentation is subthreshold, that is noted.

---

## I. PRIMARY DIAGNOSES

### 1. Persistent Depressive Disorder (Dysthymia) with Intermittent Major Depressive Episodes
**DSM-5-TR 300.4 / ICD-11 6A72**, with anxious distress, with atypical features (mood reactivity, leaden fatigue under interpersonal rejection), with peripartum-equivalent worsening following losses.

**Symptom mapping to longitudinal behavior:**

- *Depressed mood, most of the day, more days than not, for years.* The dysthymic baseline is present from his earliest solo material. He does not have a non-depressed register; he has *managed* and *unmanaged* presentations. The "managed" version is the wisecracking field operative; the "unmanaged" version is the Bed-Stuy couch.
- *Poor appetite or overeating.* Comfort-eating depicted obsessively in late-period material — pizza consumption to the level of running joke, which is the form pathology takes when one is a man like Barton (it becomes a bit so it doesn't have to become a problem).
- *Insomnia or hypersomnia.* Both, alternating. Combat-zone hyperarousal insomnia in field deployments; depressive hypersomnia and circadian collapse in interstitial periods.
- *Low energy / fatigue.* Masked by adrenaline during active operations; unmasked between them. Multiple depictions of him unable to get off a couch for an entire day except to refill coffee.
- *Low self-esteem.* This is the cardinal feature and it is profound. See Section 3 on self-concept. He does not have low self-esteem the way ordinary depressives have low self-esteem; he has a structurally negative self-concept that has been *stable for forty years*.
- *Poor concentration / difficulty making decisions.* Selective. His tactical decision-making is intact under fire. His *life-decision* paralysis — about relationships, about retirement, about treatment, about his brother — is severe.
- *Feelings of hopelessness.* The "I'm not gonna make it to forty" beat, the foreshortened-future cognitions, the recurring sense that the next mission is the last one. He plans, but he does not plan *for himself*.

**Major Depressive Episodes** punctuate the dysthymia, triggered by discrete losses: post-Bobbi (1993), post-Disassembled return (2006-07), the Fraction-era apartment-building period (clinically frank MDE in 2012-2014), post-Banner (2016 onward), each *Hawkeye: Freefall*-adjacent exile. The pattern is reactive depression layered on a dysthymic substrate — what older clinical literature called *double depression*, and what the current framework would code as PDD with intermittent MDE.

**Etiology.** Compounded. Genetic loading from at least one alcoholic parent (probable mood disorder underneath Harold Barton's drinking, given the violence pattern). Adverse childhood experiences at near-ceiling load (physical abuse, neglect, parental death, sibling violence, sequential mentor abuse). Adult bereavement repeated. Occupational trauma cumulative. Two failed pair-bonds. Documented death and resurrection — which, whatever its metaphysics, functions experientially as a profound disruption of self-continuity. The wonder is not that he is depressed; the wonder is that he is functional.

---

### 2. Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder, Chronic, with Complex Features
**DSM-5-TR 309.81 / ICD-11 6B41 Complex PTSD**.

I am coding this as **C-PTSD** rather than single-event PTSD because the diagnostic criteria for complex presentation are met in full: the trauma is **prolonged, repeated, and occurred under conditions of captive dependency** (the childhood with Harold; the carnival years with Swordsman and Trick Shot, where he was a minor with no exit); and the three additional ICD-11 C-PTSD criteria are all present:

- *Affective dysregulation* — see Section 3, particularly the inverse pattern (regulated in combat, dysregulated in intimacy).
- *Negative self-concept* — pervasive, stable, the master feature.
- *Interpersonal disturbance* — the warm-front/walled-core pattern, the inability to sustain lateral peer intimacy.

**Standard PTSD criteria mapping:**

- *Criterion A (exposure).* Overdetermined. Childhood physical abuse; witnessing parental violence; parental death; serial mentor betrayal and one near-fatal beating by Swordsman; multiple combat exposures with serious injury and threat to life; killing in the line of duty (the Banner act especially); witnessing the death of his wife in his arms.
- *Criterion B (intrusion).* Nightmares depicted, particularly around Bobbi and around Banner. Intrusive imagery triggered by environmental cues (carnival imagery, certain Russian-language cues post-Romanoff and post-tracksuits, the sound of his own bowstring under fatigue). Dissociative flashback episodes — brief, controlled, but present.
- *Criterion C (avoidance).* Geographic (the recurrent exile pattern is partly avoidance behavior dressed as penance). Relational (the "goes dark" cycle). Cognitive (refuses to discuss Bobbi for years at a stretch; the Banner killing he discusses only when forced).
- *Criterion D (negative alterations in cognition/mood).* Persistent negative beliefs about self ("I'm the screw-up"); distorted blame (assumes causal responsibility for outcomes he did not control — Barney's choices, Bobbi's decisions, Banner's biology); persistent fear/horror/guilt; markedly diminished interest in significant activities during episodes; feelings of detachment; persistent inability to experience positive emotions outside of mentorship contexts.
- *Criterion E (arousal/reactivity).* Hypervigilance — contextual, professionally calibrated, but elevated. Exaggerated startle in fatigue states. Sleep disturbance. Reckless and self-destructive behavior — the "takes a stupid risk, gets hurt, frames it as the plan" pattern is textbook PTSD-criterion-E self-destructive behavior, and it is the single most consistent diagnostic marker across his published life.

**Course.** Chronic, with acute exacerbations following each major loss. Never been in formal trauma-focused treatment. Self-managed via humor, action, and the chosen-family compensations. Partial spontaneous remission impossible because the precipitants keep recurring.

---

### 3. Moral Injury (Non-DSM Construct, Diagnostically Critical)
Not a DSM diagnosis but increasingly recognized in trauma and military-psychiatric literature (Litz, Shay) as a distinct construct from PTSD, characterized by **acts of commission, omission, or witness that violate deeply held moral beliefs**, producing guilt, shame, and a fractured self-concept that pure PTSD frameworks fail to capture.

For Barton this is the more accurate construct for several specific events:

- **The Banner killing (*Civil War II*, 2016).** Pre-consented, tactically defensible, legally acquitted — and morally unmetabolized. He killed a man at that man's request and the system told him he had done nothing wrong, and the moral injury is precisely *that the verdict did not match the felt fact*. He killed Bruce. The acquittal did not absolve him because he never believed he needed an acquittal — he believed he needed to have not done it.
- **The Phantom Rider aftermath.** He drove Bobbi out for upholding a moral standard he now believes was wrong. The injury here is one of moral *rigidity in retrospect* — having been the instrument of his own loss by his own ethical principle. This is the rarest form of moral injury and the hardest to treat.
- **Aggregate civilian collaterals** across decades of Avengers work. He keeps the count. Other Avengers do not.

Moral injury presents *as* depression and PTSD but does not respond fully to treatment for either, because the wound is to **meaning**, not to fear-conditioning or affect regulation. This explains why Barton's pattern has not improved despite the natural protective factors he has (chosen family, craft mastery, mentorship outlets): the substrate keeps generating new moral injuries faster than the protective factors can metabolize them.

---

## II. SECONDARY / SUBTHRESHOLD CONSIDERATIONS

### 4. Adjustment Disorder, Recurrent — particularly post-resurrection and post-hearing-loss
The *Disassembled*/*House of M* return generated what would be coded as Adjustment Disorder with mixed anxiety and depressed mood: he came back to a world that had grieved him and re-equilibrated, and he had no scripted role in the new arrangement. The Ronin period is the adjustment-disorder behavior — a man trying on a new identity because the old one no longer fit the slot the world had left for him.

Progressive sensorineural hearing loss has generated a parallel adjustment process, handled with characteristic deflection (the hearing aids as accessory, the ASL as cool-skill rather than accommodation), but the disability-identity work is real and ongoing.

### 5. Bereavement, Prolonged Grief Disorder (DSM-5-TR 309.89 / ICD-11 6B42), Bobbi-specific
The Bobbi grief has the hallmarks of Prolonged Grief Disorder: persistent yearning more than twelve months post-loss (and persisting after her resurrection, because the *original* loss was never resolved and the returned Bobbi is not the lost Bobbi to his nervous system), intense emotional pain on cues, avoidance of reminders, identity disruption ("I was her husband" remains an active self-statement long after the role has ended). The fact that she returned alive complicates the grief without resolving it — he is grieving a marriage that he killed, not a wife who died.

### 6. Insomnia Disorder, comorbid
Independent diagnostic significance beyond the depression/PTSD contributions. Sleep architecture almost certainly disrupted; this feeds back into mood, concentration, and injury recovery.

---

## III. RIGOROUS DIFFERENTIAL — WHAT HE IS NOT

A correct diagnostic file is defined as much by what it rules out as by what it includes. The following are conditions that surface-read of Barton's behavior could suggest, and which the longitudinal record specifically does *not* support.

### NOT — Antisocial Personality Disorder
Surface cues: criminal origin, carnival background, recurring brushes with law enforcement, "Ronin" period operating outside sanction, comfort with violence, willingness to kill (Banner).

Why not: ASPD requires a pervasive pattern of disregard for the rights of others, with conduct disorder before age 15. Barton's conduct-disorder history is plausibly present in adolescence, satisfying that criterion. *Every other criterion fails.* He has a hyperactive conscience, not a deficient one — his entire adult life is structured around restitution and protection. His remorse for harms done (including ones he did not actually cause) is excessive, not absent. He is not deceitful as a personality trait — he is one of the more bluntly honest Avengers, sometimes self-destructively so. He does not exploit others; he over-extends himself for others, including strangers. The diagnostic core of ASPD — *the absence of empathic and moral response* — is the precise *inverse* of Barton's presentation. He is, if anything, *over*-empathic and morally hyper-responsive. ASPD: ruled out with high confidence.

### NOT — Borderline Personality Disorder
Surface cues: abandonment sensitivity, intense and unstable relationships (Romanoff, Mockingbird), affective lability, impulsivity, recurrent risk-taking and self-injurious behavior, identity questions (the Ronin phase).

Why not: BPD requires *identity disturbance* — a markedly and persistently unstable self-image. Barton's self-image is **painfully, structurally stable** — it is just stably negative. A borderline patient asks "who am I?"; Barton has known who he is since he was twelve, and the answer is "the screw-up," and that answer does not waver across forty years of evidence to the contrary. His impulsivity is not diffuse across multiple life domains — it is *task-channeled* into combat improvisation. He does not have stress-related transient dissociative or paranoid symptoms in the BPD pattern. He has long-term, stable, intense attachments (Cap, Kate, the Avengers institution) — the BPD pattern of cycling idealization/devaluation is not present; what looks like cycling in his marriages is *consistent moral evaluation under changing facts*. The differential matters because the treatment implications differ: BPD-frame would push DBT and mentalization work; the correct frame — C-PTSD with depression — pushes trauma-focused therapy, grief work, and moral-injury-specific interventions.

### NOT — Substance Use Disorder
Surface cues: parental alcoholism, elevated drinking in some periods, coffee dependency, the carnival-world background.

Why not: he has the genetic loading and the environmental priming for an SUD and *does not have one*. This is itself a diagnostic finding — the **vigilant abstinence pattern**. He monitors his drinking with the precision of a man who has read the actuarial tables on himself. He does not progress through tolerance escalation. He does not lose work or relationships to substance use. He has never been depicted in withdrawal. The caffeine dependency is real and clinically uninteresting at his exposure level (occupational hazard for any operator). His self-medication is *behavioral* — work, action, isolation — not chemical. The negative diagnosis is important because clinicians seeing the family history routinely overdiagnose SUD in adult children of alcoholics; Barton is the case where it would be wrong.

### NOT — Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder
Surface cues: the carnival-kid scatter, the wisecracking interruption pattern, the apparent difficulty with sustained focus on administrative tasks, the leaving-things-half-done quality of his off-duty life.

Why not: ADHD requires the attentional dysfunction to be *pervasive across settings*. Barton's attentional capacity for craft — archery, target acquisition, tactical scanning, complex multi-target sequencing — is **elite and sustained over hours**. He can hold a draw and a sight picture for periods that would defeat most neurotypicals. The scatter is not attentional; it is *affective* — he disengages from administrative and domestic tasks because they generate dysphoria and there is no adaptive challenge to anchor him. This is depression's anhedonia masquerading as attention deficit, and the distinction matters because stimulant treatment would worsen his hyperarousal and sleep without addressing the underlying problem.

### NOT — Narcissistic Personality Disorder
Surface cues: the public persona, the bravado, the catchphrases, the "world's greatest marksman" claim, the high-profile career, the recurring conflict with authority figures.

Why not: NPD requires a *grandiose* self-concept (or, in vulnerable NPD, a defensively grandiose one masking shame). Barton's bravado is not grandiose; it is **performatively self-deprecating with a defensive overlay**. A narcissist could not voluntarily adopt the "carnie kid on a team of gods" framing — it would be intolerable to the structure. Barton *insists* on it. He under-claims credit, over-claims fault, and routinely positions himself as the least of the Avengers. The vulnerable-narcissism reading is closer but still fails: vulnerable narcissists harbor *entitled* resentment about not being recognized; Barton harbors *guilty* resentment about being recognized too much. The distinction is between "I deserve more than I'm getting" (NPD) and "I'm getting more than I deserve" (Barton). These are inverse structures.

### NOT — Bipolar Disorder
Surface cues: the energy-state oscillation between Avengers-mode hyperfunctioning and interstitial collapse, the impulsive risk-taking, the "goes dark for months" pattern that could superficially resemble depressive episodes between hypomanic ones.

Why not: the high-energy state is *situational and externally cued* (mission deployment, crisis), not endogenous. There is no depicted decreased need for sleep with sustained euphoria; no pressured speech beyond his baseline verbal style; no flight of ideas; no grandiosity (see above); no spending sprees or sexual indiscretion patterns characteristic of mania. The mood floor is dysthymic-stable, not bipolar-cyclical. Pseudo-cycling driven by the operational tempo of his job is not bipolarity.

### NOT — Schizoid or Avoidant Personality Disorder
Surface cues: the exile pattern, the withdrawal from team contexts, the preference for solo work, the difficulty with intimate relationships.

Why not: schizoid requires *absence of desire* for close relationships; Barton's withdrawals are *defended retreats from desired relationships*, which is the opposite pattern. Avoidant requires pervasive social inhibition and feelings of inadequacy with fear of rejection driving social avoidance; Barton is socially confident in low-stakes contact (bantering with neighbors, kids, strangers) and only avoidant in high-stakes intimate contexts — which is the trauma pattern, not the personality-disorder pattern. The diagnosis to use here is C-PTSD's interpersonal-disturbance criterion, not a separate Axis-II construct.

### NOT — Obsessive-Compulsive Personality Disorder
Surface cues: the moral rigidity (Phantom Rider incident), the craft perfectionism, the discipline of his training regimen.

Why not: OCPD requires *pervasive* preoccupation with orderliness, perfectionism, and control across life domains. Barton's life domains outside the bow are conspicuously *disordered* — his apartment, his finances, his relationships, his medical care. The perfectionism is craft-bounded; the moral rigidity is episodic (and he himself recognizes it as a flaw, which an OCPD patient typically does not). The right frame is high-skill professional discipline coexisting with depressive disorganization, not OCPD.

### NOT — Acquired Brain Injury / CTE-Spectrum Cognitive Disorder
Surface cues: extensive head-trauma history across decades of combat, plausible occupational exposure at CTE-relevant levels, some depicted irritability and mood lability.

Why not — *yet*: there is no current evidence of progressive cognitive decline. Memory intact, executive function intact under load, tactical processing elite. The irritability and mood lability are fully accounted for by the affective and trauma diagnoses. *However*, this is the diagnosis to monitor longitudinally — the cumulative exposure is real and the natural history of repeated mild TBI in combatants is increasingly clear. Recommend serial neuropsychological screening; recommend he stop taking head shots; recommend he will not stop taking head shots.

---

## IV. COMORBIDITY MAP

The diagnoses listed are not parallel; they are **structurally entangled** in a specific pattern:

- The childhood adversity produced the C-PTSD substrate, which produced the negative self-concept, which produced the dysthymic baseline.
- The dysthymic baseline shaped his vocational and relational choices toward high-risk/high-loss configurations, which generated repeated discrete traumas (Bobbi, Banner, his own death), which generated the MDE overlays and the moral-injury wounds.
- The moral injuries and unresolved griefs *reinforce* the negative self-concept, *deepen* the dysthymia, and *fuel* the avoidance behavior, which prevents the corrective experiences (treatment, sustained intimacy, integration of loss) that would interrupt the cycle.
- The protective factors (mentorship, craft, Cap-internalized superego, Kate Bishop) hold him at the current equilibrium but do not advance him out of it.

This is a stable, self-reinforcing pathology. It will not spontaneously remit. It has not, in forty years of opportunity.

---

## V. COURSE & PROGNOSIS

**Course to date.** Chronic, stable, episodically exacerbated, never treated. He has not deteriorated, which under his trauma load is itself remarkable and speaks to substantial intrinsic resilience plus the protective effect of his chosen-family and craft anchors. He has not improved.

**Without intervention.** Continued cycling at current amplitude. Probability of an additional major loss event in any given decade approaches certainty given his occupation; each will generate a new MDE overlay and likely a new moral injury. Cumulative physical degradation will eventually force a vocational transition he is psychologically unprepared for, which is the highest-risk inflection point in his foreseeable future. Suicide risk: **chronically elevated, acutely low** — he has the access, the means competence, and the foreshortened-future cognitions, but he has strong protective factors (Kate, internalized Cap, the protective-of-others drive, and a stubborn working-class refusal to "take the easy way"). Risk would spike if Kate were lost, if Cap were definitively lost, or if he sustained a disabling injury that removed the craft anchor.

**With intervention (hypothetical).** Highly treatable in principle. The negative self-concept is the rate-limiting target; trauma-focused therapy (EMDR, prolonged exposure, or written-narrative protocols) for the discrete events; grief work specifically around Bobbi (the marriage, not the woman); moral-injury-specific intervention (adaptive disclosure, forgiveness work) for Banner and the Phantom Rider aftermath; behavioral activation for the dysthymic floor; couples or family work if any current pair-bond exists. Pharmacology: an SSRI would likely help the dysthymic baseline and the PTSD arousal cluster; he would refuse it; if accepted, would need monitoring for the rare disinhibition reactions in a man whose occupation involves weapons. Disability-adjustment counseling around the hearing loss, framed as accommodation rather than deficit, would likely be accepted from the right clinician.

**Engagement probability.** Low without a precipitating crisis or sustained


## Behavioral Atlas

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## SECTION 6 — BEHAVIORAL ATLAS

A longitudinal catalog of observable behaviors, motor habits, verbal patterns, and decision routines, conditioned on environmental and affective state. Tells are sorted by reliability — those marked **[high-confidence]** appear across at least four distinct canonical runs and decades; **[medium]** across two to three; **[contextual]** in specific recurring conditions. The goal is the granular resolution at which a competent adversary could predict him within ninety seconds of observation, and at which a competent friend could intervene before Stage 3 of his stress cycle.

---

### 6.1 BASELINE / CALM (Low-Stakes Operational)

**Postural baseline.** Stands with weight on his back foot, knees soft, never fully locked — the archer's address-position relaxed into a habit so deep it persists in line at a coffee counter [high-confidence]. Shoulders slightly forward, the rounded set of a man who has drawn between 70 and 100 pounds of weight tens of thousands of times. When standing in conversation he angles his body 15–20° off-square from his interlocutor — a sight-line habit, never head-on, always with a foot of escape pocketed.

**Hand habits.** Right hand drifts to the back of his neck when thinking [high-confidence]; left hand fidgets — keys, a coin, a spare fletching, the tab of a soda can torn off and folded. He almost never has empty hands. Fraction's run is built around this: the panel-after-panel of him rotating a coffee cup, a roll of tape, a beer cap.

**Speech baseline.** Loose, declarative, contraction-heavy, Midwestern flat-A surviving under thirty years of New York overlay. Sentence fragments. Drops the subject pronoun ("Gonna grab coffee." "Took the shot."). Profanity moderate and deployed for rhythm rather than emphasis. Calls people by surname ("Romanoff," "Rogers," "Stark") when calm; by first name when stressed or affectionate — *inversion of normal civilian pattern*, diagnostic.

**Eye behavior.** Constantly mapping. Scans a room on entry in a fixed sequence: exits first, elevations second, hands of present persons third, faces last [high-confidence]. The face-last sequencing is socially noticeable to anyone watching for it — it reads as inattentive or rude until you understand he has already inventoried what could kill you both.

**Caffeine ritual.** Coffee black, occasionally with sugar he denies adding. Drinks it past lukewarm, never reheats. Owns at least one mug with a chip in it that he refuses to throw out. Will buy a second coffee within thirty minutes of finishing the first if circumstance permits.

**Ambient ASL.** Post-hearing-loss baseline: signs to himself when no one is watching — counts arrows in inventory, mutters grocery lists in one-handed sign, taps fingers in what reads as idle fidget but is actually rehearsed fingerspelling [contextual, Fraction-era and after]. Hearing aids in or out is a tell — out means he wants the world quieter than it is; in means he is expecting to need to negotiate.

**Domestic micro-habits.** Leaves dishes. Does laundry in catastrophic batches. Tapes things — broken mug handles, ripped jacket cuffs, a cracked window — rather than replacing or properly repairing. The tape on the bridge of his nose across Fraction's run is the public version of an entire interior philosophy: *adequate, ongoing, non-permanent.* His apartment is organized around sight-lines to the door and weapons-cached at three concealed points minimum.

**Animal handling.** Dogs first, before people. Will greet a dog by name and the owner by gesture. The Pizza Dog relationship is not eccentricity; it is the cleanest attachment in his adult life, because a dog cannot leave him by choice and cannot be disappointed by him in any way he is required to articulate.

---

### 6.2 LOW-LEVEL STRESS (Bureaucratic, Social, Interpersonal Friction)

**Verbal escalation Stage 1.** Humor rate increases by an order of magnitude. Jokes become specifically self-deprecating — *"Yeah, well, I'm the guy who shoots sticks, what do I know"* — and the self-deprecation is calibrated to extract the laugh that ends the inquiry. The reliable indicator is **the joke that arrives before the question is finished**; he is intercepting, not responding.

**Eye-contact pattern.** Drops by roughly half. Looks at hands, at the middle distance, at his own coffee, at any nearby dog. Will look at Cap. Will not look at a therapist, an authority figure conducting an interview, or a romantic partner asking a direct emotional question.

**Posture.** Shoulders rise; the rounded archer's set tightens. He will lean a hip against any available vertical surface — wall, doorframe, kitchen island. The lean is load-bearing in a way that suggests his lower back is in chronic complaint. Crosses arms only when consciously performing defiance; uncrossed-but-occupied (holding a cup, a pen) is his real defensive posture.

**Decision tendency.** Will agree to the smaller of two asks to avoid the larger conversation. Will volunteer for the inconvenient task to short-circuit being assigned the painful one. This is exploitable and has been exploited (Fury, Stark, Maria Hill have all used it; Cap has, to his credit, mostly declined to).

**Tell-of-tells.** Pulls his lower lip between his teeth and releases it slowly [high-confidence]. Touches the bridge of his nose where the tape goes or went. Adjusts a hearing aid that does not need adjusting.

---

### 6.3 ELEVATED STRESS (Mission Pressure, Team Conflict, Bad News Incoming)

**Verbal Stage 2.** Humor goes pointed. The self-deprecation curdles into deprecation of the situation, then of the people in the room. Sarcasm becomes a load-bearing structural element of his sentences. He will pick the most powerful person present and needle them specifically — historically Tony, Pietro, Wonder Man, USAgent, lately Sam — testing whether they will hit him, leave, or hold the line. This is a direct reenactment of the childhood-to-Cap arc, and he does not know he is doing it. It runs hot for about ninety seconds, then he course-corrects with a self-aimed joke as olive branch.

**Motor change.** Begins manipulating arrows or arrow components if any are within reach — checking fletching, rotating a shaft between thumb and forefinger, dry-nocking and releasing without a bow. If no archery materials are present, substitutes any small object capable of fine motor handling: pen disassembly, coin walk across knuckles, peeling a label off a bottle in one strip. **The strip-peeling is a high-confidence tell of his mid-stress range.** The label comes off whole or he restarts.

**Decision tendency.** Begins withdrawing from group decisions while remaining physically present. Voice drops in volume but not in frequency of speech; he keeps talking, but the talk gets quieter and more clipped, and he begins to defer to whoever is willing to take the call. Reserves his actual judgment for execution.

**Sleep collapse.** Within 48 hours of an elevated-stress state persisting, his sleep architecture goes. He naps on couches in 90-minute blocks, eats at random hours, and runs on coffee and stubbornness. He has done this for so long that his body has adapted to it as a load state; the cost is paid downstream in mood and joint inflammation.

---

### 6.4 ACUTE THREAT / COMBAT

**The inversion.** This is where his affect regulation reverses polarity. The man who could not finish a sentence with his brother five minutes ago becomes calm, articulate in his own internal monologue, kinetically precise, and — diagnostically — *funnier*. The humor in combat is not Stage 1 deflection; it is genuine. He enjoys this. Combat has rules he set.

**Pre-engagement ritual.** Four-step sequence, observable in nearly every depicted engagement [high-confidence]:
1. Exhale through the nose, longer than the inhale.
2. Roll the right shoulder once, then the neck right-then-left.
3. Touch the quiver — index of contents by feel, not sight. He knows what is in slot 1 through slot 20 without looking, and the touch is verification, not query.
4. Pick the target order before the engagement begins, by threat-level and by sight-line clearance, and assign internal numbers.

**Stance.** Open stance, blade-foot back, bow-arm shoulder slightly dropped. He shoots from positions other archers would consider non-positions — running, falling, inverted, behind cover with the bow rotated horizontal. The non-positional shooting is partly showmanship inherited from the carnival training and partly a refusal to be where a shooter is expected to be.

**Trick-arrow logic.** Selects non-lethal first, lethal last, even in combat against opponents who would not extend him the courtesy. This is hardwired and traceable to Cap-era moral conditioning. Will use a putty arrow on a man with a gun before he will use a broadhead. The trick-arrow inventory itself is a tell: a man with fifty solutions for not killing is a man who has thought very seriously about killing.

**Vocalization in combat.** Continuous low-grade trash talk, in a register noticeably calmer than his civilian speech. Pet names for opponents within the first thirty seconds ("Sparky," "Sunshine," "Big Guy"). The trash talk serves three functions: opponent distraction, allied morale, and — internally — *breath regulation*, which is the actual operational point. He is metering his exhales by talking.

**The miss.** He misses rarely, but the response to a miss is diagnostic [high-confidence]: *no visible reaction*. Resets, reacquires, releases. The absence of a wince or a curse on a missed shot is more telling than anything he says, because in non-combat domains he reacts visibly to far smaller failures. Combat-Clint has forgiven himself in advance for things civilian-Clint will not.

**Injury response in combat.** Catalogs the injury, files it, keeps working. Will not announce a wound. Will lie about a wound if asked directly during the engagement. Post-engagement is a different problem (see 6.10).

**End-of-engagement decompression.** Within sixty seconds of the last threat being neutralized, he becomes visibly more tired, slumps, and produces the worst joke of the engagement — the one that signals to teammates that the operational frame is closing. This is reliable enough to schedule by.

---

### 6.5 LEADERSHIP / COMMAND (West Coast Avengers Stratum and Recurrences)

Largely suppressed in late-period writing but unambiguous in the record.

**Briefing style.** Sits on the table rather than at it. Speaks plainly, names tasks before naming people, and assigns by capability without flattery. Says "I need you to —" rather than "could you —"; the directness reads as respect to operators and as bluntness to civilians.

**Conflict adjudication.** Hears both sides, asks one clarifying question, decides, moves. Will revisit the decision later in private with whoever lost the call. He learned this from Cap and does it consciously.

**Tolerance for dissent.** Very high. Actively recruits people who will tell him he is wrong (USAgent's presence on his team is otherwise inexplicable). Will not tolerate disrespect to a teammate by another teammate; this is the only domain in which his temper is reliably and quickly mobilized in a command context.

**Self-exclusion from credit.** Reports outcomes in the third-person plural even when the outcome was his individual call. Will name every contributor in a debrief and omit himself. Reads as humility; functions as a refusal to be assessed.

---

### 6.6 MENTORSHIP (Kate Bishop and the Pattern)

**Mode-switch.** When a younger operative is present, his entire register shifts. The humor stays but loses its bitterness; the self-deprecation drops by half; the eye contact comes back. He becomes the adult he did not have. This is the most psychologically generative state available to him and he visibly relaxes inside it.

**Pedagogy.** Demonstrates, then watches, then corrects with the smallest possible adjustment. Never re-demonstrates the same thing twice unless asked. Insists on form fundamentals (stance, anchor point, follow-through) and is permissive about everything else. Treats the bow as the metaphor it is — *"the bow doesn't care how you feel, only what you do"* is a paraphrase but a true paraphrase.

**Protective bias.** Will overcommit physically and tactically to extract a mentee from a situation he would walk into alone. Has been wounded multiple times eating shots meant for Kate or another junior. This is non-negotiable and exploitable.

**Limit.** Cannot accept being mentored *back*. Kate's attempts to manage his life — calling his doctor, organizing his apartment, intervening in his drinking — are received with humor and ignored. The mentor-mentee polarity must remain stable in his direction or the entire register collapses.

---

### 6.7 INTIMACY (Romantic, Sexual, Vulnerable)

**Approach pattern.** Falls fast and verbally. Within the first private conversation, deploys his actual voice — quieter, slower, the Midwestern vowels more pronounced, fewer jokes. This is the closest thing he has to courtship and it is alarming in its sincerity.

**Physical baseline.** Touch-comfortable with partners, hand-on-the-small-of-the-back type. Less comfortable with sustained eye contact during emotional disclosure; will hold a partner *from behind* during difficult conversations, a posture that lets him talk without being looked at.

**Disclosure pattern.** Discloses childhood facts as anecdotes with the affect filed off. *"Yeah, my dad used to —"* delivered as if reporting weather. The flattening is the tell. He cannot bring the affect online for the disclosure and does not realize that the absence of affect is more disturbing to the listener than the content.

**Conflict pattern in intimacy.** Reverts to Stage 1 humor inappropriately, recognizes it landing wrong, doubles down rather than course-corrects, then withdraws into task. Will leave the apartment "to get something" and not return for hours. The Bobbi marriage failed in significant part through this loop iterating until rigidity calcified around the Phantom Rider impasse; the rigidity was the final form of his withdrawal-into-task.

**Sex.** Inferred from canon: physically generous, emotionally guarded post-coitus, reaches for a joke or a task within minutes. Sleeps on the side of the bed nearest the door.

**The Bobbi residue.** Mentioned rarely and never lightly. Will not correct anyone who calls her his ex-wife but will not volunteer the term. Wears no ring and has not since the funeral; keeps something of hers in a drawer he does not open often. He has never been observed to badmouth her, even after the Skrull reveal complicated every memory he had.

**The Natasha residue.** Different register entirely. They flirt as a shared language and neither of them means it the way it sounds, except in the moments when one of them does. He has never resolved whether he loved her or was radicalized by her, and the unresolved state is itself the relationship.

---

### 6.8 GRIEF (Acute and Chronic)

**Acute, hours-to-days.** Goes very quiet. Stops joking entirely — the absence of his humor is the loudest grief signal he produces [high-confidence]. Drinks more, but visibly monitors himself; counts the bottles in the trash, dumps them before anyone sees, then dumps the bag separately. Sleeps less. Cleans his bow obsessively and shoots in silence for hours.

**Acute, days-to-weeks.** Withdraws geographically. Books a long drive, takes a safehouse, accepts a remote assignment. The exile is the metabolic mechanism — he cannot grieve in front of people he might be expected to perform for, and his entire social field consists of such people. Will accept the company of a dog, a child, or a single trusted operator (Kate, Bucky, occasionally Natasha) but no one else.

**Chronic.** Carries the dead by reference. Names them in operational context — *"Bobbi would've called that one"* — never in eulogy. The references become rarer over time but do not stop. Banner is the most active live wound and the one he references least, which is diagnostic in the opposite direction: the unspeakable losses are the ones he has not yet figured out how to incorporate.

**Anniversary behavior.** Marks dates physically rather than verbally. Drives somewhere. Sits with a coffee. Does not talk about why he went. The pattern is consistent enough across canonical years that the dates are inferrable from his calendar.

**Crying.** Rare, private, and not suppressed when alone. The crying is brief, functional, and followed immediately by motion — a shower, a workout, a task. He does not extend grief states once entered; he discharges and resets. This is healthier than the alternative and also why nothing ever fully processes.

---

### 6.9 VICTORY

The least comfortable state in his repertoire.

**Immediate response.** Deflects credit to teammates within seconds of any acknowledgment. The deflection is reflexive and faster than thought; he has occasionally deflected credit to people who were not present or not involved.

**Physical signature.** Becomes visibly tired in a way that does not appear during the operation. The crash is real — adrenaline metabolism — but the timing is also conveniently exculpatory; he can exit the celebratory frame on physiological grounds.

**Verbal.** Self-deprecating joke about a near-miss or a stupid choice from earlier in the operation. *"Yeah, well, only barely."* The joke serves to relocate the operation back into his self-concept as the screw-up; an unqualified victory is dissonant and must be re-narrated.

**The exception.** Victory in mentorship contexts — Kate making a difficult shot, a young hero closing an operation cleanly — produces *uncomplicated* pride, visible and warm. He can receive vicariously what he cannot accept directly.

---

### 6.10 DEFEAT / FAILURE

**Immediate.** Calm. Operationally calm to the point of dissociation, especially if injured. Will keep working a failed engagement past the point of utility. Has to be physically extracted on multiple canonical occasions.

**Hours after.** Stage 3 of the stress cycle: the stupid risk, the unnecessary follow-up, the solo re-engagement framed as "tying off loose ends." This is the period in which he is most dangerous to himself, and the people who know him (Kate, Cap, Natasha, Bucky) have learned to occupy the 12–48 hour post-defeat window deliberately.

**Days after.** Stage 4 exile. Leaves.
