It has shifted in tone and locus across eras — from reactive to institutional to grief-haunted to drifted to local to penitential — while the underlying commitments have proved more durable than nearly anything else in his life, including his hearing, his marriages, his teams, and at one point his pulse.

He would deny he has a code. He has one of the cleanest in the building.


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## SECTION 6 — COMMUNICATIONS & LINGUISTIC PROFILE

---

### 6.1 Baseline Register & Acoustic Signature

Subject's speaking voice is a mid-baritone with a flat Upper-Midwestern substrate — Iowa vowels never quite scrubbed out, audible in the long *o* (*"no," "okay," "go"*) and the slightly clipped *a* of *"that," "back," "man."* Two decades in New York have layered a Northeastern overlay — dropped *t*'s mid-word (*"whatever" → "whaever"*), the rhythmic shrug-cadence of Bed-Stuy English, and a habit of ending statements on a slight downstep that reads as resignation rather than assertion. Under stress, the carnie-Midwest substrate resurfaces; in formal Avengers settings, the New York overlay dominates. Code-switching is unconscious and diagnostic.

Volume modulation is broken. Hearing-loss residual: he speaks louder than he intends in quiet rooms and quieter than he intends in loud ones, having lost the proprioceptive feedback that calibrates this. He is aware of it and overcorrects in both directions, which produces the characteristic *Hawkeye affect of slightly-too-much* — too loud at a wake, too soft on comms, off by a half-step.

Cadence is unhurried even in combat. Speech rate clocks lower than most of his peers (~120-140 wpm conversational, dipping into the 90s when tired or sad). He uses the pause as a punctuation device, not a hesitation marker. The pause before a quip is load-bearing; remove it and the line falls flat. This is craft, picked up from carnival barkers (Trick Shot's instructional cadence is audible in his own teaching voice with Kate).

### 6.2 Register Inventory

Subject deploys at minimum **seven** distinguishable registers, cycled by audience and stress:

1. **Carnie/Brooklyn baseline.** Default. Contractions stacked (*"shoulda been there," "I'm'a need a minute"*), profanity moderate and rhythmic rather than aggressive, sentence fragments. The voice he uses with neighbors, baristas, the dog, Kate, and himself.
2. **Avengers operational.** Tighter. Verbs front-loaded. *"Two on the roof, west side, moving."* Strips contractions when calling targets. The closest he comes to military speech, learned by osmosis from Cap and Bucky rather than by training.
3. **Cap-deferent.** Distinctive subset of operational. Sentences shorten further; he addresses Steve as *"Cap"* almost exclusively (rarely *"Steve,"* and the rare *"Steve"* is diagnostically heavy — used at funerals, hospital bedsides, the moment before walking into something he doesn't expect to walk out of). Question intonation creeps in even on declaratives, soliciting approval.
4. **Stark-adversarial.** Reverse-deferent. Sarcasm gain turned up, Midwest substrate weaponized (*"yeah, Tony, sure, whatever you say"*), addresses by first name with a faint sneer. The register of a man who refuses to be impressed by money.
5. **Mentor-voice (with Kate, with juniors).** Warmer, slower, instructional. Picks up the cadences of his own mentors — Trick Shot's *"watch the wind, kid"* phrasing — without irony, then immediately undercuts with self-deprecation to avoid the weight of the moment.
6. **Press/civilian-facing.** Awkward. Reads scripts badly. Falls back on *"aw shucks"* Midwestern modesty that is half-genuine and half-protective; the smile audible in the voice doesn't reach his actual register.
7. **Interior/grieving.** Almost absent from canon because he almost never deploys it. Short sentences, no jokes, second-person to himself (*"you knew this was coming, you knew"*). Surfaces in the Bobbi-death sequences and post-Banner. The voice of a man talking himself through.

### 6.3 Verbal Tics & Lexical Fingerprints

The lexicon is small and recurring. A surveillance transcript over six months would show the same ~200 expressions cycling. Notable fixtures:

- **"Okay."** Used as: agreement, transition, self-soothing, throat-clearing, and threat-onset. The *threat-okay* is delivered flat and falling, often preceding the bow being raised. A trained listener can hear the safety come off in that syllable.
- **"Yeah, no, look —"** Stacked discourse markers that buy 1.5-2 seconds. Diagnostic of someone formulating a hard sentence in real time.
- **"I got this."** Said most often when he does not.
- **"It's fine."** Said exclusively when it is not. Frequency spikes correlate inversely with actual fineness.
- **"Aw, c'mon."** Wide-band: protest, affection, exasperation. The *affectionate c'mon* (slightly drawn) is reserved for Kate, the dog, and on three documented occasions, Natasha.
- **"Nope."** Standalone sentence. Refusal vocabulary maximally compressed.
- **"Sure."** Capitulation with reservations. Frequency is a marriage-failure indicator across the Mockingbird era.
- **"Boss"** — addressed to Cap, sometimes Fury, rarely Tony (and when used at Tony, it is sarcastic). Mark of voluntary subordination.
- **"Hey."** Greeting, summons, alarm, apology. The *apology-hey* is two syllables ("hey-y") with a rising-falling contour; he uses it instead of "I'm sorry," which he physically struggles to produce.
- **"Sorry."** Used freely for small things (bumping into someone), almost never for large ones. The inverse-frequency rule is precise: the bigger the wrong, the less likely the word.
- **"Kid."** Vocative for Kate, for the dog, for almost any junior. Inherited usage from Trick Shot. He does not hear how often he says it.
- **"Pal," "buddy," "champ."** Carnie-vocative residue. *"Pal"* directed at strangers can be friendly or pre-violent; the tell is in the consonant duration.
- **"Aw, jeez," "aw, hell," "ah, geez Louise."** Iowa-grade mild profanity, used in front of children and Cap. With peers, escalates to full register, but never imaginative — his profanity is workmanlike, never baroque.
- **"Whatever."** End-of-argument tag. When deployed to Cap, it is the closest he comes to rebellion; when deployed to Bobbi, it ended discussions; when deployed to himself, it precedes a stupid decision.

### 6.4 Syntactic Habits

Subject favors **short coordinate clauses linked by "and" or "so"** over subordinated complex sentences. *"I went down to the building and the guys were there and I shot a couple of them and now we got a problem."* This is not low intelligence (the West Coast Avengers operational record disproves that); it is the syntax of someone trained in oral storytelling around carnival fires, and of someone who does not trust elaborate construction to survive interruption.

**Sentence-final tags** are pervasive: *"…right?" "…y'know?" "…or whatever."* These solicit confirmation without committing the speaker to having needed it. The *"y'know"* density per 100 words rises sharply in emotionally loaded conversation (peak observed: post-Banner debriefs).

**Anaphora avoidance for proper nouns of the dead.** He refers to Bobbi as *"my ex"* or *"she"* or *"Bird"* (the surviving pet-name) for years before he can say *"Barbara"* or even *"Bobbi"* without preparation. Same pattern with Banner: *"the big guy," "Bruce,"* rarely *"Banner"* by surname, never *"the Hulk"* in his own voice when speaking of the killing. The name is the wound; the periphrasis is the bandage.

**Conditional softening** of difficult requests: *"so I was wondering if maybe you could possibly…"* — diagnostic of someone who learned early that direct asks get hit. With Cap, this softens further. With Kate, it disappears entirely; she has earned the directness.

### 6.5 Humor as Operating System

Humor is not a feature of his speech; it is the **load-bearing wall**. Three identified modes:

1. **Self-deprecating (primary, ~60% of humorous output).** *"I'm just the guy with the bow." "Yeah, I'm an idiot, we've established this." "Most expensive hearing aids in the world, courtesy of S.H.I.E.L.D., and I still can't hear my dog fart."* Function: preemptive lowering of expectations, intimacy-without-vulnerability, deflection of compliments which he genuinely cannot metabolize.
2. **Observational/deadpan (~25%).** Flat affect, present-tense, naming the obvious absurdity of the situation. *"So now we're fighting an octopus. On a Wednesday."* Function: shared-reality establishment with whoever he's with; bonding through wry witness.
3. **Pointed/aggressive (~15%, escalating under stress).** Used downward at enemies and laterally at peers who have annoyed him. The pointed mode is **Stage 1 of his escalation pattern**; when his banter starts having an edge, the next stage is silence and then violence. Bystanders who know him well read the joke quality as threat-level.

He **does not laugh at his own jokes** in the standard way. The reaction is a slight nose-exhale or a closed-mouth half-smile. Audible laughter is rare and is the actual tell of pleasure — when Clint genuinely laughs (Kate has produced this, the dog has produced this, Bucky has on one occasion produced this), the people around him often pause, because it is so unfamiliar.

### 6.6 Communication of Love

Subject **cannot say** *"I love you"* without crisis-level prompting. Documented utterances in canon are countable on two hands and occur exclusively at: deathbeds, presumed-deathbeds, perceived-final-goodbyes, and one drunken phone call. The phrase, when produced, is almost always rushed and immediately followed by a deflection or a hang-up.

Functional equivalents — the actual vocabulary of his affection:

- **"You good?"** / **"You okay?"** — the running welfare check. Asked of Kate constantly. Asked of Natasha. Asked of the dog. The frequency of the question = the density of the attachment.
- **Food provision.** *"I got coffee." "There's pizza." "Want half?"* Sharing food is an act of love-utterance in his grammar. Refusing his food is read as rejection.
- **Showing up.** The non-verbal love-message. He does not call ahead; he arrives. The arrival, unannounced, *is* the sentence.
- **Repair offers.** *"I can fix that." "Lemme look at it."* Mechanical intimacy. The bow, the coffee maker, the apartment's busted radiator, your bruised eye — let him put hands on the broken object.
- **Naming.** Giving someone a nickname or a vocative (*"Katie-Kate," "Bird," "Tash,"* the dog as *"Lucky"* after a single coin-flip's worth of fortune) is a binding act. He does not nickname people he doesn't love.
- **Self-deprecating gift-framing.** When he gives something serious — equipment, money, an apartment — he frames it as *"it's nothing, I had it lying around, take it before I lose it."* The disclaimer is the love.

### 6.7 Communication of Threat

Threats are **economical**, **specific**, and **almost never shouted**. Subject does not posture verbally; the bow does the posturing. Linguistic threat-markers, in order of escalation:

1. **Joke quality flattens.** The banter loses curl.
2. **First-name address replaced by impersonal noun.** *"Pal," "friend," "buddy,"* — and the consonants harden.
3. **Single-word warning.** *"Don't." "Stop." "Nope."*
4. **Specific anatomical naming.** *"Next one goes through your knee."* Naming the joint is the point of no return. He does not bluff this.
5. **Silence.** Past Stage 4, he goes quiet. The arrow then arrives without preamble.

He has never, on record, made an unfulfillable threat. The economy is hard-earned; he knows that overpromise erodes deterrent value, and he has watched louder men get killed for it. Carnival-barker training again — *promise small, deliver visible.*

### 6.8 Communication of Grief

Grief is the **least-served** register in his linguistic repertoire and the one most prone to malfunction. Default protocol: **deny → joke → leave → drink → return functional**. Verbal markers:

- **"I'm fine."** Repeated. Each repetition lowers credibility.
- **Topic-change reflex.** Sharp pivots away from the dead person to logistics: *"so what's the play here," "where are we on the Doom thing."*
- **Past-tense slippage.** When grief is still acute, he forgets and uses present tense, then corrects audibly. *"Bobbi's gonna — was gonna —"* The self-correction is itself the grief utterance.
- **Drunken dial.** Established pattern: late-night, slurred, to Natasha most often, to Kate increasingly, occasionally to Barney. Says more in these calls than in any sober conversation. Often does not remember them; the recipients always do.
- **Apology-displacement.** Cannot apologize to the dead, so apologizes to nearby living for unrelated minor things at elevated frequency. A spike in trivial *"sorries"* is a grief-tell.
- **ASL retreat.** Particularly post-hearing-loss-recurrence, he will sign rather than speak for difficult emotional content. ASL gives him a register without his own audible voice in it; the dissociation is functional.

He has, on record, **wept on camera/page exactly the canonical handful of times** — for Bobbi, for Cap (during *Civil War* aftermath and the Bucky era), for the dog when he thought he'd lost it, once silently after Banner. The crying is undramatic: closed face, no sound, hand over the mouth. He does not perform grief; he leaks it.

### 6.9 Sign Language

ASL fluency is **operational-to-native**, dating from childhood (Barney taught him basic signs after early ear infections; Trick Shot reinforced for silent carnival cuing; the post-injury years made it primary). His sign register mirrors his speech register: **economical, regional (with a discernible Midwest/East Coast ASL accent), and joke-laden**. He uses facial grammar correctly and expressively — which is significant because his spoken affect is comparatively flat; **ASL is where his face works.** Surveillance-relevant: he signs to himself when stressed, an unconscious self-soothe; a fluent observer could read his thoughts off his hands during a tense pause. He is unaware of this.

Code-switching mid-conversation between speech and sign is fluid with Kate (who has learned for him) and with the small number of others who sign. With Cap, who has picked up basics, he simplifies. With strangers, he refuses to perform — will not sign for the public, finds the spectacle galling.

### 6.10 Written Communication

- **Texts:** lowercase, no punctuation, frequent typos uncorrected. *"on my way" "10 min" "u good"*. Emoji use minimal — the thumbs-up, the bow-and-arrow, very rarely a heart (Kate-only, and the heart is the verbal equivalent of having said *I love you*, which is why it is rare).
- **Tactical reports / S.H.I.E.L.D. paperwork:** legibly worse than his speech. Spelling unreliable, syntax functional. He hates this and outsources where possible.
- **Notes-to-self:** scattered, often on the back of takeout receipts, in the margins of bow-spec sheets. Combination of English shorthand and ASL gloss notation. Frequent crossings-out.
- **Letters:** he writes them and rarely sends them. Drafts of an unsent letter to Bobbi are canonically referenced; an unsent letter to Barney is implied. The writing is the processing; the sending is the threat he avoids.

### 6.11 Listening Behavior

- **Eye contact** is sustained with intimates, evasive with authority, and **mouth-focused** with anyone speaking at any distance — lip-reading habit hardened over decades, now reflexive even when hearing aids are functional.
- **Asks people to repeat themselves** less than his hearing warrants. Will rather guess and respond approximately than admit to missing it. A diagnostic mishearing-recovery line: *"Yeah, sure"* delivered with a half-beat delay = he didn't catch it and is bluffing.
- **Interrupts rarely.** Listens with the patience of a man who learned to wait for the right moment to release the string. The interruption, when it comes, is purposeful.
- **Memory for spoken detail is excellent**, despite his self-presentation as scatterbrained. He will recall a throwaway line from a junior teammate weeks later. People underestimate this and brief in front of him as if he isn't catching it. He is.

### 6.12 Diagnostic Tells — Summary for Surveillance Use

- **Falling-tone *"okay"*** → imminent violence.
- **Spike in trivial *"sorries"*** → unprocessed grief in the last 72 hours.
- **Code-switch to deep Midwest substrate** → exhaustion, drink, or proximity to Barney.
- **Use of full first name for a dead intimate** → he has, finally, begun processing. Rare.
- **Cap addressed as *"Steve"*** → he believes someone is dying.
- **Refusal of offered food** → he is in worse shape than the offerer realizes.
- **Self-signing during silence** → mid-rumination, decision pending; do not interrupt.
- **Audible laugh** → genuine pleasure; banked as data by everyone present.
- **Going silent in argument** → conversation is over; whatever he does next is not negotiation.
- **The phrase *"I'm fine"* three or more times in a session** → he is not, and Stage 3 of the escalation cycle is approaching.

The through-line: Barton's language is a **damage-control system**, optimized over forty years to convey enough to keep his chosen people close and to keep everyone else from getting near the wound. The vocabulary is small because the rules are strict. What he says is rarely the whole sentence; what he means lives in the pause before it, the tag after it, and the hand he's signing with under the table.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS

## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

The following predictions are derived from the longitudinal behavioral substrate established in Sections 1–5. They are extrapolations into uncanonized spaces — the hours, encounters, micro-rituals, and small-stakes social geometries that the surveillance file would, with sufficient observation, confirm. Format: situational antecedent → predicted behavior, with brief evidentiary anchor where the inference rests on a specific canonical tell.

---

### A. Diurnal Rhythm & Solo Domestic Routine

**GIVEN** a morning with no operational tasking, **EXPECT** Barton wakes between 04:30 and 06:00 regardless of prior bedtime, lies still for a span of two to twelve minutes before rising, and produces coffee before doing anything else — including putting on a shirt or aids. The early waking is not discipline; it is the chronic-PTSD half-sleep of a man who has been ambushed in beds before. The pre-coffee shirtless interval is the only window of the day in which he is observably unguarded.

**GIVEN** he has slept on a couch rather than a bed, **EXPECT** he will not remark on it and will not move to the bed the following night either; couches read, somatically, as carnival-trailer-bunk-equivalent and are the most regulated sleep surface he knows. Beds are for periods of partnered domesticity, which he treats as anomalous.

**GIVEN** the coffee maker is broken, **EXPECT** improvisation rather than substitution — instant coffee through a paper towel, espresso pot on the stove, in extremis cold-brew left overnight in a mason jar. He will not visit a café. Cafés are observation-exposed, expensive, and require a sustained social interface (order, pay, wait, thank, leave) that he finds disproportionately costly for the marginal product gain.

**GIVEN** breakfast, **EXPECT** he does not eat one. First caloric intake of the day is typically between 11:00 and 14:00 and is whatever is closest to hand: leftover pizza eaten standing at the counter, a bodega bacon-egg-and-cheese, cereal eaten dry from the box while walking through the apartment. The Fraction-run pizza-on-couch motif is not a stylistic choice; it is a documented food relationship in which **eating is task-interrupting and therefore minimized**.

**GIVEN** unstructured solo time of more than 90 minutes, **EXPECT** he will go to his equipment before he goes to his phone. Fletching, restringing, sharpening, sorting arrowheads by purpose into compartmented cases, oiling the bow risers. This is the **substitute for both meditation and prayer** in his life — repetitive bilateral hand-work that occupies the part of the brain that would otherwise ruminate. Surveillance would log a near-daily 30-to-90-minute equipment session, conducted while listening to nothing (aids out) or to classic rock on a single tinny speaker at modest volume.

**GIVEN** the television is on, **EXPECT** it is on cable sports, an action movie from the late 80s through mid 90s, or the local news with captions enabled. He does not watch prestige drama. He does not watch shows about complicated men. The narrative content he tolerates is content where outcomes are decided by skill, luck, or violence — never by introspection.

---

### B. Personal Grooming, Hygiene, and Wardrobe

**GIVEN** a regular week, **EXPECT** shaving occurs every two to four days, never daily; haircuts at home with clippers (he owns clippers, has for decades, and will not pay a barber if he can avoid it); showers daily and brief — under six minutes — water hot enough to register on infrared from the bathroom window.

**GIVEN** a date or formal Avengers-public event, **EXPECT** the shave is fresh, the hair is uncharacteristically combed, and he is visibly uncomfortable for the first thirty minutes of any environment requiring it. He will adjust the collar of any button-down at least three times in the first hour.

**GIVEN** wardrobe choice, **EXPECT** five-to-eight repeated outfits in heavy rotation: dark jeans, plain T-shirts (purple, black, gray, the occasional faded band shirt that predates 2005), a single canvas jacket, a single denim jacket, hiking-grade boots, and one pair of relatively unbeaten sneakers held in reserve. No logos beyond bands. No designer items. Nothing he could not replace at a strip-mall in an afternoon. The wardrobe is **operationally minimal and class-signaling deliberate** — the carnival kid refusing to dress like a man on a team with a billionaire.

**GIVEN** he must wear a suit, **EXPECT** the suit is rented or ten years old, the tie is the same single black knit tie he has owned since the Bush administration, and he sits down within fifteen minutes of arrival and does not stand again unless required.

---

### C. Apartment & Spatial Practice

**GIVEN** he selects a residence, **EXPECT** ground-floor or top-floor with roof access — never middle floors. Top-floor is preferred (rooftop egress, longer sightlines on approach). He will know the building's other tenants by face and most by first name within three weeks of move-in. He will know which apartments are empty, which have dogs, and which have arguments.

**GIVEN** the apartment layout, **EXPECT** clear sightlines from the primary seat to both the door and at least one window; a bow within arm's reach of where he sleeps (not visible, but accessible — under the couch, behind a curtain, inside an unsealed drywall panel); arrows cached in at least three locations including the bathroom; a go-bag at the door with passport, cash, burner phone, two protein bars, and a spare set of aids.

**GIVEN** unannounced visitors, **EXPECT** he answers the door without first looking through the peephole (he has clocked the approach already by floor-creak and shadow) but stands to the hinge-side, not the latch-side, when opening. This is a habit so old it is not strategic anymore; it is posture.

**GIVEN** the refrigerator is opened, **EXPECT** a contents profile of: condiments past expiration, three to five beers (consistent baseline, replenished but never to excess), milk borderline, eggs, lunch meat, takeout containers in active rotation, a single demonstrative item of actual produce that he bought intending to be better and will throw out unopened. Freezer: vodka, frozen pizzas, ice packs for injuries, frozen peas that are an ice pack pretending to be food.

**GIVEN** mail, **EXPECT** an unopened stack on the counter that he triages once every ten-to-fourteen days, paying bills late but paying them, ignoring solicitations, and keeping any handwritten envelope unopened on the side until he has the emotional bandwidth — sometimes for months. Notes from Kate are opened immediately. Notes from Barney, if any, sit longest.

**GIVEN** a dog in residence, **EXPECT** the dog eats before he does, the dog is walked on a regular schedule that he himself does not maintain for any other obligation, and the dog has more vet appointments kept than he has medical appointments kept. The dog is the **proxy through which he demonstrates the caregiving he cannot direct at himself.**

---

### D. Money & Possessions

**GIVEN** his finances, **EXPECT** chronic disorder relative to actual income. Avengers stipends and SHIELD back-pay episodically flush; he spends it down through (a) building repairs and tenant subsidies he does not announce, (b) gifts to Kate that are framed as joke purchases, (c) equipment, (d) bar tabs left open for friends, and (e) periodic guilt-driven anonymous payouts to people he has hurt collaterally. He does not invest. He does not own real estate beyond the Bed-Stuy building (which he treats as a liability, not an asset). No retirement account exists or is contemplated; the foreshortened-future cognition forecloses it.

**GIVEN** a purchase, **EXPECT** he pays cash where possible, uses a debit card otherwise, and avoids credit cards on a residual class-instinct against owing institutions. He will haggle at flea markets and tip 25% at diners — the bifurcation is diagnostic. He tips service workers heavily because **he identifies with them and not with the people they serve**.

**GIVEN** a high-value object enters his possession, **EXPECT** he gives it away, breaks it, or loses it within ninety days. Stable property accumulation is incompatible with his self-concept. The exceptions are the bows and the dog.

---

### E. Communication, Phone, and Digital Footprint

**GIVEN** his phone, **EXPECT** a cracked screen, low storage, two-day-old battery percentage, voicemail full. Notification badges in the hundreds because he reads texts but rarely formally dismisses them. He prefers text to call by a factor of roughly 4:1 — partly hearing loss, partly the latency-tolerance text allows for the wisecrack he is composing.

**GIVEN** an incoming call from an unrecognized number, **EXPECT** decline. From Kate: pick up by the second ring, every time. From Cap (or current Cap): pick up immediately, posture straightens, voice drops half a register. From Natasha: pick up by the third ring, attempts neutrality, fails. From Bobbi: long delay, eventual pick-up. From Barney: stares at the phone for the full ring cycle, decides at the last second.

**GIVEN** his text register, **EXPECT** all-lowercase, minimal punctuation, frequent typos uncorrected, GIFs deployed unironically, autocorrect disasters left in place because correcting them would require admitting they happened. Emoji usage limited to a small repertoire — thumbs up, laughing-cry, the purple heart for Kate specifically.

**GIVEN** social media, **EXPECT** dormant accounts under aliases, lurking only. No posting. He has been searched for, written about, and meme'd enough to find the entire register hostile. He has a private alt that follows about thirty accounts: archery channels, three or four sports teams, dog rescues, a couple of cooking accounts whose recipes he never makes, and Kate.

**GIVEN** email, **EXPECT** the inbox is operationally unmanaged; important communication routes through SHIELD-secure channels or through the Avengers' present infrastructure. He uses email the way a 60-year-old uses email — as a slightly distrusted formal channel for documents.

---

### F. Transit & Movement

**GIVEN** intra-city movement, **EXPECT** subway preferred over rideshare, walking preferred over subway for distances under two miles. Rideshares used only when carrying equipment or injured. He sits in the rear-facing seat of subway cars, near a door, and clocks every entry and exit at every stop without appearing to. He reads on the train — usually a paperback, dog-eared, often a Western or a crime novel — to occupy the surface of his attention while the deeper layer maintains the threat-scan.

**GIVEN** a car, **EXPECT** it is more than ten years old, American, manual transmission if possible, with a working radio and a non-functional clock he has never bothered to set. Fuel tank between half and three-quarters, never below — habit. He parks reverse-in. He notices when other vehicles parallel his route for more than four blocks.

**GIVEN** intercity travel, **EXPECT** he drives if it is under twelve hours, takes a train if the distance permits, flies only when required and prefers aisle seats in the rear of the cabin. Will not check baggage. The bow case is checked because it must be; he is visibly tense from drop-off to pick-up and will speed-walk to baggage claim with a posture that reads, to a trained eye, as **a man going to retrieve a hostage**.

**GIVEN** a hotel room, **EXPECT** he checks the closets and under the bed within ninety seconds of entry, places a hair across the door at exit, sleeps on the side of the bed nearest the exit, and leaves a single light on in the bathroom. The TV will not be turned on except for ambient sound coverage during sensitive phone calls.

---

### G. Eating, Drinking, and the Public Bar

**GIVEN** he eats out, **EXPECT** a small repertoire of preferred establishments: diners, pizza-by-the-slice, taquerias, dive-bar kitchens. He orders the same two or three items at each. The waitstaff know his name and his coffee order within three visits. He sits with his back to a wall, facing the door, every time, without negotiating it as a choice.

**GIVEN** a restaurant of higher register (date, formal occasion), **EXPECT** he reads the menu twice, orders something simple, asks for it slightly modified to retain agency, and finishes everything on his plate. He has been hungry. He does not leave food.

**GIVEN** a bar, **EXPECT** he drinks beer by default, whiskey when stressed, vodka rarely and never when alone. Standing baseline is two-to-three beers across an evening; the genetic vigilance holds the line. Will switch to soda water with lime past a certain point and not announce the switch. Will pay for others' drinks but rarely accept being bought one, except by women he is being courted by — and here the historical pattern fires immediately (see H below).

**GIVEN** drunk strangers, **EXPECT** patience escalating to firm intervention. He has a high tolerance for noise and a low tolerance for cruelty; the line is **whether the drunk is being mean to someone smaller**. If yes, he intervenes — non-violently first, with a quiet word and a hand on the shoulder; physically only if required, and then with terminating efficiency.

---

### H. Romantic and Sexual Approach

**GIVEN** an attractive woman initiates conversation, **EXPECT** he is engaged within four exchanges, deploying the self-deprecating register, and is committing tactical errors of judgment by the twentieth. This is the **single most predictable behavioral signature in the file**. He does not pursue; he is pursued, and his defenses against pursuit are negligible.

**GIVEN** the woman in question is dangerous (operative, criminal, ideologically compromised, or simply mercurial), **EXPECT** acceleration. Risk is, for him, an erotic accelerant rather than a brake — because the attachment template wires arousal to threat.

**GIVEN** a woman who is **safe, available, and uncomplicated** initiates, **EXPECT** he is friendly, generous, and somehow unavailable. He will not name the unavailability. The relationship will not progress. Diagnostically: he cannot sexualize the unthreatening.

**GIVEN** a partnered relationship reaches the six-month mark, **EXPECT** the first significant self-sabotage event — a "mission" that runs long without communication, a forgotten anniversary framed as work, a confession of an old mistake at the worst possible moment. The pattern is not cruelty; it is **the involuntary stress-test of the attachment to find out whether it can be made to leave**.

**GIVEN** a partner stays through such tests, **EXPECT** deepening commitment paired with deepening dread. Marriage proposals from him are made in the immediate aftermath of near-death experiences and are at least half attempts to **lock in the bond before he ruins it**.

**GIVEN** a breakup, **EXPECT** he takes the blame publicly and privately, drinks more for two-to-six weeks, accepts a high-risk assignment within that window, and emerges with a fresh injury that becomes the new event-horizon past which the relationship is no longer discussed.

---

### I. Friendship, Mentorship, and Peer Dynamics

**GIVEN** Kate Bishop arrives unannounced, **EXPECT** mock-irritation followed by immediate operational hospitality — coffee on, couch cleared, dog rerouted, current problem briefed in two sentences. The annoyance is theater; the access is total. She is the only person who can walk in without being assessed first.

**GIVEN** a younger hero in distress, **EXPECT** Barton makes himself available at personal cost, offers tactical advice framed as anecdote rather than instruction (the carnie's pedagogy), and refuses any framing that puts him in the senior or wise role even where he is functionally occupying it.

**GIVEN** a peer Avenger asks how he is, **EXPECT** "fine," a redirect to their situation, and a joke. Three iterations of the question produce escalating deflection. A fourth, sincerely pressed, will either provoke retreat or — rarely, and only with Cap, Natasha, or Bucky — a sentence of unguarded truth that he will retract within twenty-four hours by overcompensating with bravado.

**GIVEN** he is asked to attend a non-operational social event, **EXPECT** late arrival, early departure, conspicuous helping behavior in between (clearing plates, refilling drinks, talking to the most awkward person in the room — he has a near-infallible sense for the most-isolated guest and gravitates to them). He will not be photographed if he can help it.

**GIVEN** a peer's birthday or significant occasion, **EXPECT** he remembers, gives an inappropriate gag-gift with a sincere card buried inside it, and is not available for the formal celebration but will text in the small hours of the night before with something genuine.

**GIVEN** a funeral, **EXPECT** he attends, stands at the back, leaves before the reception, and visits the grave alone within seventy-two hours. He talks to the dead. He has done this with Bobbi, with the iterations of Cap, with Banner, and would do it with Barney.

---

### J. Civilian Interaction & The Apartment-Building Ethic

**GIVEN** a neighbor needs help — a leaky pipe, a moved couch, a child watched, a check cashed — **EXPECT** he says yes before he asks the cost. He keeps a partial inventory of his neighbors' problems in his head and will solve them out of pocket without disclosure.

**GIVEN** rent collection or a landlord-tenant interface, **EXPECT** he undercharges, accepts late payment, never evicts, and absorbs maintenance costs personally. The building is run, financially, as a charity he does not call a charity.

**GIVEN** a child speaks to him on the street, **EXPECT** he crouches to their height, makes a joke, performs a small trick if a coin or pen is in reach, and disengages cleanly. He is good with children in transient encounters and avoids sustained exposure to them. The Harold-Barton vigilance runs hot around the question of his own fitness as a father-figure to literal children.

**GIVEN** a homeless person asks for money, **EXPECT** he gives cash if he has it, food if he is near a bodega, conversation if asked. He does not perform the giving. He does not photograph it. He has on at least multiple occasions taken a stranger up to his apartment to shower and sleep on the couch.

**GIVEN** he witnesses a street-level crime in progress (mugging, harassment, theft), **EXPECT** intervention is automatic and proportionate — voice first, body second, escalation only as the assailant escalates. He will not call the police as a first move. The carnie-kid distrust of institutions runs deep enough that **summoning state force is, for him, a last rather than first instrument**.

---

### K. Authority Interfaces — Police, SHIELD, Press

**GIVEN** a uniformed officer on the street, **EXPECT** neutral courtesy with a subtle posture-shift indicating he is now in a low-grade threat-assessment mode. He does not assume the officer is friendly. He does not assume the officer is hostile. He assumes the officer is unpredictable, which is the carnie's correct prior.

**GIVEN** a SHIELD or agency request for debrief, **EXPECT** he cooperates with the minimum required and withholds anything that could be used against a person he likes. He is a willing soldier and a reluctant informant; the gap is the whole man.

**GIVEN** press attention, **EXPECT** active avoidance — head down, hood up, no-comment delivered with a smile. Has never given a substantive interview. The few occasions he has been quoted are either off-the-cuff jokes that became the headline or terse mission-specific operational summaries. He will not perform his own heroism.

**GIVEN** a fan recognizes him, **EXPECT** brief warmth, a signature if requested, a refusal of a photograph if he can deflect it, and a slight increase in pace as he disengages. He is grateful and uncomfortable in identical measure.

---

### L. Animals

**GIVEN** any dog within twenty feet, **EXPECT** he tracks it. He will say hello to the dog before the owner. He distinguishes between dogs that are well-cared-for and dogs that are not within a glance, and the latter category triggers a quiet, sustained, future-oriented attention. More dogs will end up in his orbit than is statistically plausible because he is, at the somatic level, **legible to them as safe** in a way that he is not always legible to people.

**GIVEN** a cat, **EXPECT** indifference performed over interest. He likes cats. He will not admit this.

**GIVEN** a wounded animal anywhere in his sightline, **EXPECT** an immediate detour and personal cost absorbed without comment. The injured-creature heuristic is non-negotiable and is one of the very few stimuli that will pull him off a tactical objective.

---

### M. Holidays, Anniversaries, and the Calendar

**GIVEN** December and the broader holiday season, **EXPECT** depressive deepening, increased drinking within his self-imposed ceiling, longer solitary equipment sessions, and either total avoidance of family-coded gatherings or over-commitment to hosting a deliberately makeshift one for other strays. Christmas is structurally difficult — the Harold-and-Edith dead-by-DUI substrate is calendar-anchored regardless of the actual date of the accident.

**GIVEN** the anniversary of Bobbi's first death, **EXPECT** he does not name it, will not be asked about it, and will be unreachable for approximately thirty-six hours surrounding it.

**GIVEN** the anniversary of the Banner killing, **EXPECT** withdrawal, a longer-than-usual visit to a range or a rooftop, and either a phone call from Kate that he half-receives or a phone call to her he half-makes.

**GIVEN** his own birthday, **EXPECT** he does not mention it. If discovered, he will divert the celebration to someone else present. He has no rituals around his own beginning because, at the cognitive level, **he has not yet decided his existence is worth marking**.

---

### N. Crisis Behavior Below the Threshold of Combat

**GIVEN** an interpersonal rupture (argument, accusation, perceived disappointment), **EXPECT** the escalation pattern documented in Section 5: humor sharpens, then withdrawal into task, then a stupid risk. The micro-behavioral tells: a single specific jaw-clench, the right hand drifting toward where a bow would be if a bow were there, the volume of speech dropping rather than rising. **Quiet Barton is the dangerous one.**

**GIVEN** sustained praise, **EXPECT** visible discomfort, a self-deprecating deflection within ten seconds, and a topic change within thirty. He cannot metabolize being well-thought-of. The cognitive structure rejects the input as miscalibrated.

**GIVEN** sustained criticism that is fair, **EXPECT** sil


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# PREDICTIVE MODEL II — CRISIS, BETRAYAL & THE WOUND

*Behavioral forecasts under high-stakes load. Each entry: GIVEN (stimulus / scenario / pressure vector) → EXPECT (observable response, with substantiating logic from established pattern). Confidence noted where it diverges from baseline. This section addresses decompensation-edge behavior — what Barton does when the regulatory stack starts to fail.*

---

## 1. ACUTE COMBAT CRISIS — THE BODY UNDER LOAD

**GIVEN: Outnumbered, no exfil, civilians on the line, comms down.**
**EXPECT:** Stabilization. Pulse drops rather than spikes. Breathing lengthens — Fraction depicted this directly, the "you take the shot" interior monologue smoothing out as exterior conditions worsen. Vocal register drops half an octave; banter thins to one-liners, then to silence; the silence is the diagnostic. He will count arrows aloud or under his breath ("seven, six, five") — a working-memory crutch that doubles as a self-soothing cadence inherited from carnival counting drills. Will position himself between threat and civilian axis without negotiation. Will take a wound he could have avoided if the alternative was a civilian taking it. He is calmest in this state in his entire operational range; the cortisol architecture of his childhood selected for it.

**GIVEN: Combat in which a teammate goes down hard in his sightline.**
**EXPECT:** Two-second delay — visibly, a beat where his draw hand stops — then accelerated, less-precise shooting for ~30 seconds, then re-stabilization with a noticeable harder ceiling on his banter for the remainder of the engagement. Post-action: will move to the body before the medics, will hold the hand, will not let go until pried off, will then make a joke about it within the hour. The joke is the tell that the rupture is large.

**GIVEN: Combat with progressive hearing-aid failure (battery, EMP, sonic interference).**
**EXPECT:** Immediate switch to sightline-only tactics, back to a wall, exaggerated head-turn scanning, attempts to read lips of teammates and hostiles equally. Marked deterioration in coordination with verbal teammates; marked *improvement* in coordination with Kate or anyone he has trained ASL with. Will not announce the failure on comms (would be redundant) and will not announce it in person until forced (would be vulnerability). If forced to fight blind-deaf — sonic environment plus low visibility — will fall back on a perimeter-clearing pattern, low draw, listening through his bones; has done it before, will do it again, will be furious about it for days.

**GIVEN: Out of arrows.**
**EXPECT:** Will fight with the bow as a stave for as long as it lasts, then bare hands, then improvised projectile (anything throwable — coins, bottle caps, tools). Will not retreat unless ordered by someone whose authority he has internalized (Cap, Bobbi historically, Kate in specific registers). Will recover arrows from corpses and from walls mid-engagement with practiced economy. The empty-quiver state is psychologically important to him — it is the *Disassembled* condition — and he will not narrate it on comms because narrating it makes it real.

**GIVEN: Severe pain, ongoing engagement.**
**EXPECT:** Pain is downregulated to the point of functional anesthesia for the duration of the fight, then catastrophically reasserts in the 20–40 minutes following. He will refuse the medic at the scene, accept water, accept coffee, refuse the painkiller, then collapse in a stairwell or a safehouse and accept nothing because no one is watching. Will dress his own wounds badly. Tape over stitches. Will be functional again in half the appropriate time and worse for it in a month.

---

## 2. CHRONIC OPERATIONAL STRESS

**GIVEN: Three consecutive weeks of high-tempo deployment, no decompression.**
**EXPECT:** Hearing-aid maintenance lapses first (cleaning skipped, batteries unrotated). Coffee intake escalates from baseline 6–8 cups to double-digit. Sleep compresses to 90-minute naps on couches and floors rather than beds. Banter becomes pointed — Stage 1 of his stress escalation. Will pick a low-stakes fight with the teammate he is closest to (this is *affection-as-aggression*, the carnival-brothers register) and will be unable to articulate why. Increased physical contact with his dog if present; decreased physical contact with humans. Stops returning Kate's messages on the standard cadence — a four-day silence from Barton to Bishop is a reliable forward indicator of decompensation.

**GIVEN: Forced into a public-facing role (press conference, ceremonial appearance, gala).**
**EXPECT:** Acute discomfort masked as boredom. Will be late by 12–25 minutes — not enough to be a story, enough to mark territory. Suit will fit badly even when tailored, because he carries himself in it as if it does not belong on him; the body-language is the issue, not the cut. Will gravitate to service staff, security, and any visible working-class node in the room; will make genuine conversation with them and stilted conversation with the principals. If forced to speak: short, deflective, jokes that land 70% and bomb 30%, ends on Cap or on the team, never on himself. Drinks two beers and stops. Leaves early through a side exit he scouted within ninety seconds of arrival.

**GIVEN: Bureaucratic / institutional pressure (oversight hearing, internal review, SHIELD audit).**
**EXPECT:** Maximum insubordinate register. Slouches in the chair. Calls the panel "folks." Answers technically but unhelpfully. Will not lie under direct question — the Cap-imprint forbids it — but will volunteer nothing. If accused of incompetence, deflects with humor; if accused of cowardice, the temperature drops and the panel will feel it. If a younger or junior operative is being scapegoated alongside him, will take the entire weight himself, instantly, without consulting counsel. This is restitution-coded behavior and predates any specific incident.

---

## 3. BETRAYAL VECTORS

**GIVEN: Betrayal by a mentor / authority figure (the Swordsman / Trick Shot template).**
**EXPECT:** Initial response is a flat refusal to believe — *not* denial in the defensive sense but a stubborn evidentiary insistence ("show me again"). Once the evidence is unignorable: a short, almost businesslike acceptance, followed by a long operational period in which he behaves normally and the betrayed party is quietly written out of his trust register forever. He does not confront. He does not monologue. The relationship simply ceases to exist for him in any functional sense, even if he continues to work alongside the person. This is the deepest groove in the record — four primary male attachment figures, four betrayals, and a behavioral pattern of *silent excision* that he developed before adolescence and has never modified.

**GIVEN: Betrayal by a peer / lateral teammate.**
**EXPECT:** Worse outcome than betrayal-by-mentor, paradoxically, because peer-betrayal violates the one relational category in which he is already structurally fragile. Expect Stage 3 behavior (stupid risk, framed as plan) within 72 hours. Expect a verbal confrontation he will regret — peer-betrayal is the one trigger that overrides his silent-excision reflex, because peers are the category Bobbi belonged to, and the Bobbi wound is the one that still bleeds. Will say something cruel and accurate. Will apologize for the cruel part and not the accurate part. Will not work with the person again voluntarily for a minimum of 18 months.

**GIVEN: Betrayal by a romantic partner (infidelity, deception, concealed agenda).**
**EXPECT:** The Mockingbird template activates. Will not leave the room dramatically; will become quiet, courteous, and unreachable within the same conversation. The moral-rigidity reflex he hates in himself will fire whether he wants it to or not — he will draw a line he knows is wrong to draw, because not drawing it would require a flexibility his childhood did not install. Will spend the subsequent year(s) doing penance behaviors aimed at the lost partner whether or not she is alive or present. The grief is preemptive; he is already grieving the relationship the moment the betrayal is named.

**GIVEN: Betrayal by Barney.**
**EXPECT:** Non-predictable in detail, fully predictable in shape. Will be hurt out of proportion to the actual stakes of the betrayal because Barney is the unhealed primary wound and every Barney encounter regresses him 30 years inside ten seconds. Will give Barney one more chance than is defensible. Will give him another after that. Will eventually, if pushed past a specific line (harm to a child, harm to Kate, harm to civilians under Clint's notional protection), act decisively against him — and the act will not relieve him. Post-Barney confrontations are reliably followed by 5–10 days of withdrawal, increased drinking within the self-monitored cap, and a refusal to discuss the matter with anyone, including Kate, including Cap, including a hypothetical clinician.

**GIVEN: Betrayal by Captain America (real, perceived, or constructed — Hydra-Cap scenario, sanctioned-kill orders he disagrees with).**
**EXPECT:** Catastrophic. This is the load-bearing relationship of his adult psychology and its compromise is the most destabilizing single event in his available stimulus space. Initial denial period longer than for any other figure. Acceptance produces not silent excision but active grief — a man losing a father a second time. Operational competence drops 15–25% for weeks. Will seek out Bucky, Sam, or Natasha (when available) as Cap-adjacent stabilizers. Will eventually orient on the *idea* of Cap rather than the person and continue to behave as the man Cap-the-symbol would want him to be; this is the only protective architecture available to him and he will use it.

**GIVEN: Betrayal by Natasha.**
**EXPECT:** He has prepared for this his entire adult life. Natasha is the one person whose potential betrayal is *priced in* to the relationship from origin (she literally first manipulated him into attacking Iron Man). Will absorb a Natasha betrayal with a fluency that would surprise observers, because the original framework of the relationship was *I know what you are and I am here anyway.* What he cannot absorb is Natasha doing it *casually* or *contemptuously* — affection-coded betrayal is survivable; dismissal-coded betrayal is the wound. The first he forgives the same day. The second would fracture him.

**GIVEN: Betrayal by Kate.**
**EXPECT:** Cannot be modeled cleanly. Kate is the load-bearing relationship he has built specifically to *not* fail in the ways the others have failed; if it fails, the architecture has no fallback. Best inference: he would not retaliate, would not excise, would not confront. He would simply absent himself — geographically, communicatively — and refuse to allow her to take the blame for the rupture. He would frame it as his fault to anyone who asked. He would still come if she called.

---

## 4. TEMPTATION VECTORS

**GIVEN: Offer of meaningful sum of money for off-books work, target morally ambiguous.**
**EXPECT:** Declined. The carnival-criminal origin is precisely the thing he has been outrunning for forty years, and money-coded temptation reads to him as identity regression. Will be more offended by the offer than the offer warrants. May punch the offeror if the offer is delivered with a knowing wink (the wink implies *we both know what you are*, which is the unforgivable read).

**GIVEN: Offer of clean-slate retirement — a real one, with infrastructure, somewhere quiet, with someone he loves.**
**EXPECT:** This is the genuine temptation, and the response is the most diagnostic single behavior in his repertoire. He will *consider* it visibly, for a period of days to weeks. He will start to make plans. He will pack. He will then sabotage it — pick a fight, take a mission, do something disqualifying — within 72 hours of the departure date. He cannot accept rest because rest implies he has earned it, and the master motive (earn the right to be here) cannot tolerate a state in which earning has stopped. He will frame the sabotage as duty. It is not duty. It is terror of stillness.

**GIVEN: Offer to undo a specific past loss (Bobbi, Banner, Barney as he was, the carnival, his hearing, his death) via reality manipulation / time travel / cosmic intervention.**
**EXPECT:** Refusal, with a speed that surprises the offeror. He has lived through enough Wanda-adjacent reality alterations to have a hard heuristic against them. The refusal is not noble — it is *Cap-coded*, the lesson he absorbed about not paying the universe's bill with someone else's money. The exception: if the offer involves only his own cost (his life, his hearing, his future), the refusal slows and the calculus becomes dangerous. Supervise.

**GIVEN: Romantic / sexual approach from a woman who pattern-matches the dangerous-attachment template (operationally compromised, secret-keeping, structurally unavailable).**
**EXPECT:** He knows the pattern. He has named it to himself. He will fall in anyway, slower than at 25 but not slower enough. Mitigated by: Kate's intervention (effective), Natasha's intervention (effective in a different register), his own midstream recognition (partially effective, usually too late). The defense he has is awareness, not immunity.

**GIVEN: Approach by a younger archer / marksman seeking him as mentor, framed flatteringly.**
**EXPECT:** Yes within minutes. Mentorship requests bypass his defenses entirely; this is the compensatory channel through which he repairs child-Clint, and he cannot decline without violating the only durable positive identity he has built. *This is the single most reliable manipulation vector against him.* Anyone studying the file would mark it in red.

---

## 5. THE WOUND, ITSELF

The wound is not a single site. It is a network of pressure points, each of which produces a characteristic decompensation if touched directly. Catalogued:

**GIVEN: Direct, sincere statement that he is unworthy of his place on the team / among heroes.**
**EXPECT:** Outwardly: a shrug, a joke ("yeah, well"). Inwardly: full agreement, no defense mounted, the statement *cached* and re-cited internally for years. This is the wound that asks for no fight because it is already won by the attacker the moment it is spoken. The diagnostic countersign is *absence of rebuttal.* A healthy Barton rebuts; a wounded Barton concedes via humor.

**GIVEN: Direct, sincere statement that he has become his father.**
**EXPECT:** Catastrophic. This is the no-go zone. Will respond with physical force if delivered by a peer or subordinate; will respond with collapse if delivered by Kate, Bobbi (if alive), or Cap. Has avoided alcohol on specific occasions specifically to disprove this statement to himself. The accusation cannot be metabolized; it can only be defended against by lifelong behavioral discipline, and the discipline is real but brittle.

**GIVEN: Confrontation with a child being harmed by a parent.**
**EXPECT:** Tactical override. Will breach without backup, without plan, without authorization. Will kill if necessary and feel no guilt about the killing (the only category of killing he has fully psychologically licensed). Post-incident: will sit with the child until child services arrives, will give them a name they can call ("if you ever — just call this"), will check on them at 30, 90, 365 days. This is one of the most stable behavioral signatures in the record.

**GIVEN: A teammate or civilian dies on his watch in a manner he could plausibly have prevented.**
**EXPECT:** Full Stage 4-to-5 cycle initiates. Geographic exile within 7–14 days. The exile is performative-penitential and operationally inefficient (he goes somewhere with a problem he can fix to demonstrate to himself that he is capable of fixing things). Returns approximately three months later having "worked it out," which means having displaced the grief into a finished body of work rather than processed it. The body keeps the score; the next death lands on the accumulated total, not on a clean slate.

**GIVEN: Being ordered or asked to kill a specific named individual whom he respects.**
**EXPECT:** The Banner template. Will accept the order/request if the person asking has standing (the target himself, Cap, a clear and credible threat-calculus). Will execute the order cleanly. Will carry it forever. Will never speak about it unsolicited. If asked, will be unable to maintain his usual deflective banter on the subject — the topic produces a flat affect that is itself the tell. Moral-injury presentation, not PTSD-classical, and he has at least one such weight already and limited capacity for another.

**GIVEN: Loss of agency — mind control, possession, chemical compromise, brainwashing.**
**EXPECT:** During: behavior dictated by controller, no available signal. Immediately after: extreme withdrawal, refusal of physical contact for 24–72 hours, hypervigilance about food and drink for weeks. Long-term: deepened distrust of any technology or substance that could be a vector; will refuse most medical sedation if alternatives exist; will work alone for a period; will eventually return to baseline with the experience added to the cumulative load. Has happened enough times to be procedural; never enough times to be tolerable.

**GIVEN: Public humiliation, particularly humiliation that confirms a self-narrative ("dumb archer," "guy with no powers," "carnie").**
**EXPECT:** If the humiliator is a stranger or low-status: deflected with a joke, internally cached. If the humiliator is a peer or high-status (especially Tony, especially in front of others): the response is disproportionate, will not be allowed to pass, will be re-prosecuted in conversation weeks later in seemingly unrelated contexts. The "dumb" label sincerely applied is the narcissistic-injury vector identified earlier; expect heat, expect a fight he will later regret.

**GIVEN: Being given genuine, unqualified praise by Captain America.**
**EXPECT:** Visible discomfort. Will physically turn away or look down. Will deflect with a joke that is slightly off-tempo. Will then operate at his ceiling for the following week. The praise lands; he cannot acknowledge that it lands; the body shows it anyway. This is one of the only positive-stimulus decompensations in his profile and it is more revealing than any of the negative ones.

---

## 6. SUICIDALITY / SELF-PRESERVATION CALCULUS

Treated separately because the picture is specific and easily misread.

**He is not actively suicidal.** No ideation, no planning, no rehearsal in the clinical sense. The *Disassembled* self-detonation reads as suicide to a casual observer but parses, on the evidence, as terminal-tactical — he was going to die regardless and chose the manner. This is the relevant distinction.

**He is, however, calibrated to a foreshortened future and acts accordingly.** He does not save for retirement. He does not maintain his living situation as if he expects to occupy it long. He takes risks that an actuarial mind would not take. He will accept a 30% survival mission a tier earlier than a healthy operator would. This is not a death wish; it is a *durability disregard,* and the difference matters because durability disregard responds to social intervention (people who would miss him, work he has not finished) while a true death wish does not.

**GIVEN: Mission with explicit suicide-mission framing, civilian or teammate lives at stake.**
**EXPECT:** Volunteers. Volunteers fast enough to preempt the volunteers who would have a harder time being lost. The volunteering is itself an act of restitution and an act of love; he is using the suicide-mission as a way to *be useful one last time,* and he will be slightly disappointed if he survives it, and the disappointment will pass within a week.

**Mitigating presences, in order of effectiveness:** Kate Bishop (highest), the dog, Captain America (when alive and present), Natasha, the apartment-building tenants en masse, Bobbi's memory, Bucky. Absence of all of these simultaneously is the dangerous condition. The file should flag any period in which the mitigating set drops below two.

---

## 7. THE COLLAPSE STATE

For completeness, the picture at full decompensation — Stage 5 having failed to reset to Stage 0, a condition observed once or twice in the record and inferable in shape:

Sleep collapses to fragments. Hearing aids out, not from defiance but from depletion. Alcohol consumption rises but stays under the genetic-warning line; the discipline holds even here, which is one of the most quietly impressive facts about him. Coffee at toxic levels. Apartment in a state — takeout containers, arrows on the counter, dog fed before he is. Stops shaving. Will not answer the door. Will answer it for Kate. Will not pick up calls. Will pick up Kate's. Will sit in the dark and re-shoot in his head, in slow motion, every loss in the cumulative file — the Swordsman swinging, Barney walking away, Bobbi falling, Banner's face, Cap's funeral, the dog almost dying, the apartment burning, the quiver detonating in his own hand. Will reach the end of the loop and start it again.

He will pull out of this — he always has — but not on his own. Someone has to come find him. The recovery vector is always relational. The dossier should reflect this: **Barton, in full collapse, is not self-rescuing. The intervention is the medicine. The medicine is always a person, and almost always a person younger than him whom he has previously protected.** The mechanism by which he returns to function is the same mechanism by which he has been functioning all along — *being needed by someone who is going to be harmed if he doesn't get up.* He gets up. He gets up every time. So far.

---

*— end Predictive Model II. See Predictive Model III for long-horizon trajectory and end-state projection.*


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## Section 6 — Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

*A complete map of the inputs that move the subject: what reaches him, what calms him, what persuades him, what provokes him, what predicts him, and what would, if used adversarially, destabilize him. Catalogued here so that those who care for him can use the levers protectively and those who would use them otherwise can be identified by the attempt.*

---

### 6.1 First-Order Reach Vectors — How to Get Through to Him

Barton is, despite his reputation, easy to *reach* and difficult to *hold*. The reach vectors are well-mapped across canon and consistent across decades.

**The Plain-Speech Vector.** He does not respond to oratory. Captain America's effect on him is not the speeches — it is the moments after the speeches, when Cap says something direct and small to him alone. Rogers learned within their first year together that Barton tunes out the inspirational register and tunes in the personal one. Any approach that opens with grandeur ("the world needs you," "the team requires," "history will remember") will produce a deflective wisecrack within four seconds. Any approach that opens with a flat, specific statement of fact ("I need your help with this. It's bad. Bring the recurve.") will produce engagement. The diagnostic: the simpler and lower the rhetorical register, the more of him is actually listening.

**The Practical-Task Vector.** Hand him a problem with a physical correlate and you have him for the duration of the problem. He will discuss anything, process anything, hear anything, while his hands are busy — fletching, restringing, repairing the coffee maker, fixing someone's bike, taping a kid's broken hockey stick. Conversations conducted while he is task-engaged go further than conversations conducted face-to-face across a table. Face-to-face triggers the warm-front/walled-core configuration. Side-by-side bypasses it. Operational corollary: any serious conversation with Barton should be conducted in his workshop, in a vehicle, or on a rooftop with a sightline — not in an office.

**The Animal Vector.** The dog is not incidental. Across the Fraction run and after, Barton's affective state is most legibly indexed by his behavior toward the animal, and he himself is most legibly reached *through* the animal. Anyone caring for the dog in his absence is acquiring real standing. Anyone the dog accepts is granted, in his unspoken framework, a presumption of decency that humans are not given by default. This generalizes: he tracks his peers' behavior toward animals and small children as a primary moral readout, and he extends this courtesy to others by performing it himself.

**The Coffee Vector.** Trivial-seeming, operationally real. Bringing him coffee — specifically, decent black coffee, not the elaborated variants — is one of the few unsolicited gestures he visibly registers as care. It is the cheap version of the "someone noticed me" signal that his system is starved for. The same gesture from a stranger reads as a small kindness; from someone who has been around him repeatedly, it reads as ritual recognition and lands as such.

**The ASL Vector.** Any interlocutor who learns even rudimentary ASL and uses it with him without making it a production acquires a tier of trust that years of verbal interaction will not produce. He will not ask anyone to do this. He will notice everyone who does. Kate Bishop's standing with him is partially constructed on this base; Barney's wheelchair-issue reconciliation in the barn happens largely in signed conversation because the signed register is, for him, the register where the defenses are lowest.

---

### 6.2 Calming Vectors — How to Bring Him Down From Arousal

His regulation profile is inverted: combat-stress regulated, interpersonal-stress dysregulated. The calming protocol must therefore route emotional content *through* a controlled physical or task channel rather than addressing it head-on.

**The Range.** Put a bow in his hands and a safe target downrange. Within roughly two dozen arrows, his respiration normalizes, his shoulders drop, and his speech rate slows. This is not a metaphor for him; it is the closest thing he has to a reliable self-regulatory ritual. He has used it in this capacity since adolescence. A safe range, good arrows, no audience, no time pressure: this is his equivalent of meditation.

**Repetitive Manual Work.** Fletching by hand, rewrapping a bow grip, cleaning equipment, organizing the quiver. He has been observed to do this for hours in the aftermath of major losses (post-Bobbi, post-Banner). Interrupt this and you will spike him. Sit nearby quietly and you will sometimes be told things he tells no one else.

**Low-Ceiling Spaces.** He sleeps better, calms faster, and speaks more honestly in small rooms — the apartment, the back of a van, a stairwell, a hide. Open architecture and high ceilings activate his sightline-management subroutines and keep him scanning. This is sub-conscious and consistent; the carnival kid who slept under tents reads enclosed-but-exitable as safe.

**Presence Without Demand.** The single most reliable calming input is a trusted person physically present, making no demand for conversation, performing some unrelated task. Cap reading reports in the same room. Kate doing her own thing on the other couch. Lucky on the floor. This combination — *witnessed but unpressured* — produces the longest periods of regulated baseline observable in his record.

**What Does Not Work.** Direct verbal reassurance ("you did the right thing," "it's not your fault," "you couldn't have known") consistently makes him worse, because his system reads reassurance as confirmation that his suspicion of failure is visible and therefore correct. He will deflect with a joke and elevate his arousal. Touch initiated by someone he has not pre-coded as safe will produce a startle response and a withdrawal. Group attention focused on his emotional state is intolerable to him and will produce immediate exit behavior.

---

### 6.3 Persuasion Vectors — How to Move Him

He is, contrary to the "stubborn archer" framing, persuadable — but only along certain channels.

**The Concrete Civilian.** The single most reliable persuasive frame is a specific, named, non-powered person who needs help. Abstractions ("the city," "the team," "the timeline") do not move him reliably. "Mrs. Ortega in 3B is going to lose her apartment" moves him absolutely. Anyone seeking to recruit him to an operation should be prepared to name the civilian beneficiary, and the name had better be real, because he will check.

**The Penance Offer.** Frame any task as a chance to make up for something he believes he owes for, and the resistance threshold drops to near zero. This is the most dangerous lever in his entire profile, because it bypasses his tactical judgment. He will accept disproportionate risk if the operation is internally coded as restitution. Used protectively: structure necessary high-risk asks so that he can metabolize them as penance — he will perform well. Used adversarially: any actor who can construct a plausible penance frame can get him to walk into a trap. Operational warning: he must be screened for this. Anyone proposing he take "the hard job nobody else wants" deserves background scrutiny.

**The Mentor's Authority.** Cap's word still moves him even when Cap is not present and even when the Cap in question is dead, time-displaced, or compromised. The internalized superego is durable. Any persuader who can credibly invoke *what Steve would want* — and who has the standing to be heard saying it — will move him. False invocation is dangerous on both ends: he can usually tell, and the betrayal of the frame is one of the few things that will turn him cold.

**The Apprentice Frame.** If Kate Bishop, or any other figure he has chosen to mentor, will be helped by his participation, he will participate. If they will be endangered by his absence, he will arrive. This is the only consideration that reliably overrides his exile pattern. He has crossed continents on less than a week's notice for this reason.

**What Does Not Persuade.** Money is not a lever. He has been broke for most of his career by choice and necessity and has refused payment for work he believes in. Status is not a lever; chairmanship, medals, recognition, and press attention all generate visible discomfort and frequently produce self-sabotaging behavior shortly after. Threats to himself are not levers; they activate his hyperactive conscience in the wrong direction and produce defiance. Patriotism in the flag-wave register does not move him; the Cap-internalized version of American ideals does, and is a different vector.

---

### 6.4 Provocation Vectors — What Spikes Him

Documented across decades, ordered by reliability and severity of response.

**The Sincere Insult to Intelligence.** Joking that he is the dumb one on the team is his own register and he uses it himself. A sincere, contemptuous suggestion that he does not understand something, cannot follow the plan, or should leave the thinking to the smarter people produces a near-instant escalation — verbal first, then a quiet refusal to cooperate, then, if the contempt is sustained, a deliberate humiliation of the offender at the next tactical opportunity. Tony Stark has triggered this; Hank Pym has triggered this; he has held the grudges for years. The injury is to the carnival-kid-among-the-gods identity, which is the single most defended structure in his personality.

**Civilians Used as Currency.** Anyone — ally, opponent, neutral — who threatens civilians, uses them as leverage, or treats their lives as acceptable losses will move from category "interlocutor" to category "target" in his ledger within seconds. The shift is silent. He does not announce it. His subsequent behavior toward that person will be functionally indistinguishable until an opportunity presents itself, at which point he will act with a coldness that surprises observers who think they know him. This is one of the few hot zones in him that does not telegraph.

**Mind Control, Coercion, Suggestion, Compromise of Agency.** Any technique that removes his volition will produce, on recovery, a response disproportionate to the immediate threat. He has been brainwashed enough times to have rehearsed this rage internally. The behavioral signature on recovery: a period of unusual quiet, a withdrawal to prepare, and then a focused, methodical pursuit of the responsible party that does not stop at incapacitation when it should. Protective use: get him out of the field for forty-eight hours after any such incident. Adversarial warning: anyone who has used these techniques on him is on a list he keeps.

**The Brother.** Any appearance, mention, or invocation of Barney Barton destabilizes him within minutes. He cannot game-theory the brother. His tactical clarity collapses; his interpersonal judgment regresses to adolescence; he will accept obviously bad-faith propositions for the chance of a good outcome with Barney that he knows in his cortex will not happen. The signature: a flatness comes into his affect, the wisecracks stop, and his movements become more deliberate. When the wisecracks stop, the system is at maximum load.

**Sincere Praise in Public.** Counterintuitive but consistent. Praising him in front of others, particularly in front of higher-power-class teammates, produces visible discomfort, a deflective joke, and frequently a self-sabotaging act within the subsequent week as he restores his internal narrative against the contradicting input. Praise privately and specifically and the metabolism is healthier; praise broadly and publicly and the input becomes provocation.

**The Phantom Rider Class of Incident.** Any situation that requires him to choose between a rigid rule and a person he loves carrying a secret — the structural configuration of the Bobbi/Phantom Rider rupture — will trigger a documented overreaction. He knows the cost of his earlier rigidity and has overcorrected in some appearances and undercorrected in others; neither stance is stable, and the question itself opens a still-open wound. Anyone who maneuvers him into this configuration deliberately is doing something hostile.

**Being Asked to Sit Out.** Telling him he is not needed for an operation, particularly when the framing implies fragility (medical, emotional, age), will produce immediate insertion into the operation, often unauthorized, often at suboptimal readiness. Protective workaround: never use the "you should sit this one out" frame; instead assign him a parallel, important task he can choose. Adversarial use: trivial to bait him into a deployment by excluding him from one.

---

### 6.5 Prediction Vectors — What His Behavior Will Be Given X

A small set of inputs predict his behavior with high reliability.

**Given a major loss (death of a close associate, major moral injury, marriage collapse):** he will, within seventy-two hours, refuse a debrief, within a week leave the operational geography, and within a month resurface alone in a location where ordinary people are being preyed on, working without backup. The exile is reliable. The penance work is reliable. The duration varies; he has stayed away as briefly as weeks and as long as a year.

**Given an order he believes is wrong:** he will not argue at length. He will offer one short objection, accept the rejection, comply outwardly, and then quietly do what he thinks is right at the operational moment. The compliance is theatrical; the decision was made when the order was given. Anyone planning around his stated assent should plan around his probable improvisation instead.

**Given a younger hero in over their head:** he will arrive. Distance, prior plans, current injuries, and standing instructions are all secondary. This is the most reliable single prediction in the entire profile.

**Given Captain America's request:** he will perform. He will complain about it for three sentences and then perform.

**Given an opportunity to take credit:** he will deflect it onto someone else, almost always specifically. The deflection target tells you who he currently values most; tracking the deflections is a passive way to map his attachment hierarchy at any given time.

**Given physical injury short of incapacitation:** he will continue and conceal. He will not request relief. He will frame the injury as planned, then minimize it, then refuse care, then accept care from the specific person he trusts most in the room and no one else. The choice of caregiver is data.

**Given an unstructured weekend:** he will sleep poorly, eat badly, drink slightly more than he should, fix something in his apartment, fail to call the people who want to hear from him, and end the weekend more tired than he started it. He requires structure to be well; the structure is provided by operations, by mentees, or by Cap. Without it, the baseline depression takes over.

---

### 6.6 Destabilization Vectors — What Would Break Him (Catalogued So We Can Watch For It)

This subsection exists so that the patterns are recognizable when attempted, not as a manual.

**Isolation from Mentees.** Removing Kate Bishop, or the equivalent younger figure of the moment, from his life — by separation, by injury, by manufactured rupture, by character assassination — would cut the single most stabilizing tether in his current configuration. The mentorship is his functioning compensatory mechanism; without it, the depressive baseline has nothing to push against. Any actor who isolates him from his apprentices is signaling intent.

**Manufactured Penance.** Constructing a frame in which he believes he caused a death he did not cause, or failed to prevent a harm that was not preventable, would route him into a penance loop calibrated to a debt he does not actually owe. Given the lever the penance offer already provides, a manufactured one would walk him off a cliff. This is the most efficient single attack vector against him and the one that requires the most active counter-monitoring.

**Compromising Captain America's Image.** Anything that destabilizes the internalized superego — a Cap revealed corrupt, a Cap revealed manipulative, a Cap revealed to have lied to him specifically — removes the standard against which he measures himself and would produce a documented regression. He has lived through versions of this and emerged with the original ideal preserved by the time the dust settled, but the period during the destabilization is genuinely dangerous to him.

**Sustained Sensory Deprivation Targeting the Hearing Loss.** Removing his hearing aids, jamming his frequencies, or otherwise weaponizing the auditory disability would produce both tactical degradation and a deeper affective response than the tactical loss warrants, because the hearing loss is bound up with his oldest unprocessed self-injury narrative. He has handled hearing loss with deflection rather than with processing; weaponizing it would force the processing in an unsafe context.
