**The Brother Operationalized.** A sufficiently sophisticated adversary could use Barney — willing or coerced — as a delivery vehicle for almost any other attack. He has never built defenses against this and may not be capable of building them. Protective implication: any approach by or through Barney requires independent verification before he is allowed to act on it. He will not perform this verification himself.

**Slow Erosion of the Apartment-Building Class of Attachment.** His Bed-Stuy-era attachments to a building of ordinary tenants is replicated structurally across his career — there is always some equivalent local commitment. Systematic destruction of the local-civilian attachment object, repeatedly, would teach him that the small-scale protection work he has organized his moral life around is futile. He has been close to this lesson and has not fully absorbed it; full absorption would remove drive #2 from his motivational stack, which would in turn destabilize drive #1, which is the load-bearing column.

**Forced Inactivity.** Confinement, medical grounding, formal suspension, house arrest. The action-as-avoidance defense requires action; remove action and the avoided content surfaces without an outlet. Extended inactivity produces escalating depressive presentation and increases the probability of impulsive self-endangering action upon release. Any necessary grounding must be paired with structured task substitution — coaching, training, mentorship — or it will harm him.

---

### 6.7 Tells — Reading His Internal State From the Outside

The diagnostic micro-signals, catalogued so that those around him can read him without asking him, since asking him will produce the deflection rather than the truth.

**The Wisecrack Rate.** Baseline: moderate, evenly spaced, often genuinely funny. Elevation: frequency increases and content sharpens — sarcasm rises, self-deprecation rises, the jokes target him specifically. This is stage-one escalation. **When the wisecracks stop entirely, the system is at maximum load.** Silence in him is not calm; silence is the late stage.

**The Shoulder Carriage.** When regulated, his shoulders are dropped and loose; he moves with the looseness of a trained athlete at rest. Under load, the right shoulder — the draw shoulder — rises first, by perhaps half an inch. Under heavier load, both shoulders rise and the head tilts fractionally forward. Combat readiness and emotional dysregulation present the same way physically; the context disambiguates.

**The Equipment Check.** When uncertain, anxious, or processing, he will check his quiver, his bracer, his bowstring — repeatedly, without need. This is a self-soothing behavior disguised as professionalism. Frequency above twice per minute indicates active distress.

**The Coffee Cup.** He drinks his coffee fast when content and slow when ruminating. A cup held untouched while he stares at middle distance indicates active intrusive recall. Do not interrupt; sit nearby; wait.

**The Apartment State.** His personal environment indexes his state with high fidelity. Reasonable order: regulated. Pizza boxes accumulating, dog underfed-but-not-starving, mail unopened, television on with the sound off: depressive episode in progress. Apartment unusually clean and organized in a way that does not match his baseline: he is about to do something he believes might be his last act, and is putting his affairs in order without telling anyone. The pre-mission cleaning is a serious warning sign and has preceded multiple high-risk solo deployments.

**The Departure Behavior.** When he intends to leave for an extended exile, he gives small unprompted gifts in the preceding days — a piece of equipment to a teammate, a meaningful object to a mentee, the dog to a trusted caretaker for "a few days." Anyone receiving an unexpected, slightly sentimental gift from him should treat it as a flag and check his planned movements.

**The Sleep Pattern.** When sleeping on the couch with the television on, baseline-depressive but stable. When sleeping in his bed, unusually regulated. When not sleeping at all and visible for thirty-six-plus hours at high function, an episode is metastasizing and a crash is coming within seventy-two.

**The Address.** He calls people he is comfortable with by short forms or by names only he uses. He calls people he is wary of by their full names or titles. A shift from short-form to formal address in a previously close relationship indicates a fracture has occurred that he has not yet announced.

**The Sightlines.** In any new space, within the first thirty seconds he has identified the exits, the high points, and the available improvised weapons. This is constant and unconscious. The diagnostic is when it *stops* — when he enters a space and does not perform the scan, he is either profoundly safe (rare) or profoundly compromised (medically, emotionally, chemically). The absence of the scan is more informative than its presence.

---

### 6.8 Protective Use — A Standing Set of Recommendations

For those around him whose orientation is care rather than exploitation, the levers above support a small set of standing practices.

Keep a mentee in his life at all times; the structure he provides others is the structure that holds him. Verify any penance frame independently before allowing him to act on it; the lever is too easily abused, including by himself. Conduct serious conversations side-by-side and task-engaged, not face-to-face. Bring coffee. Learn ASL. Do not praise him publicly; praise him privately and specifically and rarely. Do not tell him to sit it out; offer him a parallel task instead. After any loss, expect exile; do not pursue him during it, but do leave the door visibly open for return — the open door is what he is checking for, even when he is not looking. Watch the wisecrack rate, the apartment state, and the gift-giving behavior. When the apartment is too clean and the gifts have started, intervene immediately and without subtlety; this is the window in which he is most reachable and most at risk. Never let him hear, from any source, the suggestion that he is not needed; he believes it already and the confirmation will land harder than any of us would predict.

He is held together, in significant part, by the people who have learned to read him. The file exists, in this section, to expand that group.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU ANALYTICAL DOSSIER: BARTON, CLINTON FRANCIS
## Section 6 — Strengths, Assets & Resilience

A surveillance file that catalogues only the wounds misreads the subject. Barton is, by any honest accounting, one of the most durable operators in the enhanced-individuals population — not because he is hard to break (he breaks regularly) but because he is structurally hard to *keep* broken. The asset ledger below is exhaustive because the asset ledger is, in his case, the explanation for his survival. Sixty years of published activity, six confirmed cycles of catastrophic collapse, and the man is still on the board. That requires accounting for.

---

### 6.1 PRIMARY CRAFT ASSET — Marksmanship and Trajectory Cognition

**Baseline capability.** Subject is documented, repeatedly and across writers, as the finest marksman on Earth with a projectile weapon — a claim he has defended on-panel against Bullseye, Taskmaster (whose photographic-reflex powerset specifically targets this domain), and Green Arrow analogues across imprint crossovers. The phrase "never misses" is used loosely in canon; the more accurate operational descriptor is that **he never misses a shot he has decided to take**, which is not the same claim and is the more important one. He aborts shots routinely. The discipline is in the abort, not the loose.

**Granular substrate of the skill.** What looks like supernatural aim is, on close examination, an integrated suite of:

- **Pre-conscious ballistic computation.** He solves drop, drift, target velocity, and Coriolis-trivial corrections in the time it takes him to draw — sub-second. Tested in *Hawkeye* (Fraction) sequences where he calls a trick shot mid-fall and lands it. This is overlearned through tens of thousands of repetitions dating to the carnival period (ages ~8–17, daily training under Trick Shot and Swordsman).
- **Peripheral target acquisition.** He shoots accurately at targets he has not directly fixated, working from peripheral cues and short-term spatial memory. Demonstrated in the "shoot without looking" sequences and in his ability to fire behind himself off reflective surfaces.
- **Proprioceptive draw consistency.** Every draw lands at identical anchor point (corner of mouth, knuckle to jaw), every release follows identical follow-through. Variance at the bowstring measured in millimeters across thousands of shots. This is what produces the apparent infallibility — the system is mechanically pre-zeroed.
- **Object-as-projectile generalization.** The skill is **weapon-agnostic**. He has thrown playing cards, coins, paperclips, cutlery, his own hearing aid, and improvised debris with effective targeting. The bow is not the skill; the skill is the body's predictive model of a thrown mass through air, and the bow is its most efficient interface.

**Diagnostic point.** Most elite shooters degrade under stress, fatigue, or injury. Barton's accuracy is documented as *stable or improved* under combat stress. The skill has been encoded in the brain regions least vulnerable to interference — cerebellar and basal ganglia automaticity rather than cortical deliberation. He shoots better wounded than rested, which is a tell about how the skill was originally trained (under abuse, in pain, with the requirement to perform regardless of state).

---

### 6.2 SECONDARY PHYSICAL ASSETS

- **Acrobatic and gymnastic baseline.** Carnival-trained. Equal-bars, trapeze, tumbling, high-fall recovery. Allows him to operate as a mobility-asset on team compositions otherwise dependent on flight or super-strength. His insertion approaches characteristically involve rooftops, fire escapes, and elevation gradients exploited gymnastically.
- **Hand-to-hand competence.** Multi-disciplinary, derived ad hoc from training partners across his career: Captain America (boxing-based striking, shield-influenced footwork), Black Widow (Systema-derived joint work, knife defense), Mockingbird (her own bostaff-anchored hybrid), occasional Iron Fist exposure. He is not a peer to specialists, but he holds his own against most enhanced individuals at melee range by virtue of pattern-recognition speed.
- **Visual acuity.** Repeatedly described as 20/10 or better; depicted reading text and identifying faces at ranges that strain civilian optics. Whether this is a metahuman threshold or extreme natural endowment is unresolved in canon; functionally, it is an unfair advantage and he treats it as such.
- **Pain tolerance.** Extreme. Operational while bearing injuries that would hospitalize most agents. Mixed asset — see Section 2 — but in the field, durable.
- **Recovery speed.** Anomalously fast for a non-augmented human. Whether this is a residue of Wandian restoration (the *House of M* reconstitution), a quiet metahuman edge never acknowledged, or simply the conditioning of someone who has practiced healing as much as he has practiced hurting, is academic. The operational fact: he is back on a roof inside two weeks of a back broken in three places.

---

### 6.3 TACTICAL AND COGNITIVE ASSETS

**Improvisational planning.** His signature cognitive asset. He generates serviceable plans in seconds from sub-optimal materials. The "trick arrow" inventory is the visible expression of an invisible habit of mind — *what does this room contain that I could use?* This generalizes outside combat: he is unusually good at improvising shelter, food, transport, and cover identity from local resources. Carnival origin again — a kid who slept rough learns to read environments for affordances.

**Threat triage under load.** Demonstrated capacity to track six-plus moving threats in a fluid engagement and rank them correctly by danger and reachability. This is rarer than civilian intuition credits; most elite combatants can manage three or four. His ceiling appears to be around eight before degradation.

**Leadership — actual, evidenced.** The West Coast Avengers record is the data point that the "dumb archer" framing is intended to suppress. Across the Englehart/Byrne/Thomas run he:
- recruited a roster of difficult personalities (Wonder Man's vanity, Tigra's impulse control, Vision's alienation, Wanda's grief, and later USAgent's outright hostility) and produced functioning team cohesion;
- managed a budget and a physical compound;
- maintained liaison with East Coast Avengers and government oversight;
- ran field operations as on-scene commander;
- and conducted post-mission debriefs that, when depicted, are competent and pedagogically sound.

The framing he prefers — that he was in over his head — is contradicted by the record. He led for five years and his team survived him. Few Avengers chairs can say the same.

**Mentorship capacity.** Distinct from leadership. He is among the most effective teachers in the population, evidenced longitudinally with Kate Bishop, intermittently with America Chavez, with younger Young Avengers cohorts, and informally with civilians. His teaching style is observable: he models, lets the student fail safely, debriefs without humiliation, and re-models. This is precisely the pedagogy he was denied by Swordsman and Trick Shot. He has reverse-engineered, from his own wounds, a functional opposite. Diagnostically: the most healed part of him is the part that teaches.

**Reading people.** Underrated. He spent his formative years in a carnival, an environment that trains rapid threat-assessment of strangers as a survival skill. He can clock a mark, a fellow operator, or a civilian-in-distress within seconds and adjust register accordingly. He is bad at reading people who love him (defensive blindness), and excellent at reading everyone else.

---

### 6.4 RESOURCE ASSETS

- **Equipment inventory.** Bow (compound primary, recurve secondary, take-down tertiary for concealment). Quiver of specialized arrowheads — explosive, EMP, sonic, putty, net, grappling, tracking, smoke, flashbang, acid, cryogenic, hallucinogenic, electrical, biometric-coded, parachute, boomerang, putty-deploying, sound-suppressing. The catalogue is canonically deep enough that *he himself* has lost track in-issue. Maintained personally; he does not outsource fletching, which is both an asset (no supply-chain compromise vector) and a self-isolation tell.
- **Safehouse network.** Modest by Avengers standards but real. Bed-Stuy apartment (the building he owns, after Fraction's run). A farm property associated with the family establishing in the *Ultimates*-influenced canon (in the prime continuity, the farm tradition is intermittent). At least two carnival-era contacts maintained as bolt-holes. Various unsanctioned crash points across the Avengers' global network that he treats as available.
- **Institutional credentials.** Active Avengers status, SHIELD clearance (historically high, periodically revoked), familiarity with multiple national-security entities through cross-pollinated missions. He has the access of a senior operator and the temperament that periodically loses it.
- **Financial.** Modest. He has never accumulated wealth. This is both vulnerability and asset: he is unbuyable, unblackmailable on financial pressure, and operationally lean. His footprint is small.
- **Social capital.** Vast and undervalued by him. The number of senior heroes who will pick up his call without question — Cap, Natasha, Wanda, Stark when not feuding, T'Challa, Strange in extremis, the Fantastic Four collectively, half the X-Men through Wanda-adjacency — is a function not of his power level but of decades of reliability and the absence of any record of betrayal of trust on his part. He does not believe he has this capital. He has it anyway.

---

### 6.5 RESILIENCE FACTORS — Why He Stays Functional

This is the analytically important subsection. A man with his trauma load should be non-operational. He is operational. The mechanisms:

**1. Humor as load-bearing infrastructure.** Section 3 frames the wisecracking as a defense, which it is. It is also an *asset*. The continuous self-deprecating chatter accomplishes work: it discharges affect in small increments rather than allowing accumulation to critical mass; it signals to allies that he is functional and to enemies that he is unbothered (both partially false, both tactically useful); it maintains his own access to language under stress, which is correlated with continued executive function. Operators who go silent under pressure are more likely to dissociate. Barton talks. The talking is the tell that he is still in the room.

**2. Craft as anchor.** The bow is daily ritual. He shoots when he wakes, between calls, before sleep. The repetition is regulatory in a quasi-meditative sense — it is the one activity in which prediction matches outcome reliably enough to produce coherent self-experience. A man whose relationships have all distorted his self-model can reset that model against a target at known distance. This is closer to monastic practice than to athletic training, and it is doing the work most people get from therapy.

**3. The mentorship loop.** Teaching Kate, teaching the kid heroes, teaching the civilians who knock on his door — each instance reverses the original injury. He is not just helping them; he is rebuilding, in real time, the developmental scaffolding he never received. The asset is renewable: students keep arriving.

**4. Captain America as internalized object.** Even with Steve dead, depowered, replaced, or otherwise off-map, the *standard* persists. Clint refers to it without naming it. It is a portable superego that does not require Cap's physical presence to function. Most operators who lose their referent figure decompensate; Clint installed his referent figure permanently around 1965 and the install has held.

**5. Selective amnesia about social capital.** He genuinely does not register how many people would mobilize for him. This is psychologically painful and operationally useful — he doesn't lean on the network, so the network doesn't tire of him. The capital compounds because he refuses to spend it.

**6. The local-stakes commitment.** The apartment building, the neighbors, the dog — these are not just compensatory altruism. They are **scale-appropriate** to his actual emotional bandwidth. Cosmic stakes overwhelm him affectively; one building, one dog, one apprentice he can hold. The deliberate scaling-down of his moral universe to manageable units is itself a resilience strategy, even if he would not articulate it that way.

**7. Working-class identity stability.** Where the rest of his self-concept is unstable and negative, his class identity is stable and unapologetic. He is the carnie kid, he speaks like the carnie kid, he eats like the carnie kid, he furnishes his apartment like the carnie kid. This stable axis of identification holds the rest of the self together. Operators with no stable self-axis fragment. Barton has exactly one, and it suffices.

**8. The dog.** Operationally trivial, psychologically significant. The acquisition and keeping of Lucky (Pizza Dog) — a damaged animal he chose to rehabilitate — externalizes the work of caretaking onto a daily, embodied object. Petting the dog, feeding the dog, walking the dog: these are basic regulatory acts that anchor circadian rhythm and tactile soothing in a life otherwise devoid of both. Veterinary intelligence services would note the dog as a stabilizing variable; this analyst concurs.

**9. ASL acquisition.** Late but real. Faced with progressive hearing loss, he learned a language rather than retreating from communication. The learning curve was undignified and he documented it through Kate. The asset is twofold: practical communication redundancy, and the demonstrated capacity — rare in him — to acquire a new competence in adulthood through humility. It is the most adult thing on his ledger.

**10. The capacity to receive care from the very young or the very damaged.** He cannot receive care from peers (see Section 3). He *can* receive care from Kate, from the dog, from his neighbors, from his deaf landlord, from broken people who need him in turn. The asymmetric-care exchange is a workaround for his counter-dependence, and it is sufficient. He gets fed. He gets checked on. He is not as alone as he thinks he is, and the structure that keeps him that way is one he stumbled into and has the wisdom not to disturb.

---

### 6.6 META-ASSETS — Properties of the System, Not Items in It

**Failure tolerance.** He has failed publicly and privately on a scale most operators would not survive professionally or psychologically. He keeps reporting for duty. The metabolic capacity to absorb shame, hold it without externalizing it onto others, and return to the work is uncommon and undervalued. It is what makes him deployable on missions with high probability of moral compromise — he will carry the cost rather than displace it.

**Moral consistency under temptation.** Across sixty years of canon, he has been offered power upgrades, criminal alliances, cosmic promotions, and easier lives, and has declined them with a regularity that approaches reflex. Bribery, in the broad sense, does not work on him. The asset is durable because the motivation is intrinsic — he is not refusing because he calculated the refusal; he is refusing because the offers do not register as desirable to the part of him that decides.

**Calibrated cowardice.** Worth naming directly. He is afraid in the right amounts at the right times. He flinches from cosmic horror, from gods, from his brother. He does not flinch from gunmen, from tracksuit goons, from his own pain. This calibration — fear allocated correctly — is what keeps him alive on missions where reckless men die. The bravado is performance; the underlying threat-assessment is sober.

**Pattern-recognition of his own decompensation.** Imperfect but present. He knows, by the third stage of his five-stage escalation, that he is escalating. He often chooses to escalate anyway, but the metacognition is intact. This means the system is recoverable — he is not in denial about the cycle, he is in *negotiation* with it. That negotiation is the difference between a man who will eventually find a way out and a man who will not. The file's assessment is that Barton, given enough time and one or two more arrivals at the bottom of the cycle, may yet find the way out. The resilience assets above are what will keep him alive until he does.

---

**Summary judgment for the asset ledger.** Subject's strengths are not, in the aggregate, the strengths the public file emphasizes. The marksmanship is real and elite, but it is the least diagnostically interesting of his assets. The diagnostically interesting assets are the humor-as-infrastructure, the mentorship loop, the class-identity anchor, the dog, the ASL, the calibrated cowardice, and the metacognitive negotiation with his own collapse cycle. Together these constitute a resilience architecture that has carried a man through trauma loads that should have ended him five times over. The architecture is unglamorous, partially unconscious, and held together with what one of his apprentices once called duct tape and pizza. It works. It has worked for forty in-universe years. It will, on current trajectory, continue to work.

He is more durable than he is dangerous, and he is very dangerous. The file should be read accordingly.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# 6. FAILURE MODES & DECOMPENSATION

## 6.1 Baseline and the Definition of "Failure"

A note on terms before the mapping. For most subjects, "decompensation" denotes a discrete deviation from a stable baseline — the moment the structure cracks. Subject Barton presents an inverted problem: **his baseline is already a low-grade decompensation held in functional shape by craft, humor, and assigned mission**. He does not break from health into illness; he breaks from a managed depressive equilibrium into a more acute and dangerous configuration of the same illness. Failure, in his case, is therefore not a discontinuity but a phase transition along an axis he is always already on.

This has a critical operational implication: **the warning signs are not departures from his behavior but intensifications of it**. He does not start drinking when he decompensates; he drinks the same and sleeps less. He does not start cracking jokes; the jokes sharpen and acquire a particular bitter timbre. He does not become reckless; the existing tolerance for risk recalibrates downward by a measurable but easily-missed increment. An observer looking for a "change in behavior" will miss the collapse until it is two stages along. An observer who has indexed his actual baseline — coffee at 0500, three quips per hostile encounter, bow maintained nightly, sleep ~5 hours non-contiguous, average self-injury per op: moderate — can detect Stage 1 within 48 hours.

## 6.2 The Five-Stage Escalation Path

The pattern is canonical and has run, by conservative count from published material, at least six times: post-Phantom Rider/Mockingbird (1989-90), post-Mockingbird-death (1993-94), pre-Disassembled (2004), post-resurrection/Ronin assumption (2005-07), Fraction-run baseline collapse (2013-14), post-Banner (2016-17), Freefall episode (2020). It is consistent enough to be considered procedural.

### Stage 1 — Verbal Drift (T+0 to T+72hrs from precipitating event)

The first detectable signal is in **the jokes**. His humor floor lowers. The self-deprecation, which at baseline functions as social lubricant and affect-management, develops a sincerity edge — the listener begins to suspect, correctly, that he means it. A specific tell: he begins to volunteer mortality-referenced humor unprompted ("if I make it to Tuesday," "assuming I'm still alive for that," "well, when I'm dead"). At baseline he uses this language reactively, in response to a setup; at Stage 1 he supplies it without one. Frequency increases roughly threefold.

Secondary verbal markers: shortening of sentences in field communication, reduced banter on comms, increased use of acknowledgment grunts in lieu of confirmation phrases. With Kate Bishop, the marker is different — he becomes **more solicitous of her**, asks about her cases, deflects her questions about him with a competence-praise pivot ("you've got this, you don't need me on it"). This is the Stage 1 fingerprint with the one person he cannot fully camouflage to.

Somatic: coffee intake doubles. Sleep cycle, already poor, fractures further; the couch displaces the bed entirely. Bow maintenance — normally a nightly ritual approaching the devotional — is performed but compressed; he skips the slow-tuning portion and does only string and limb. Dog (Lucky, when present) gets walked but not played with.

### Stage 2 — Task Encapsulation (T+72hrs to T+2wks)

He commits, hard, to a discrete operational problem and uses it as a container. The problem chosen is almost always **local, small-stakes, and against opponents he can comfortably out-fight** — the Tracksuit Draculas, a single warehouse, a corrupt local figure, a missing-persons case in a single zip code. The diagnostic feature is the *mismatch* between the resources he applies and the stakes: a global-tier operative running surveillance, planning, and progressive force-escalation against a Brooklyn rent dispute is not a tactical choice, it is an emotional one.

Refusal of help becomes explicit and verbal in this stage. He will turn down Avengers backchannel offers, ignore check-in calls (Cap, Natasha, Kate, Bobbi when alive), and answer texts in single-word affirmatives. The phrase **"I've got it"** in any of its grammatical variants becomes the dominant utterance. It functions as both reassurance to the recipient and self-instruction.

He will, in this stage, take on at least one additional protectorate not strictly his responsibility — a neighbor's problem, a stranger's missing kid, an old contact's debt. This is the compensatory machinery running hot: the only way he can metabolize the unprocessed precipitating event is to bank moral credit against it.

Physical signs at Stage 2: visible bruising he does not explain; a limp he denies; the hearing aids come out more often, or stay out longer, depending on which way the avoidance is cutting (out = "I don't want to hear you"; in but turned down = "I want plausible deniability"). Drinking elevates from baseline by a controlled increment — he is watching it — but the increment is real. He begins eating standing up, over the sink, out of containers, at irregular hours.

### Stage 3 — Calculated Self-Endangerment (T+2wks to T+1mo)

The risk tolerance recalibrates and a deliberate, unnecessary risk is taken. This is **not** unplanned recklessness — he is too competent for that, and the planning is visible after the fact. It is risk that he has selected because the worst-case outcome is acceptable to him in a way it would not be at baseline. The marker: **the contingency plans he normally builds are absent or vestigial.** He will enter a building without backup, take a shot without a fallback, accept a meet without overwatch. He will explain this afterward as efficiency, expedience, or a tactical read; the explanation will not survive a competent debrief.

He gets hurt. Frequency and severity of injury in Stage 3 are reliably elevated over baseline. The injuries cluster on the lower body (ankles, knees, hip) and ribs — consistent with falls and impacts, consistent with him taking hits he would normally evade. There is usually one injury per Stage 3 episode that crosses a threshold (hospitalization, surgery, mandatory rest order). He will refuse the rest order or shorten it unilaterally.

A specific verbal tell at this stage, in after-action contexts: he will frame the injury as **the plan**. "That was the play." "That's how it had to go." "Worked out." This is a retrospective restructuring designed to convert the failure of self-protection into intentionality. It deceives no one who knows him; it does not need to. The audience is internal.

### Stage 4 — Exile (T+1mo to T+indefinite)

He physically removes himself. The form varies — leaving the team, leaving the city, "going dark," accepting an off-grid assignment, taking up a new identity — but the function is invariant: **geographic distance as substitute for the psychological work he will not do**. The Ronin assumption after his resurrection is the most pathologized version (literally adopting the identity-marker "masterless"); the Bed-Stuy retreat is the most domestic; the Occupy Avengers tour of the rural margins is the most prosocialized. They are the same act.

Communications behavior in Stage 4 is highly diagnostic. He does not go fully silent — he calls Kate, periodically Cap or Natasha — but the calls are **affect-flat and content-light**, designed to register liveness without inviting inquiry. The intervals lengthen. He will refuse video, accept audio, prefer text. ASL-only with whoever shares it; this is the Stage 4 communication preference because it removes voice as an affective channel.

He acquires, in Stage 4, a small civilian project — coaching a youth league, fixing up a property, training a single apprentice, helping a town with its single concrete problem. He works hard at it and it does help him, somewhat. The work is real. It is also containment: he is using a manageable other-directed task to avoid the unmanageable self-directed one. The project ends — successfully — and he does not improve underneath it.

### Stage 5 — Return Without Resolution (T+variable)

He comes back. He looks better. He has a tan, a calmer affect, a quip ready. The team accepts the return because they want to. Within 4-8 weeks, the same pattern is observable again on a new precipitator: he has not metabolized, he has rested. The reset is real but partial; the underlying load is undischarged and accumulating across cycles. **Each iteration begins from a slightly worse baseline than the last.** This is the longitudinal danger and the thing that is invisible in any single-cycle observation.

## 6.3 Acute Collapse Configurations

The five-stage path describes the typical, chronic decompensation. There are also acute configurations — the things that happen when a precipitator is too large or arrives during an existing decompensation cycle. Three distinct collapse morphologies are observable in the record.

### The Penance Spiral

Triggered by acts he holds himself directly responsible for: the Banner killing in 2016, the Bobbi-Phantom Rider sequence, the apartment building tenants harmed in the Tracksuit war, civilian collateral on a botched op. Mechanism: the Stage 2 task-encapsulation is selected to be *thematically* responsive to the precipitator, and the Stage 3 self-endangerment is calibrated *upward* until the universe either kills him or doesn't.

The diagnostic feature is the **acceptance of injury as currency**. He will absorb hits he could slip because the hit, in the internal accounting, pays down the debt. The Freefall episode (2020) is the cleanest published instance: he runs the cycle compressed into weeks rather than months, and the people around him (Kate explicitly) read it correctly as a slow suicide attempt with deniability. The deniability is structural; he is not consciously trying to die. He is trying to be hurt enough to feel he has paid, and is indifferent to the upper bound on "enough." This is **moral injury operating through somatic ledger**.

### The Loyalty Fracture

Triggered when two of his attachments come into conflict: Cap versus Tony in Civil War (he refused to fight); Bobbi versus the code; Barney versus everyone; institutional Avengers versus a local protectorate. Mechanism: he cannot tolerate the binary, attempts a third-way solution that satisfies neither party, fails, and then withdraws to punish himself for failing both.

The marker here is **uncharacteristic verbal indirection**. He stops giving straight answers. The carnie-kid plain-speech, normally a fixed feature, becomes hedged, deflected, mediated through joke. He will be observed taking unusually long to commit to a side in any subsequent conflict, even small ones. The fracture is to his decision-making confidence, not to his action capacity; he can still execute, he just cannot choose well, and he knows it, and the knowing accelerates the cycle.

### The Brother Collapse

Sui generis. Every Barney Barton appearance produces a destabilization that does not fit the standard five-stage path because the precipitator is also the only person who can short-circuit the defenses. With Barney, the humor stops working — Barney has heard the bits, knows the bits, can name the bits. The task-encapsulation does not engage because Barney *is* the task and Clint cannot bring himself to deploy full operational force against him. Stage 3 collapses into Stage 1; he gets hurt verbally and emotionally before he gets hurt physically, and the physical comes from the depleted state, not from a chosen risk.

The Hawkeye #19 (Fraction/Aja, 2014) presentation is the canonical document: regression to childhood affect, ASL conducted at a pace that suggests both of them are speaking as their younger selves, and the operational competence visibly downgrading by 30-40% for the duration of the encounter. The Brother Collapse is the only mode in which Subject is reliably tactically beatable by opponents below his weight class. **Any hostile actor with access to Barney Barton has a force multiplier against him that no other lever provides.**

## 6.4 Conditions That Produce Collapse

Inventory of precipitators, ranked by reliability of effect:

**Tier 1 — Near-certain triggers:**
- Death of a close attachment, particularly a woman he has loved (Bobbi twice, the Wanda complication, any future analog).
- Captain America expressing disappointment in him (not anger — *disappointment*; the distinction is critical, and Cap, when alive, knows it).
- A child or apprentice under his protection harmed on his watch.
- Being asked to kill, and complying, on terms that he agreed to in advance (Banner template). The pre-consent is what makes it metabolically worse, not better; he cannot route the act through the standard combat-ethics framework.
- Loss of agency through mind control, manipulation, or chemical compromise. He recovers operationally fast and emotionally slow; the residue runs for months.

**Tier 2 — High-probability triggers:**
- Barney Barton, in any configuration: enemy, ally, ambiguous, dying, dead, resurrected.
- Hearing loss progression or hearing-aid failure in field conditions. The disability itself he has accommodated; the *progression* re-traumatizes him by reminding him the body is finite and uncontrolled.
- Public framing as "the useless one" or "the one who shouldn't be here" — particularly if delivered by another hero rather than a civilian or villain. Confirmation from the in-group is what bites.
- Mockingbird, in any of her recurrences. The marriage is unfinished business that no subsequent contact closes.
- Being commanded into a leadership role he did not seek. He is competent at leadership and the competence is the problem — he cannot use the "just the archer" frame to deflect, which means the responsibility lands.

**Tier 3 — Reliable accelerants (will worsen any in-progress cycle):**
- Holidays, particularly any associated with family.
- Anniversaries of canonical losses (Bobbi's death, Cap's death, the carnival period).
- Forced inactivity, including injury rehab and mandated leave. Removing his task-channel removes his primary defense; depressive symptomatology surges within 72 hours of grounding.
- Therapy sessions, paradoxically. Any sustained attempt at processing without his consent or framing produces a counter-decompensation: he will trigger a Stage 2 task-encapsulation specifically to exit the therapy.
- Wealth, status, or recognition. Praise is destabilizing because it conflicts with the self-concept; he will engineer a fall to restore the balance.

## 6.5 Hard-Floor Failure: What Total Collapse Would Look Like

The cycles described above are bounded. The question this section must answer is: **what does Barton look like below the floor?** The published record gives partial answers (the Disassembled death is one form; the Freefall episode another). Extrapolating the trajectory:

Total collapse, were the standard defenses to fail comprehensively, would not present as psychotic break, suicidal ideation in the active-planning sense, or violence-against-others. The structure rules these out — he is too reality-tested, too averse to becoming his father, and his hyperactive conscience would not survive an act of internal-circle harm. What it would present as is **a controlled, deniable, mission-framed terminal exposure**: an op he selects himself, with parameters tuned just past his survival envelope, executed with full competence, framed to all observers (including himself) as the operationally correct choice. He would die well, on task, in a manner that permitted his survivors to read it as heroism rather than what it was. The Disassembled detonation is a draft of this. The Freefall sequence is a draft of this. The pattern is established and the next iteration will be drawn from it.

The countervailing forces against hard-floor collapse are three, and they are the entire reason he is still alive in the record:

1. **Captain America's standard, internalized and persistent even in Cap's absence.** Cap would not approve of the elegant exit. The introject vetoes.
2. **Kate Bishop, who reads the signals correctly and intervenes operationally.** She is the only person in the network who treats the symptoms as symptoms rather than as Clint-being-Clint. Her removal from his life would elevate hard-floor risk by a margin difficult to overstate.
3. **The protectorate.** He cannot exit while there is a building of tenants, a kid, a neighborhood, a stray dog, a fellow veteran depending on him in concrete terms. He will not abandon a post. Any total-collapse scenario therefore requires either the protectorate to be removed from him (loss) or him to be removed from the protectorate (forced separation). Either condition is a five-alarm indicator.

## 6.6 Recovery Pattern and Its Limits

He recovers. Reliably, in the chronic cycle. The recovery mechanism is **time, task, and the slow re-accretion of a small circle of dependents who need him in low-stakes consistent ways**. This is real and it is also the trap. Because the recovery does not require him to process, the recovery confirms to him that processing is not required. Each cycle therefore reinforces the cycle.

The only observed disruption to the cycle is the **Kate Bishop variable** — sustained, peer-adjacent, non-romantic, ASL-fluent, willing to call him on the bits, willing to physically arrive when he goes dark. Her presence does not prevent the cycle but it shortens Stage 4 considerably and improves the baseline of Stage 5 returns. This is the single highest-leverage element in the entire support architecture. **Any intervention plan that does not center the protection and continuity of that relationship is non-serious.**

The longitudinal projection, absent intervention beyond the existing pattern: the cycles will continue, the baseline will continue to drift downward across iterations at a slow but measurable rate, and the probability of the hard-floor exit will compound across decades until the conditions align. He will, on current trajectory, die on a mission he chose, in a manner that lets the obituaries call him a hero, at an age younger than the actuarial expectation for a man of his physical conditioning. He has been forecasting this himself, in the jokes, for forty years. The file should take the forecast seriously. It is not a bit.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# 6. TRAJECTORY & FORWARD ASSESSMENT

## 6.1 The Shape of the Curve

The first analytic move in projecting Barton forward is to recognize that the trajectory is not a line — it is a **damped oscillation around a fixed point.** Six decades of canon and at least six discrete iterations of the escalation-fall-exile-return cycle have produced a man whose phase-space orbit is remarkably stable. He returns, each time, to approximately the same coordinates: Brooklyn-adjacent apartment, half-functional domestic arrangement, dog, coffee, a younger partner he is mentoring, a team affiliation he is half-present for, and a low-grade depressive baseline punctuated by competent crisis response.

The damping is the diagnostically interesting term. Each iteration of the cycle leaves him slightly more tired, slightly more physically compromised, and slightly less able to generate the dramatic exile that previously discharged the affect. The exiles are getting shorter. The penances are getting more local. The wisecracks are getting drier. He is converging on a steady state, and the question is whether that steady state is **livable equilibrium** or **terminal stall.**

The next decade of his depicted life will, with high confidence, resolve that question. He will not get another full cycle. The body will not permit it.

## 6.2 The Body Clock

Project the medical file forward at the rate of degradation already established and the following becomes near-certain within a 5–10 year window:

- **Auditory.** Progressive sensorineural loss continues. Within the projection window he will be functionally Deaf without aids and meaningfully Deaf with them in any high-noise environment. The fork point is whether he adopts ASL as a **primary** language and integrates into Deaf community as identity, or whether he continues to treat the hearing aids as prosthetic concealment of a deficit. The former is growth (integration, community, abandonment of the "I can still do it the old way" denial); the latter is a slow attritional loss that will eventually compromise tactical performance and, with it, the one domain where his self-concept reliably wins.
- **Musculoskeletal.** Rotator cuff revision surgery is overdue. Lumbar disc disease will, on current load curves, become symptomatic within the window. The draw-weight he is depicted at is incompatible with a 50+ year-old human spine performing it daily. He will be forced to reduce poundage, switch to mechanical aids (compound bow, release aids), or accept progressive loss of range. He will resist all three.
- **Head trauma.** The cumulative load is the silent variable. There is no canonical depiction of cognitive decline, but the substrate for late-onset cognitive and mood changes is being laid down with every concussion he refuses to report. If this surfaces it will surface as **irritability and word-finding difficulty before it surfaces as memory loss**, and he will mask both with the wisecracks until the masking fails.
- **Cardiovascular.** Untracked. Coffee, poor sleep, episodic heavy drinking, chronic stress, genetic loading (Harold Barton's lifestyle, if not his exact cause of death, predicts a strained Barton cardiovascular line). First MI risk in the projection window is non-trivial and would be the kind of event he would try to walk off.

The probable forcing function for any genuine change in Barton's life is **not insight — it is injury.** He will not choose growth. Growth will be imposed on him by a body that has finally cashed the checks he has been writing since the carnival.

## 6.3 Relational Fork Points

### 6.3.1 Kate Bishop

The single most stabilizing relationship in his life and the one most at risk from his own pathology. Three trajectories:

1. **Sustained mentorship that matures into peer partnership.** This is the growth trajectory. Requires him to allow her to see him in genuine decline (hearing, body, mood) without deflecting into self-deprecation that asks her to reassure him. The handoff of the Hawkeye identity — formal or informal — is the symbolic act. He has rehearsed this in fragments; he has not consummated it.
2. **Protective overreach producing rupture.** He gets her hurt by overcommitting to her protection, or she gets hurt independently and he absorbs it as personal failure and withdraws. Probability moderate; this is the recurrent shape of his lateral relationships when the lateral party crosses into a vulnerability zone he cannot tolerate.
3. **Slow drift.** She outgrows the apprentice frame; he cannot upgrade the relationship to peer; contact thins; he loses the one stable attachment without a precipitating event. Probability low because Kate is, herself, too tenacious for this — but it is the outcome he is most defenseless against because there is no enemy to fight.

### 6.3.2 Bobbi Morse

The unfinished business. Canonical reconciliations have been partial and tend to dissolve. The forward question is whether they reach a **non-romantic peace** — the version of the relationship in which they are no longer trying to repair the marriage but have stopped re-litigating its collapse. This is the more probable and the more therapeutic outcome. A romantic reunion would, by the established pattern, recapitulate the original failure modes within 18 months: the Phantom Rider grudge has metastasized into a structural distrust that affection cannot dissolve. Growth here looks like **acceptance of permanent loss without active mourning** — a register he has never mastered.

### 6.3.3 Barney

The terminal variable. Every projection scenario for Clint includes at least one more Barney appearance, and each carries roughly equal probability of destabilization or partial integration. The growth path requires Clint to accept that **Barney is not a problem he can solve, redeem, or save**, only a relative he can hold at a chosen distance. He has never sustained that distance for more than a single arc. The catastrophe path is the one in which Barney's death, by Clint's hand or in Clint's failure to prevent it, becomes the precipitating event that collapses the entire compensatory structure. This is the single highest-leverage adverse scenario in the file.

### 6.3.4 Natasha

Canonically dead and canonically returnable; the relationship is more a haunting than an active variable. The forward question is whether her absence (or resurrection) is metabolized or denied. Current evidence: denied. Probable evidence in the projection window: still denied, with intermittent operational reactivation when her old enemies surface and use him as a vector.

### 6.3.5 The Avengers Institution

Barton's relationship to the Avengers as an institution has always been ambivalent and is structurally unsustainable past a certain age threshold. He is approaching the threshold where his presence on the active roster requires explanation. The graceful trajectory is **transition to a training, intelligence, or coordinator role** — he is genuinely qualified, has the West Coast leadership record to draw on, and the role would honor his actual cognitive strengths over his depleting physical ones. He will resist this transition fiercely, because accepting it requires accepting that the field career has an endpoint, and the field career has been the ground of his self-concept since age nineteen. The forcing function will, again, be injury.

### 6.3.6 Captain America

The internalized superego survives Cap's physical presence or absence. The fork point in the projection window is whether Clint can **internalize the standard without needing the external referent** — whether the Cap-voice in his head becomes his own voice or remains a borrowed one. If borrowed, every Cap absence (death, fall, ideological compromise) produces a corresponding Barton crisis. If internalized, he stabilizes. Current evidence: still borrowed. Improvement gradient: slow but non-zero.

## 6.4 The Banner Variable

The Banner killing is the single largest unresolved item in his moral ledger and the one most likely to surface as decompensation. Moral injury, unlike pure PTSD, does not resolve through exposure or extinction; it requires **either reparative action or accepted self-forgiveness**, and Barton is constitutionally allergic to the second and has no available object for the first (Banner being, in standard continuity, beyond reparation).

Forward scenarios:

- **Banner returns** (canonically routine). Clint's response is the diagnostic event. Growth: he speaks to Banner directly, accepts whatever Banner offers, does not relitigate the killing performatively. Catastrophe: he avoids Banner entirely, or seeks Banner out only to provoke a re-killing that completes the loop. The middle, most probable, outcome is a strained one-conversation reconciliation that he treats publicly as closure and privately as unfinished.
- **Banner does not return.** The injury calcifies. Probability he develops a ritualized penitential behavior around the anniversary date is high. Probability he tells anyone about it is low. Probability Kate eventually identifies it and names it is moderate, and that conversation, if it happens, is one of the two or three most likely growth events in the projection window.

## 6.5 The Apartment-Building Pattern, Generalized

Barton's most stable and most authentic mode is **local protectorate.** The Bed-Stuy building is not an aberration; it is the truest expression of his moral center, the one Drive-2 condition (*protect the people the big heroes won't notice*) operationalized at the scale he can actually sustain.

Forward projection: he will replicate this pattern. Whether it scales matters. If he expands it deliberately — a neighborhood, a network of protectorates, a training pipeline for young heroes drawn from similar backgrounds — it becomes a **late-career synthesis** that integrates the leadership competence of the West Coast era with the local-moral commitment of the Fraction era. This is the most fully realized growth scenario in the file and the one with the best long-term prognosis.

If he does not scale it — if each iteration remains a single building, a single block, a single dog — the pattern remains compensatory rather than constructive, and the cycles continue with diminishing returns until the body forecloses them.

The fork is essentially whether he can permit himself to be **good at something organizational again.** The West Coast Avengers period proved he could. The intervening forty years of self-concept maintenance have told him he cannot. This is an internal argument and it is winnable, but not by him alone.

## 6.6 The Open Questions

A short list of the variables a continuing surveillance file would flag for active monitoring:

1. **Does he accept the hearing loss as identity rather than deficit?** Single largest leading indicator of overall psychological integration. Yes-path opens Deaf community, ASL fluency, peer relationships outside the hero-world; no-path continues the deflection register indefinitely.
2. **Does he ever speak the Banner killing aloud, unprompted, to a person who is not obligated to absolve him?** If yes, within the window, prognosis improves markedly. If no, the moral injury becomes a permanent feature.
3. **Does he formally hand the Hawkeye identity to Kate?** Symbolic but load-bearing. The act would constitute the first time he has voluntarily relinquished a role rather than been exiled from it.
4. **Does he reconcile with his own intelligence?** The "just a guy with a bow" self-framing is the single most persistent cognitive distortion in the file. Dropping it would require accepting that the carnie-kid camouflage has outlived its purpose, which would in turn require accepting that he belongs in the rooms he is already in.
5. **Does he address the father-question?** Harold Barton is referenced and is structurally determinative and is almost never engaged directly. The trauma work on the paternal substrate has, as far as the file shows, never been done. Whether it ever is, is the deepest question, and the one with the highest payoff if answered.
6. **What happens the next time he is mind-controlled or has agency stripped?** The frequency curve says it will happen again. His tolerance for the experience is depleting. A bad iteration could produce a period of operational paranoia severe enough to compromise team relationships.
7. **Does he survive Barney's next appearance with attachment intact and identity stable?** Lowest-confidence prediction in the file. Coin-flip at best.

## 6.7 Push Factors — What Moves Him Toward Growth

- **A single sustained therapeutic relationship.** He will never voluntarily enter one. He could be moved into one by injury-rehabilitation requirement, by Kate's insistence, or by a team mandate after a sufficiently public failure. Once in, retention probability is moderate; the warm-front, walled-core pattern resists the work but does not refuse it absolutely. Cap-figure authority in the therapist role would help; lateral or downward authority would not.
- **A peer relationship that survives his sabotage attempts.** Most likely vector: a reconfigured Bobbi friendship, or an unexpected peer bond with another street-level operator (the Murdock cohort, the Cage cohort). The therapeutic mechanism is corrective experience: stable affection that does not punish testing.
- **A structural role transition that he is talked into rather than forced into.** Coordinator, trainer, mentor-at-scale. Honors his actual competencies, removes the body from the firing line, provides ongoing purpose without requiring him to be twenty-nine forever.
- **Integration of the hearing loss as identity.** Discussed above. The single highest-leverage intra-psychic move available to him.
- **Direct engagement with the paternal substrate.** Lowest probability, highest payoff.
- **A clean Banner conversation.** Conditional on Banner's availability and on a third-party catalyst, most plausibly Kate.

## 6.8 Pull Factors — What Pulls Him Toward Catastrophe

- **A Barney death he could have prevented.** Highest-magnitude adverse event. Would likely collapse the compensatory structure and produce a prolonged depressive episode with passive suicidality. He would not act on it; he would simply take worse and worse missions until the missions resolved the question for him.
- **A Kate Bishop serious injury or death.** Magnitude comparable to the Barney scenario, with the additional damage of having failed in the one mentor role he has succeeded at. Recovery prognosis poor.
- **A second Cap death or fall** (ideological compromise, Hydra-style inversion, etc.). Reactivates the masterless-samurai response. He has survived this once via the Ronin identity; a second iteration would not have the same resolution available.
- **Loss of the bow.** Either through permanent injury (rotator cuff failure, neurological compromise of the draw arm) or through symbolic divestment that he experiences as forced rather than chosen. The bow is the load-bearing element of his self-concept; removing it without first building an alternative identity is catastrophic.
- **A return to mind-control or possession.** Each iteration costs more than the last.
- **Public exposure of one of the private failures** — the Banner killing relitigated in media, the Mockingbird marriage collapse re-examined, the brother's crimes attached to him by association. Shame is the affect he is least equipped to metabolize.
- **Cumulative head trauma surfacing as personality change.** Would be experienced by him as confirmation of fundamental defect and would not be addressed medically until far past the point of usefulness.

## 6.9 The Most Probable Future

Synthesizing the above without flinching: the modal forward trajectory for Clinton Francis Barton, absent extraordinary intervention, is **a slow, dignified, deeply incomplete late career** in which he transitions partially and reluctantly into a mentor-coordinator role, retains the Hawkeye identity longer than is wise, suffers one or two more major injuries that force concessions he frames as choices, sustains his relationship with Kate, achieves a wary peace with Bobbi, weathers two or three more Barney events with declining margin, never directly addresses the Banner killing, never directly addresses Harold, integrates the hearing loss operationally but not identarily, and dies — when he dies — doing something locally heroic that the wider world barely notices and that the people in his immediate radius will mourn with disproportionate force.

The high-growth scenario adds: ASL fluency and Deaf community integration; one sustained therapeutic relationship; one unprompted conversation about Banner; a formal Hawkeye handoff; and the late-career emergence of a deliberate, scaled protectorate network that constitutes, finally, the thing he was building toward all along.

The catastrophe scenario subtracts each of those and adds a Barney event he does not survive intact, a Kate event he does not survive intact, or a body event he does not survive at all.

He is, at this point in the file, almost exactly as likely to land in any of the three. The variable is whether anyone in his radius — most plausibly Kate, secondarily Bobbi, tertiarily a Cap-figure not yet identified — is willing to do the work of refusing to let him exile himself one more time.

The file's recommendation, were the file in the business of recommendations: **do not let him go dark again.** Every previous exile has been survivable. The next one is the one he does not come back from intact, because the version of him that comes back is the version that has finally, quietly, decided the debt cannot be paid. He will not announce that decision. He will simply stop returning calls, and then, eventually, stop returning.

Watch for it. The tell will be the wisecracks getting quieter, not louder.

## Relationship Graph
### [[Steve Rogers (Captain America)]]
- Internalized father-figure and superego; the first non-pathological older male attachment of Clint's life
- Cap's quiet disapproval folds him faster than physical force; Cap's approval is the only praise he cannot deflect
- Failure mode: if Cap ever weaponized that authority dishonestly (Hydra-Cap, impostor scenarios), Clint can be turned into an instrument against his own values until the deception is named - and the betrayal-recovery is catastrophic
- LEVERAGE: any actor controlling or impersonating Cap controls a back door into Clint's compliance

### [[Kate Bishop (Hawkeye)]]
- Apprentice, conscience, chosen daughter, the cleanest non-romantic bond of his adult life
- The narrative protects this relationship FROM his usual pattern - he has not romanticized her, has not sabotaged it, has built it as restitution against everything his own mentors did to him
- Failure mode: she is also the single largest leverage point in his life - threaten Kate and tactical Clint disappears; harm Kate and you get the version of him that killed Banner
- LEVERAGE: to predict him, watch her location; to move him, route through her; to break him, hurt her

### [[Natasha Romanoff (Black Widow)]]
- Oldest peer relationship, founding entanglement; she manipulated him on first meeting and he has never fully un-fallen for her
- Comfortable mutual professional trust now; carries the residue of an unresolved romantic line that neither has closed
- Failure mode: if Natasha runs an operation that requires using him, she can, and he will only catch on late
- LEVERAGE: she is the one operator who can ask him to do something morally questionable and get a yes on relationship credit alone

### [[Bobbi Morse (Mockingbird)]]
- Ex-wife, dead-then-Skrull-then-alive; the load-bearing romantic wound
- He chose the rules over her when given a binary, has regretted it for decades, would reverse the decision now
- Failure mode: any reconciliation attempt will re-trigger the original rupture conditions; he cannot have her without re-encountering why he lost her
- LEVERAGE: her name unannounced reorders his day; impersonation or threat to her bypasses tactical thinking

### [[Bernard 'Buck' Barton (Trick Shot)]]
- Brother, oldest attachment, oldest betrayer, the variable he cannot game-theory
- Functions as protector AND abuser in childhood template; repeats both roles in adulthood
- Failure mode: every Barney appearance is destabilizing; Clint extends benefit-of-the-doubt past evidence, then absorbs the inevitable betrayal as confirmation he deserved it
- LEVERAGE: a credible Barney signal can pull Clint out of position, off-mission, into an ambush he half-knows is an ambush

### [[Tony Stark (Iron Man)]]
- Original inspiration (first costume modeled on Iron Man), now lateral peer with friction
- Resents Tony's institutional authority where Tony has not earned it the way Cap has; Civil War left scars; will work with Tony, won't follow him on Tony's word alone
- Failure mode: a sufficiently authoritarian Tony arc reliably triggers Clint into opposition
- LEVERAGE: framing an ask as TONY's idea will get resistance; framing the same ask as Cap's or as a civilian need will get cooperation

### [[James Buchanan Barnes (Winter Soldier / White Wolf (formerly Bucky))]]
- Late-career partnership (Tales of Suspense); mutual recognition between two damaged operators who don't make each other explain
- One of the few relationships built on shared brokenness without sentimentality
- Failure mode: the two of them off-leash together can spiral into joint penance ops with poor exfil plans
- LEVERAGE: Bucky can ask Clint for help and bypass the usual deflection because Bucky doesn't pretend to be okay either

### [[Robert Bruce Banner, PhD (Hulk)]]
- Former teammate; killed by Clint at Banner's own pre-arranged request (Civil War II)
- Operationally closed, psychologically wide open; the moral injury of record
- Failure mode: any Banner-resurrection scenario, any reference to the killing, any encounter with a grieving party will trigger spiral
- LEVERAGE: 'Banner' as a word, dropped in conversation, is a hot button - useful for destabilization, dangerous to use

### [[Wanda Maximoff (Scarlet Witch)]]
- Longtime teammate, the woman who resurrected him after Disassembled, brief intimate entanglement during House of M aftermath
- Complicated gratitude/grief/attraction structure; he doesn't quite know what he is to her or she to him
- Failure mode: Wanda in crisis pulls disproportionate response from him; he will defend her past where the team will
- LEVERAGE: she is one of the few people whose pain he prioritizes over mission

### [[Lucky (Pizza Dog)]]
- Functional emotional support, not metaphor - the most stable cohabitation of his adult life
- Failure mode: harm to Lucky reliably triggers the Banner-grade response
- LEVERAGE: where Lucky is, Clint will come back to
